# Skyrim:Glacial Crevice

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Glacial Crevice | | |

| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Frost Troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1GlacialCrevice01 | |
| Region | |

| [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") | |

Glacial Crevice

The **Glacial Crevice** is a small cave in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"), which must be traversed to reach the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)"). It contains only one zone, *[Glacial Crevice](#Glacial_Crevice)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**: Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").

### Exterior

The exterior to this cave is the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). There are two entrances. The first entrance is at the river's headwater south of [Sharpslope Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sharpslope_Cave "Skyrim:Sharpslope Cave"), and is guarded by two leveled [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). The second entrance/exit is in the isolated southwest area of the vale, and can only be initially accessed by proceeding through the cave from the first entrance. Finally, after retrieving the [diamond paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond_Paragon "Skyrim:Diamond Paragon") from the [frost giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Giant "Skyrim:Frost Giant") in the southwest area of the vale, it may be used in the [paragon platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") to reach an otherwise inaccessible ledge in the cave.

### Glacial Crevice

Chamber

The entrance at the river's headwater leads into a partly flooded ice tunnel which proceeds south to a huge dimly lit open-roofed chamber. The chamber is deeply flooded, with various ledges and terraces rising above you, including an icy ramp against the east wall rising up to further ledges and terraces. A large iceberg that can be climbed and explored floats in the middle of the chamber, but holds nothing of interest. Under the water are two passages; one is a narrow passage in the middle of the west wall, and the other is a far wider passage to the south. A current runs from south to north, so anything falling into the water will slowly float back toward the entrance. To completely explore this cave system, there are two distinct circuits you will need to follow. If you don't wish to fully explore the cave system, skip to [here](#Once).

Completing the upper circuit first allows you to later loot any of the enemies that may fall from the ledges or walkways. It's recommended that you first deal with the Falmer in this chamber by climbing the icy ramp against the east wall. A [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") is either wandering the ramp, in a battle with up to two Falmer patrolling this section of the chamber, or already lying dead. Too much noise will alert two more Falmer at the top, one of which is a magic-user, which are patrolling between two Falmer tents. As the path continues to ascend, it crosses a damaged Falmer bridge before reaching a ledge high above the water with the two empty tents. A Falmer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") is to the left of the tent to the north. Above you are more ledges and a bridge that cannot be reached from here. Next to the south tent is a passage heading southwest. However, it's recommended that you leave that for now, and instead return to the bottom of the icy path or simply jump down into the water.

For this next section, unless you are an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian"), you will require [potions of waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Potion of Waterbreathing") or preferably a corresponding [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(effect) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (effect)") item or [spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(spell) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (spell)"). If you returned to the bottom of the chamber by jumping into the water, you will probably be near where a small waterfall cascades into the water. A wide partially submerged passage is west of the waterfall; ignore this passage at this time. (It leads to an area with a Falmer tent, a Falmer hive, and a rowboat, as described [below](#large_overturned_bug).) The submerged passage that you should now find can be reached by swimming north, toward the iceberg in the middle of the chamber. When you reach the iceberg, swim to its west side and look at the west wall below the waterline, where you should find a fully submerged tunnel entrance. This submerged passage leads to an almost completely flooded chamber with five dead Falmer floating in the water. The water is partly frozen over; however, there are gaps in the surface ice, with a Falmer chest next to another dead Falmer on the ice. Another submerged passage continues to the west to another deeply flooded chamber, with Falmer-built walkways and bridges crisscrossing above you between ledges. The first walkway rises on your left. There is also a wide passage descending in the western corner of the chamber near the base of the walkway, but this forms part of the lower circuit, so ignore it for now.

Climbing the first two walkways leads to a ledge with a leveled Falmer guarding an empty tent. The next ledge has a short passage heading south, which ends with a Falmer magic-user guarding a tent and two Falmer chests, with one chest in the tent and the other to its left. The next walkway leads to a narrow ledge that continues to rise, spiraling upward, with a Falmer patrolling the path. At the top are two passages. The first passage heads east past a closed gate, and leads to the exit in the isolated southwest area of the Forgotten Vale; this is the route to take if you've already fully explored or aren't interested in fully exploring the cave system. The second passage at the top heads west, with a lookout point to the right of the entrance overlooking the ledges below. After a short distance you'll come upon a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap facing away from you, with the [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers it just ahead. The passage turns south to reach a closed gate onto a ledge high above a narrow crevice. Two leveled Falmer patrol the ledge, where a walkway descends to another ledge holding a tent containing a Falmer chest. The first ledge continues south along the left wall, before the sides of the crevice narrow and the paths on both sides join together briefly before widening and splitting again. The path on the left rises, while the path on the right descends. A leveled Falmer and a [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") patrol the right ledge, while farther along the left ledge is another Falmer. Either party can be alerted by fighting with the other. The path on the left leads to a bridge crossing to another platform, with an unlocked Falmer chest at the far end and an inaccessible ledge directly above. Backtracking and following the path on the right as it descends leads down to an icy tunnel with a tripwire across it triggering twin claw traps from the sides. Past the traps is a gate, beyond which the passage turns left before leading out to the ledge with the two tents at the top of the huge open-roofed chamber where you previously stopped and dropped to the water below.

From here, return through the submerged passage west of the iceberg to the tall chamber with the walkways above. This time, head west down the wide passage near the base of the first walkway as it narrows and turns south. You emerge in the partly flooded crevice. Any Falmer or chaurus corpses that fell from the ledges and walkways above will have floated toward the beginning of the crevice due to the current, and can be looted here. Proceeding southeast, you will eventually reach a small area on the shore, where a Falmer magic-user stands by a Falmer tent containing a Falmer chest. An empty [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") is to the right, and a rowboat is moored in the water. The boat seems to have been built from a large overturned bug. The passage widens and turns north at this point to lead back into the south end of the huge first chamber west of the small waterfall, completing the lower circuit.

Once you've completed both circuits, or if you don't wish to fully explore the cave system, take the submerged passage west of the iceberg in the main chamber, and continue to the tall chamber with crisscrossing walkways and bridges. Climb these to the top, and take the gated passage heading east. The passage rises and turns north before opening into a chamber with three Falmer tents. The middle tent is larger and more ornate, and contains a Falmer chest. An icy ramp to the left ascends in a clockwise spiral around the walls of the chamber. At the top, another passage heads southeast before emerging far above the main chamber on a ledge leading south. A Falmer on the first section of the ledge patrols backwards and forwards to an empty tent, beyond which is a Falmer hive on the right wall concealing a leveled Falmer. A second tent beyond the hive contains a Falmer chest. Ahead are two more empty Falmer hives and a bridge spanning the chamber to the east, with a Falmer at either end. Across the bridge is a ledge heading north toward two broken stone pillars. The pillars flank yet another passage heading east leading to the exit in the isolated southwest area of the Forgotten Vale, which is filled with Falmer settlements.

Once you've retrieved the diamond paragon, you can use it in the paragon platform to teleport to an otherwise inaccessible ledge with an unlocked stone chest holding quality loot to the south. The broken stone arch forming the portal allows you to return directly to the paragon platform. The ledge is far above the crevice, near where the walls narrow and the ledges join. From this ledge, you can drop down to further ledges below, or using at least two words of the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), cross to another wide ledge opposite. However, none of the other ledges hold anything of interest.

## Notes

- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

- There are some glitched areas under the water, particularly in the arch-shaped passages that connect to the first area. Coming into contact with them may cause you to drop to the bottom, then surface and gasp for air.

## Maps

Glacial Crevice

Glenmoril Coven

**Glenmoril Coven** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") or [Glenmoril Witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch"). It contains only one zone, *[Glenmoril Cave](#Glenmoril_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor")**: Claim the head of a [Glenmoril Witch](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch") for [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").
- **[Purity](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity "Skyrim:Purity")**: Help a member of the Circle give up their beasthood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

As you approach the cave, it becomes clear all is not well. The local plant life is dead, and there are mutilated shrines along the path to the cave. The path starts immediately to the north of an [unmarked ruined tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Unmarked_Ruins_and_Monuments "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") and has a number of switchbacks as it climbs toward the cave entrance. You are likely to encounter a random [creature](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") or two along this path. As you near the top, there are numerous [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") symbols formed from the bones and antlers of large elk, spriggan and goat heads on stakes, and taproots hanging from trees. A patch of [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") grows on a tree stump near the entrance, with several troll and animal skulls on either side. The entrance is marked by lit braziers on stands.

### Glenmoril Cave

Glenmoril Cave

Upon entering, a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") is in an alcove straight ahead where the tunnel first turns to the right. There are three enemies in the large chamber nearby. A [hag](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag") patrols near a campfire in the middle, and there is a leveled creature (such as a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), or [troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll")) hiding in the darkness to the right. There is an additional weak creature by the western tunnel on the upper level. There is a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide") next to the central pillar and another just to the northwest. Due south of the fire is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a basket holding a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and two [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flowers, a pair of [ragged robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Robes "Skyrim:Ragged Robes") next to a patch of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus, and two skulls to go with the two nearby rib cages. There are ramps leading upwards on either side and four tunnels leading out from the center room: two on the lower level and two on the higher level.

#### Lower North Tunnel

The northern tunnel on the lower level leads to a small room, where a hag is standing on a stake-studded ledge on the left. An earthen ramp leads up to it starting behind a rock pillar in front. There is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel with a lit goat horn lantern on top, and to the right is an open crate containing two [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") and a [briar heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Briar_Heart "Skyrim:Briar Heart"), with a birds' nest beside it holding another rock warbler egg. Farther to the right is an unlocked wooden chest.

#### Lower West Tunnel

The twisting tunnel to the west on the lower level leads to a small room with a waterfall. There is a single hag by the waterfall on the lower far side of the chamber and nothing else.

#### Upper North Tunnel

The tunnel to the north on the upper level leads to a medium-sized room. After following the tunnel, turn left to go around the stake studded edge. There is a creature at this point and a hag farther on near a table with a built-in [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). On the table is a dead [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat"), a goat's head, a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), and a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*.

#### Upper West Tunnel

The upper western chamber

Before the western tunnel on the upper level, there is a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") on the left and another on the right inside the tunnel. There is also an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") in the tunnel, on the left-hand wall after turning the corner by the brazier. The passage opens into a chamber dominated by a shallow pool with a path around it to the right. There is a leveled creature around the corner and a hag on the far left side standing in front of a hagraven-style tent. There is another Namira's rot and a bleeding crown on the right. Across from these sits another pillar, behind which is an open crate containing two [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") and three [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales").

Beside the tent is a bloodied altar of Hircine with a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), one of three random potions (a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina")), and a nightshade flower. On the other side of the tent is a boss-level unlocked chest. Inside the tent there are two barrels of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") and an open crate containing a copy of the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") skill book *[Horror of Castle Xyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Horror_of_Castle_Xyr "Skyrim:Horror of Castle Xyr")*, two more slaughterfish eggs, and three more slaughterfish scales. By another pillar at the southern end of the pool are three [white caps](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") and a bleeding crown.

## Notes

- During the quest [Blood's Honor](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood%27s_Honor "Skyrim:Blood's Honor"), the hags will be replaced by the Glenmoril Witches. The witches are unique hagravens; for details on their background, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Glenmoril_Wyrd "Lore:Glenmoril Wyrd"). However, the cave itself, including its layout and all loot, does not respawn.
- The bloodied altar in the upper west chamber is a shrine to [Hircine](/wiki/Lore:Hircine "Lore:Hircine").

## Bugs

- The dead goat can become stuck in the table.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, addresses this issue. It needed the "do not havok settle" box checked.
- If the location is not cleared prior to Blood’s Honor, it can’t be marked as “Cleared” on the map later. This is because the boss tag is attached to one of the native hags, replaced by unique Glenmoril Witches by the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=18729))
  - Clear the location then start Blood's Honor.

## Overview

Gloombound Mine

**Gloombound Mine** is a small [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") supporting the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur"). It contains only one zone, *[Gloombound Mine](#Gloombound_Mine)*.

It is owned and worked by [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") from Narzulbur, with the help of hired workers from the Orc stronghold of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur"). [Dushnamub](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnamub "Skyrim:Dushnamub") will [buy ebony ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bor "Skyrim:Bor")  [Gadba gro-Largash](/wiki/Skyrim:Gadba_gro-Largash "Skyrim:Gadba gro-Largash")\*  [Mogdurz](/wiki/Skyrim:Mogdurz "Skyrim:Mogdurz")  [Mul gro-Largash](/wiki/Skyrim:Mul_gro-Largash "Skyrim:Mul gro-Largash")\* |

\* These Orcs have been hired from Largashbur due to a deficit of workers in Narzulbur.

## Related Quests

- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

The exterior of the mine is the Orc stronghold of Narzulbur. A [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") is in the covered work area beneath the mine.

### Gloombound Mine

Top of the tunnel

The mine is the richest source of ebony in Skyrim. On a single trip to the mine, it is possible to obtain 63 pieces of [ebony ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ore "Skyrim:Ebony Ore"), which can be smelted into 31 ingots (or 50 and 25 respectively if you are not willing to steal). Care must be taken as there are several pockets of [flammable gas](/wiki/Skyrim:Flammable_Gas "Skyrim:Flammable Gas") within the mine, so any naked flame can cause an explosive fire. There are numerous [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") found throughout the mine.

Upon entering the mine, there is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush on your left and a ramp leading down to a crossroads; a [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") can be found on a table to the left. Turn left (north) past the table to reach two ebony ore veins (one on the right wall, and the other on the ground) as well as an iron ore vein on the ground. At the end of the tunnel, on the end wall, is another ebony ore vein.

Turning right (south) at the crossroads will land you at a dead end with an ebony ore vein. Straight ahead (east) at the crossroads; you will pass a shelf on your left with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), as well as an iron ore vein on the ground in front of it. Follow the tunnel up the ramp and you will find an iron ore vein on the ground on the left. At the top of the ramp, if you turn left, you will encounter a dead end with two ebony ore veins, one on the left wall, the other on the right.

Far end of the mine

Turning around past the top of the ramp, an ebony ore vein is on the ground on the right. Continue straight ahead past an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") to reach a tunnel on your right, where there is an iron ore vein on the ground. Just after this vein, on the left, is a barrel with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet") on top of it. Two ebony ore veins are at the end of the tunnel, both on the ground.

Back to the turn, now on your left (west) are two upright barrels, one of which has a piece of ebony ore lying on top. The turn takes you through a braced section of tunnel with a dogleg. Partway through are two iron ore veins, both on your right. Farther along the tunnel as it turns to the right is an ebony ore vein. Next to this vein is a cart which contains three pieces of ebony ore. Just past this is another vein on the right hand wall. Be careful between this ore vein and the end of the tunnel as there is a [loose segment of planks](/wiki/Skyrim:Rotten_Planks "Skyrim:Rotten Planks") in the middle of the ground, which will crumble and drop you down to the crossroads by the entrance if you step on it. Between the planking and the end of the tunnel is a bucket containing two pieces of ebony ore. At the end of the tunnel, five ebony ore veins can be found: two on the ground, and one on each of the three walls at the end of the tunnel.

## Notes

- This is the only marked mine on the map that is part of an Orc stronghold.
- One of the Orc workers may trigger the rotten planks and fall to their death.
- One of the pieces of ebony ore outside may not be marked as owned by the stronghold.

# Skyrim:Gloomreach

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Gloomreach ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gloomreach)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Gloomreach "Lore:Gloomreach")) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Withershins](/wiki/Skyrim:Withershins "Skyrim:Withershins")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| GloomreachExterior  Gloomreach01  Gloomreach02 | |
| Region | |
| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| Southeast of [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Smelters](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 3 |

Entrance to Gloomreach

**Gloomreach** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") in the Reach containing [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") and [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer").

There are many samples of [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") and [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") that can be collected from within this cave system. The easiest way of finding the cave is to travel to the [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn"), then travel southeast from there. The cave is found on the far side of the river from the inn.

It contains two zones: *[Gloomreach](#Gloomreach)* and *[Gloomreach Hive](#Gloomreach_Hive)*.

### Exterior

There are many [mudcrabs](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") and [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish") along the banks and in this part of the river. Several [juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper "Skyrim:Juniper") trees line the route, and a couple [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plants as well as three [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") grow around the entrance.

### Gloomreach

The first room in Gloomreach

Upon entering, you find yourself in a natural cave with an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus growing in front of you against the cave wall to your right. The tunnel turns to the southeast, and you can see a tree bathed in a pool of natural light from above. As you move forward, you will see a juniper tree off to the left in another pool of light; on the wall beside this is a [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella") growing on the cave wall. As the cave opens up, there is a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus to the left. Following the cave around to the left, you come to two patches of [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") together, near the juniper tree. Farther around there is a tunnel heading to the northeast, with a lit brazier to the right of the entrance. There are two rock pillars in the cave, and above you on the southwest wall is a ledge.

Following the tunnel to the northeast, after a short distance the tunnel turns to the southeast and then opens into another cave with a juniper tree. On your left is a partially buried cart with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") inside and another beside it. To the right of the tree, the cave is staggered and continues to the southeast. Tread carefully, as there is a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") patrolling this area. Along the right-hand wall is a bleeding crown, a fly amanita, and a pickaxe on a barrel. Continuing forward, you pass under a wooden scaffolding tower with another pickaxe next to a bedroll underneath and a bleeding crown on the left. To the right of this is a barrel with a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Withershins](/wiki/Skyrim:Withershins "Skyrim:Withershins")* on top. Past this you come to a junction with a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") on the ground in front of you, as well as a path continuing toward the southeast and another path on your right to the south-southwest.

Taking this second tunnel leads to a small cave with two [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), several chaurus eggs, and a bleeding crown. Fighting the chaurus may well alert several Falmer who come to investigate. The exit to this cave is to the southeast, and comes out above a second path below. There is a blisterwort fungus in front of you. Turning right takes you past a bleeding crown and a blisterwort along a ledge over and along the left of the below path. The ledge continues to the northwest, and the path below opens into an open area with several cages, a Falmer tent, and stairs up at the far end. Caution is needed as you pass a couple crates and barrels, as there is a Falmer lurking here. The path then splits again. To the left, the ledge follows the cave around and descends to the lower area. On your right, it joins with a wooden scaffolding structure that goes around a rock pillar before exiting the cave heading northwest.

Back at the original junction and continuing straight ahead past the first corundum ore vein, the tunnel bears to the southwest before you come to a dead [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat "Skyrim:Goat") with a broken cart to the left. Just past these is a braced section of tunnel, with the other path overhead. On the ground behind this is a corundum ore vein. Entering the open area at ground level, you pass between two cages, both adept-locked, with the one on the right holding a [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). Next is a table to the left holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a [leather helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"), past which is a cart on the left and a damaged cage on the right containing a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). You will also find a third corundum ore vein ahead. Against the north wall near the cage with the skeever is an imp stool and a bleeding crown. Farther to the left is the Falmer tent, which contains an unlocked chest. Continuing to the southwest, you pass several of the supports for the wooden scaffolding. By the bottom of the earthen ramp back up to the higher ledge is a bookcase holding two pickaxes and a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"). Opposite this in the western corner is a set of shelves containing a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") under a scaffold tower.

On the ledge, after taking the path that crosses the room around the rock pillar, you will exit into a tunnel heading northwest. You will find an unlocked chest on your left; opposite this is a straw bale and a stack of crates and sacks. Among these is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a pickaxe, and a knapsack. Past these items is a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") and a bleeding crown, followed by the entrance to Gloomreach Hive.

### Gloomreach Hive

Upon entering, you will be in a tunnel that twists and turns until you come to an arch with glowing mushrooms above. There is a patrolling Falmer around this area who may have already set off a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that activates a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap hinged on the left. Just past the tripwire is a path that leads to the right and winds its way around and down in the next room. To your left is a ledge to the south. There is another Falmer and a chaurus here; while fighting these, a third Falmer is likely to come up from below to investigate. The south tunnel leads into a small cave only containing chaurus eggs. Descending the path around the room, you pass an imp stool, three bleeding crowns, and a second imp stool. At the bottom is a path heading to the southeast. Before going in that direction, there is a third imp stool against the north wall, and in the water is an unlocked chest and a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") floating on the surface. On the ramp starting underwater to the northwest that leads back out of the pool are two blisterwort and a bleeding crown under the water. There are also two Namira's rot, one on either side of the tunnel heading southeast.

Follow the tunnel as it twists and turns and rises until you reach a closed gate. Two Falmer are in this area. One is patrolling near you and the other is off to the left near the back of the cave; a third will investigate any fighting from a ramp leading up from below to the south. In the eastern corner is a Falmer tent, and along the back is a fence with an unlocked chest next to it. Descend the ramp to the south, which leads to another Falmer tent with an unlocked chest to the left of it. If you have come to Gloomreach to retrieve an item, this is where you will find it. The path makes a couple switchbacks to reach the floor of this room. There is a final Falmer in a Falmer tent up a rise to the northwest. On the cave floor, you can find many fungi: four blisterwort, an imp stool, two Namira's rot, and three bleeding crown. There is a closed gate to the south that leads to a shortcut tunnel that returns to Gloomreach, ending on the ledge previously seen near the exit from these caves.

## Notes

- It is possible to bypass almost all of the first zone, including all of the enemies in the zone, by climbing the wall in the southwest part of the first cavern, effectively entering Gloomreach Hive through the exit.
- Gloomreach also [appears](/wiki/Online:Gloomreach "Online:Gloomreach") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

# Skyrim:Glory of the Dead

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Companions.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Companions.png) | **Cure [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s spirit and become Harbinger of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb") |
| Reward: | [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"), [Shield of Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield_of_Ysgramor "Skyrim:Shield of Ysgramor"), Word for the [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") shout, [Harbinger](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions#Leadership "Skyrim:Companions") of the Companions, New crafting options at the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge"), 7 new [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =3 ([Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress"), [Athis](/wiki/Skyrim:Athis "Skyrim:Athis"), [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas"), [Njada Stonearm](/wiki/Skyrim:Njada_Stonearm "Skyrim:Njada Stonearm"), [Ria](/wiki/Skyrim:Ria "Skyrim:Ria"), [Torvar](/wiki/Skyrim:Torvar "Skyrim:Torvar"), and [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas")) |
| ID: | C06 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge") | | |

The Companions and the citizens of Whiterun bid their goodbyes to Kodlak

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Have [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane") mend [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad").
2. Return Wuuthrad to [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb").
3. Make your way through the tomb.
4. Meet [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane").
5. Fight one final [spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak%27s_Wolf_Spirit "Skyrim:Kodlak's Wolf Spirit").
6. Release Kodlak.

### The Funeral

After the events of [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge"), [Vilkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Vilkas "Skyrim:Vilkas") will run towards the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") to participate in the late Harbinger [Kodlak Whitemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")'s funeral. The ceremony is to be held near [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane")'s smithy. All of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") will be present, along with the Jarl, steward and the local [priestess of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Danica_Pure-Spring "Skyrim:Danica Pure-Spring"). Kodlak is placed above the forge, and the ceremony ends with [Aela the Huntress](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela_the_Huntress "Skyrim:Aela the Huntress") lighting the fire, symbolizing a final goodbye:

:   **Eorlund:** *"Who will start?"*
:   **Aela:** *"I'll do it. Before the ancient flame..."*
:   **Everyone:** *"We grieve."*
:   **Eorlund:** *"At this loss..."*
:   **Everyone:** *"We weep."*
:   **Vilkas:** *"For the fallen..."*
:   **Everyone:** *"We shout."*
:   **Farkas:** *"And for ourselves..."*
:   **Everyone:** *"We take our leave."*

After the ritual, Eorlund will seek you out, asking for the fragments of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad") and Kodlak's secret fragment from his chambers. Retrieve the fragment from the end table in his room. [Kodlak's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Kodlak's Journal"), also in the end table, offers some insights on him and his visions. Return to Eorlund with the fragment. When he accepts it, he will inform you that your Shield-Siblings have gone to [the Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge") for a gathering and suggests you join them:

:   *"Thank you. Your Shield-Siblings have withdrawn to the Underforge. I think they're waiting for you."*

### Wuuthrad Finally Returned!

*"Just because something is, doesn't mean it must be."*

In the Underforge you will find the three members of the [Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Circle "Skyrim:The Circle"), [Farkas](/wiki/Skyrim:Farkas "Skyrim:Farkas"), Vilkas and Aela, talking around the blood fountain, all of them frustrated and discouraged. They all know that Kodlak died without being granted his only wish, namely to be freed of his lycanthropy so he could spend his afterlife in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Lore:Sovngarde "Lore:Sovngarde"). While they know of a way to cleanse his soul, it requires them to enter the [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb") and perform a ceremony:

**Vilkas**: *"The old man had one wish before he died. And he didn't get it. It's as simple as that."*
**Aela**: *"Being moon-born is not so much of a curse as you might think, Vilkas."*
**Vilkas**: *"That's fine for you. But he wanted to be clean. He wanted to meet Ysgramor and know the glories of Sovngarde. But all that was taken from him."*
**Aela**: *"And you avenged him."*
**Farkas**: *"Kodlak did not care for vengeance."*
**Vilkas**: *"No, Farkas, he didn't. And that's not what this is about. We should be honoring Kodlak, no matter our own thoughts on the blood."*
**Aela**: *"You're right. It's what he wanted, and he deserved to have it."*
**Vilkas**: *"Kodlak used to speak of a way to cleanse his soul, even in death. You know the legends of the Tomb of Ysgramor."*
**Aela**: *"There the souls of the Harbingers will heed the call of northern steel. We can't even enter the tomb without Wuuthrad, and it's in pieces, like it has been for a thousand years."*

At this point, Eorlund Gray-Mane enters with the repaired [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad") on his back:

**Eorlund**: *"And dragons were just stories. And the elves once ruled Skyrim. Just because something is, doesn't mean it must be. The blade is a weapon. A tool. Tools are meant to be broken. And repaired."*
**Vilkas**: *"Is that? Did you repair the blade?"*
**Eorlund**: *"This is the first time I've had all the pieces, thanks to our Shield-Brother/Shield-Sister here. "The flames of a hero can reforge the shattered." The flames of Kodlak shall fuel the rebirth of Wuuthrad. And now it will take you to meet him once more."*

He will then address you personally:

:   *"As the one who bore the fragments, I think you should be the one to carry Wuuthrad into battle."*

He will then hand you the weapon and speak to the other members:

:   *"The rest of you, prepare to journey to the Tomb of Ysgramor. For Kodlak."*

Your allies will then take off towards the legendary [Ysgramor's Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Tomb "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Tomb").

### Ghosts of the Companions

The Ysgramor statue

A final request from [Kodlak](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak_Whitemane "Skyrim:Kodlak Whitemane")

[Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)") awaits.

As soon as you enter the tomb, Vilkas will approach and warn you about the dangers that lie ahead. He also says he will take no part in the task, as he has too much grief in his heart. Activate the Ysgramor statue, which will take Wuuthrad from your inventory, and place it on the statue to lower the wall. You may reclaim Wuuthrad by activating the statue again, and the wall will remain open. Followed by Aela the Huntress and Farkas, two skeevers greet you as you head north into the tomb. Continue down, and follow the path around until you are heading west into the next chamber with several [Companion ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Companion_Ghost "Skyrim:Companion Ghost") who taunt and warn of your impending death. They attack with Ancient Nord Bows, Swords, and Battle Axes, but their loot will disappear quickly if not searched immediately. Now head south until you enter a large room, with more tombs encircling a pond. Here one or two more ghostly apparitions test your courage before moving deeper into the tomb. Going west up the small stairs past the tombs, you encounter a spider web to the south that must be broken through to continue. It is here that Farkas reveals that, *"Ever since [Dustman's Cairn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dustman%27s_Cairn "Skyrim:Dustman's Cairn"), the big crawly ones are my weakness"*. Consequently, he will proceed no further and instead runs back to join Vilkas at the statue. With Aela the Huntress as your only ally now, hack your way through the spider webs and face a Giant Frostbite spider, and many poison-spitting [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). Follow the stairs down past the white caps into the next area. Two more companion ghosts await you, and after finishing them off, search the [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") laid out on the tables for valuables, and a potion of stamina beside the wrapped body. Be sure to search the draugr skeletons in their tombs for leveled weapons and armor. Heading east up the small stairs, open the next iron door and you'll enter an area with draugr tombs to your right, but a closed gate to your left. Activating the pedestal will open the closed gate. Enter this chamber heading north, where four more ghosts await shooting arrows, and wielding both one and two-handed weapons. Dispose of them, and find the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") skill book *[The Legendary Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legendary_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:The Legendary Sancre Tor")* in the center of the room next to the burial urns. Up the stone stairs and through this final iron door.

### The Trip to Sovngarde

You will find the ghost of Kodlak Whitemane warming his hands near the Flame of the Harbinger. After explaining that the room is, in fact, swarming with the ghosts of his predecessors, whom you can't see, he will ask you if you still own the  [Glenmoril Witch heads](/wiki/Skyrim:Glenmoril_Witch_Head "Skyrim:Glenmoril Witch Head"). He will then ask you to toss one into the Flame, in an attempt to cure him of his werewolf curse. After doing so, Kodlak's [wolf spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Kodlak%27s_Wolf_Spirit "Skyrim:Kodlak's Wolf Spirit") will be released and immediately attack. After the battle, Kodlak will thank you and name you the new leader of the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"). He will then travel to Sovngarde and finally find his peace, completing the quest.

### Harbinger of the Companions

You can now speak to Aela, who will recognize your new position and tell you she is going to stay in the tomb for a while longer, for further studies. If you linger there, Vilkas and Farkas will arrive and also say they want to stay. All three will then become available as [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers").

You can cure yourself of [lycanthropy](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") before you leave the tomb if you wish. If you don't, you will be required to [cure two other Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity "Skyrim:Purity") of their lycanthropy before you will again have the option to do so. Consider that choosing to remain a werewolf is the only way to access the quest [Totems of Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Totems_of_Hircine "Skyrim:Totems of Hircine"), which grants unique abilities you may use while in beast form. You may come back to cure your lycanthropy later. To cure yourself now, throw another Glenmoril Witch head into the fire. Your wolf spirit will emerge. Kill it to rid yourself of being a werewolf permanently. If Aela, Vilkas or Farkas are around, they will aid in the fight.

After you've finished, continue up the spiral wooden stairs and locate the chest on the northeastern ledge to claim the [Shield of Ysgramor](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield_of_Ysgramor "Skyrim:Shield of Ysgramor"), along with some other valuable loot, then exit through the nearby door by activating a chain. Go up the stairs, and through another short hallway before arriving at another wall with a chain. Pulling the chain opens the wall to the first chamber in the tomb as well as the wall on the opposite side. Before leaving the tomb, you can take Wuuthrad from Ysgramor's statue if you didn't earlier. Exit the tomb through the Western (W) passageway, which was previously inaccessible. Follow the set of stairs outside up the mountain to discover a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") which teaches part of the [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Directly north (to the right) of the word wall is a gold ore vein.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked when you complete this quest and finish the questline:

-  **Glory of the Dead** (30 points/Silver)

## Notes

- Once the funeral ceremony has begun, you won't be able to use the Skyforge until the quest is finished.
- Once the quest is finished, everything in the Harbinger's room at Jorrvaskr becomes free to take.
- Aela and Farkas, as quest-specific followers, behave differently than "permanent" followers:

:   - Neither of them will enter sneak mode when you do, and when either can see you, the sneak eye remains open.
    - If you get too close to them while sneaking, they will yell *"Stay away from me!"* as if you were going to pickpocket them.
    - Accidentally attacking either of them might turn them hostile.

- Aela, Farkas, (and Vilkas after he speaks to you at the entry) will only repeat *"For Kodlak!"* during the quest, and won't have any dialogue options, including skill training.
- You can bring any other follower with you and they will help clear the tomb. However, at the final fight they may ignore Kodlak's wolf spirit as if it were invisible to them. If you choose to cure yourself, they will fight your released spirit normally.
- The ghosts' remains cannot be looted and will disappear immediately.
- It's possible to pickpocket the ghosts' armor and weapons with the [Perfect Touch](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") perk before they engage in combat or after casting [Pacify](/wiki/Skyrim:Pacify_(spell) "Skyrim:Pacify (spell)") on them.

:   - All ghosts wear a full set of [Ancient Nord Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge#Forging "Skyrim:Skyforge") and wield one of the various [Ancient Nord weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Specialty_Gear#Draugr_Equipment "Skyrim:Specialty Gear").

- Although Farkas, Vilkas, and Aela are presumably supposed to lose their essential statuses after this quest, they remain essential even then.

## Bugs

- The quest may not start if you are in combat with Eorlund Gray-Mane
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
  -  To start the quest, first select Eorlund and enter `kill` in the console, followed by enter `setstage C06 0` and finally `resurrect`.
- Kodlak's ghost may not appear when entering the final chamber.
  -  Using the console command `setstage C06 60` will allow you to put the witch's head in the fire, at which point Kodlak's wolf spirit will appear. After defeating the spirit, Kodlak may still not appear, at which point the console command `setstage C06 200` will end the quest as usual, with Aela exclaiming that she heard Kodlak pronounce you leader.
- If you leave the Underforge while the circle is talking after the funeral, the dialogue may not continue when you return.
- If you follow the Circle members heading to Ysgramor's Tomb after Wuuthrad has been assembled, the group may eventually get stuck running back and forth between Dawnstar and the mountain range about halfway towards Driftshade Refuge.
- If Eorlund isn't around: Go to the Skyforge and execute the following commands (note that player.placeatme does not work): "prid 1A683" then "resurrect" then "moveto player". Talk to him to continue the mission. **?**
- If enough time has passed since [Skjor](/wiki/Skyrim:Skjor "Skyrim:Skjor")'s death in [The Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Silver_Hand "Skyrim:The Silver Hand") to allow his body to be deleted, this quest may not start.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. Bethesda mistakenly included a mandatory alias for Skjor despite the fact that he's killed off before the questline gets this far. His alias is now marked as optional to allow the quest to start.
- [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") may be seen using the Skyforge while Kodlak's funeral scene is underway.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.6, addresses this issue. Her AI package will now disable sandbox behavior until you retrieve the final Wuuthrad fragment from Kodlak's room after Eorlund asks you to retrieve it.
- Kodlak's corpse may be seen without his Wolf Armor equipped during the funeral scene.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.6, fixes this bug.
- If you leave during the funeral and then begin the Battle for Whiterun, the funeral may be over when you return, and you won't be able to continue the quest. **?**

| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* Speak to Kodlak |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage C06 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest C06`.

# Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |

Glover Mallory's House

**Glover Mallory's House** is the home of [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is in the marketplace along the waterfront between [Morvayn Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Manor "Skyrim:Morvayn Manor") to the southeast and the [Abandoned Building](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Building "Skyrim:Abandoned Building") to the west.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory") [Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith") |

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").
- **[Paid in Full](/wiki/Skyrim:Paid_in_Full "Skyrim:Paid in Full")**: Recover the [bonemold formula](/wiki/Skyrim:Bonemold_Formula "Skyrim:Bonemold Formula") for [Glover Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory "Skyrim:Glover Mallory").

### Exterior

In front of the entrance is a porch attached to the house, complete with a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), with a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") and a [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plant to the right of the porch, and three more scathecraw plants to the left. A  "Guild") Guild shadowmark is on the wall of the house to the left of the entrance. To the right of the entrance around and beyond the smelter are six unusable barrels and another scathecraw plant. Along the back of the building on the waterfront is another scathecraw plant among more unusable barrels. The entrance has an adept-level lock.

### Glover Mallory's House

Glover's living area

The entrance leads into a cooking and living area on the lower floor of the house. In the southeast corner are two food barrels, with two copies of *[The Poison Song, Book II](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Poison_Song,_Book_II "Skyrim:The Poison Song, Book II")* on the wall ledge to the right. In the southwest corner are two chairs and a table holding two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), three [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a sample of [Felsaad tern feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Felsaad_Tern_Feathers "Skyrim:Felsaad Tern Feathers"), and copies of *[History of Raven Rock, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._I "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. I")* and *[Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._II "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. II")*. In the northwest corner is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand and a sideboard holding a bottle of [matze](/wiki/Skyrim:Matze "Skyrim:Matze"), a copy of *[The Red Year, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Year,_Vol._I "Skyrim:The Red Year, Vol. I")*, and an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox"). Along the north wall is a doorway to the next room. In the northeast corner are two food urns.

Stair room

The next room is circular, and features stairs leading up to the upper floor and down to the basement. Along the curved west wall are two food urns, six sacks, a food barrel with a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top, and a narrow table holding two more bottles of Nord mead, an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), and a copy of *[The Axe Man](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Axe_Man "Skyrim:The Axe Man")*.

Glover's sleeping area

The small circular room on the upper floor is the sleeping area. To the west near the top of the stairs is a chest, two chairs, and a small round table holding a red apple, a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), and a copy of *[The House of Troubles](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Troubles "Skyrim:The House of Troubles")*. To the south is an owned single bed. To the southwest is a sideboard holding two large [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a copy of *[Ahzidal's Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Descent "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Descent")*.

Basement stairs

The small circular basement room features a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover%27s_Guild_Key "Skyrim:Glover's Guild Key")-locked door on the south wall. To the southwest is a set of shelves holding copies of *[Bone, Part I](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_I "Skyrim:Bone, Part I")* and *[Part II](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone,_Part_II "Skyrim:Bone, Part II")*. To the west are two straw bales, a wood pile, and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). To the north beneath the stairs are three food barrels and another wood pile.

Glover's locked room

Beyond the key-locked door is a room dedicated to the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), with guild banners hanging on the wall opposite the door. In the northeast corner are two ingredient barrels and a chair. In the southeast corner is a [thief cache](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_Cache "Skyrim:Thief Cache") with the  "Cache") Cache shadowmark painted on the side; unlike all other caches, this cache doesn't include a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger").

On the south wall between the banners is a shield rack with a leveled enchanted [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield") and a leveled enchanted [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"). On the wall ledge below the rack is a leveled [light feet](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Light_Feet "Skyrim:Potion of Light Feet") potion, a leveled [pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") potion, a leveled [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") potion, a [strong box](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), and a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Glover's Letter") to Glover's [daughter](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_(person) "Skyrim:Sapphire (person)").

Along the west wall are two sideboards flanking a display case. The sideboard to the left of the display case holds three potent [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison") and two [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") poisons, six bottles of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), one bottle of [sujamma](/wiki/Skyrim:Sujamma "Skyrim:Sujamma"), one bottle of [shein](/wiki/Skyrim:Shein "Skyrim:Shein"), two empty [lesser soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), and one filled lesser soul gem. The display case contains a complete set of [Blackguard's armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Unique_Armor#Blackguard.27s_Armor "Skyrim:Unique Armor"). The sideboard to the right of the display case holds four [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), three bottles of [Black-Briar Reserve](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Reserve "Skyrim:Black-Briar Reserve"), five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), seven lockpicks, one large coin purse, two medium coin purses, and one small coin purse.

## Notes

- The [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Glover_Mallory%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Glover Mallory's House Key") carried by Glover Mallory only unlocks the entrance to the house. After completing the quest [Paid in Full](/wiki/Skyrim:Paid_in_Full "Skyrim:Paid in Full"), he will hand you the key that unlocks the basement door.
  - You don't need to be a part of the Thieves Guild in order to be able to access his basement storage room: you can get to it by using a plate (platter, wooden plate, etc.) pressed up against the door and using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") shout or running up against it to pass through the plate and into the room. All the items there are free to take, but you'll need another plate and the same method to get back out. Also, unless you're a friend to him, this process should only be used when he is out of the house (either during normal business hours, or when he's working on the shrine outside of town), as being there otherwise might be considered trespassing.

## Bugs

- All the Blackguard's Armor items will respawn when Glover's basement resets, allowing multiple copies of the set to be obtained. Glover's Letter also respawns along with the rest of the house, allowing you to give it to Sapphire repeatedly and receive unlimited Exquisite Sapphires, since she is not coded to respond only once to it.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=13442))
- The Blackguard's Armor pieces found here don't have an ArmorMaterial keyword assigned so the full set doesn't count toward the *Matching Set* perk.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Golden and Dark Smithing

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: *not written*  **Reward**: written by multiple users, *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Learn the secrets of [Golden](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden "Skyrim:Golden") and [Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark "Skyrim:Dark") smithing.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | *[Notes on the Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes_on_the_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Notes on the Blacksmith")* |
| Location(s): | Saints camp west of [Secunda's Kiss](/wiki/Skyrim:Secunda%27s_Kiss "Skyrim:Secunda's Kiss"); [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill") |
| Reward: | [Golden](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden "Skyrim:Golden") and [Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark "Skyrim:Dark") smithing. |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE025\_MiscQuest\_GSDSGearBook |
| Added by: | [Saints & Seducers](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers") |

Joften the blacksmith has hidden his "toys"

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find Joften's notes on Golden and Dark Smithing.
2. Read Joften's notes.

## Detailed Walkthrough

While investigating the first Saints camp for [Balance of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Balance_of_Power "Skyrim:Balance of Power"), you will slay the [Saints Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Saints Bandit Leader"). In his corpse is a note called *[Notes on the Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Notes_on_the_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Notes on the Blacksmith")*, which gives details about the blacksmith Joften and his ability to forge Golden & Dark equipment. However, it would appear the bandits lost patience with Joften, who became increasingly insane, and ended up killing him. His notes, however, are hidden and would likely reveal his secrets. The only hint given was that as a child, Joften used to play in the area around [Half-Moon Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Half-Moon_Mill "Skyrim:Half-Moon Mill"), so the bandits had intended to investigate there.

Head to Half-Moon Mill and search under the bridge to find a chest containing *[Joften's Notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Joften%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Joften's Notes")* as well as other loot. Reading the journal will complete the quest and allow you to craft Golden/Dark equipment once you have the Daedric Smithing perk.

The chest and the note will be there regardless of whether the quest has been started, so if the player did not loot the note that starts the quest and the Saints Bandit Leader's corpse despawned, they can still learn Golden and Dark smithing.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE025_MiscQuest_GSDSGearBook stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE025_MiscQuest_GSDSGearBook`.

# Skyrim:Goldenglow Estate
