Goldenglow Estate

**Goldenglow Estate** is a [honey farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Settlements "Skyrim:Settlements") west of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") containing [mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercenary_(Goldenglow) "Skyrim:Mercenary (Goldenglow)"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the farm's owner [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth"). It contains four zones: *[Goldenglow Estate Sewer](#Goldenglow_Estate_Sewer)*, *[Goldenglow Estate](#Goldenglow_Estate)*, *[Goldenglow Estate Second Floor](#Goldenglow_Estate_Second_Floor)*, and *[Goldenglow Estate Basement](#Goldenglow_Estate_Basement)*.

The estate is inaccessible before the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quest [Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear") is started, until which time the door to the estate will be locked and the entire area will be protected by invisible walls. All items in and on the estate are not marked as owned and are therefore free to take. The mercenaries will be hostile to you at all times.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Aringoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Aringoth "Skyrim:Aringoth")  [Mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercenary_(Goldenglow) "Skyrim:Mercenary (Goldenglow)") |

### Thieves Guild

- **[Loud and Clear](/wiki/Skyrim:Loud_and_Clear "Skyrim:Loud and Clear")**: Send a message to a former [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") client.
- **[The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny")**: Find items for [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") throughout the [questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Primary_Quests "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

### Exterior

The estate comprises a house, an apiary, and docks on a group of three small islands in [Lake Honrich](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Honrich "Skyrim:Lake Honrich") connected by footbridges. The front gate can only be unlocked with the [gate key](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Gate_Key "Skyrim:Goldenglow Gate Key"), which is carried by the mercenary watching the gate. There are many mercenaries guarding the outside of the property. Most of these are within earshot of each other, and will converge on you when you engage in battle. Near the cart to the northeast of the gate are some barrels of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). From the front gate, the path forks, with a turn to the west that leads across a wooden bridge to the pasture and the beehives. Under the bridge is a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant. There are also many [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), and [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") covering the islands that make up the estate. The other fork of the path continues onward to the north, crossing a stone bridge and ultimately leading to the front door of the house. This door is unlocked. Outside, in front of the house, is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), two [chicken nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), and a large wooden platform. To the right of the front door is a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). At the rear of the property is the [sewer](#Goldenglow_Estate_Sewer) exit. Nearby is the rear door to the house, which is locked, but leads into a deserted corridor ideal for quiet infiltration. The path continues past the house and curves around to the docks at the rear of the property. There is a second wooden bridge southwest of the house that crosses to the main pasture, where the beehives are kept. There are several wooden lookout platforms on all sides of the islands.

### Goldenglow Estate Sewer

If you speak to [Vex](/wiki/Skyrim:Vex "Skyrim:Vex") before coming to the honey farm during the related quest, she will advise you of a sewer entrance that provides a discreet method of infiltration. This will add an optional quest objective and a map marker showing the location of the sewer entrance on the western side of the main island. Upon entering, you will be in a darkened tunnel heading to the north. Following the tunnel, you will encounter two skeevers. You will then come to a small chamber, with another tunnel heading east. A short distance into the tunnel, you will see more skeevers ahead. Just in front of them are two [tripwires](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that release an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns"), which will ignite a series of [oil slicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") along this part of the tunnel. Firing the slicks is an easy way to deal with the skeevers without the risk of contracting a [disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Diseases "Skyrim:Diseases").

Partway along the tunnel is an adept-locked gate on the right. This opens into a small room, with the skeletal remains of someone lying on a bedroll with a copy of the [Pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Guide to Better Thieving](/wiki/Skyrim:Guide_to_Better_Thieving "Skyrim:Guide to Better Thieving")* next to it, an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the left, and several bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") scattered around the room. Farther along the tunnel is a circular room with a central stone pillar; the room may contain more living skeevers, and features many human and animal bones scattered on the floor. A tunnel exits the room heading east, but take care: there is another tripwire at the entrance to this tunnel that triggers a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap. At the end of the tunnel, on the left is a ladder leading up and outside, and on the right is a hole in the ceiling serving as a shortcut exit from the house's basement.

### Goldenglow Estate

Climbing the ladder brings you out beside the main house, with the farm's docks to the southeast where a large ship and a rowboat are docked. Near the docks are several food barrels under a wooden structure. To the right is the rear entrance for the house, which is locked. The first floor consists of six rooms connected by four hallways, and there are four doors that lead to other areas of the estate.

Entering this rear door leads into a deserted corridor heading southwest, with a door on your immediate right, a T-junction ahead, an adept-locked door farther along on the right, and a turning at the end to the southeast. The door on the right opens into a room with a long wooden table and chairs with an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), two cheese wheels, and a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") in a cast iron pot on top. Against the southwest wall is a round wooden table with four pieces of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on top. Against the northwest wall is a doorway, and to the left is a set of shelves holding two [drums](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), and two food sacks. Against the northeast wall is a set of shelves and a long end table, both holding only clutter. The doorway at the end leads out into another corridor parallel to the first, with a turn to the southeast and an open double door ahead. The turn leads to the T-junction in the first corridor, and has two long end tables with a set of shelves between them. On the shelves is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), and on the far end table is a bottle of alto wine and two bottles of wine. Opposite the shelves is another corridor heading to the southwest, also parallel to the first.

The room ahead is a kitchen, with two long wooden tables in an L-shape holding a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), many pieces of cheese, and two loaves of bread. There are three sets of shelves in the room, one against the northeast wall, one against a partition wall, and the third at the rear of the room against the southwest wall. These hold a total of five bottles of alto wine, twelve bottles of wine, ten loaves of bread, and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"). Hanging above the tables is a rack holding five [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), and to the right also hanging from the ceiling are four [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and two bunches of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). There are more loaves of bread in a basket on the floor beside the tables, and another rack hanging from the ceiling toward the rear of the room holding two more rabbits and three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). In the southern corner is a large vat.

Taking the corridor opposite the shelves leads to a room at the front of the building, with an exit in the middle of the southwest wall and an end table between two benches against the southeast wall. In the west corner is a food barrel. Against the northwest wall is a long wooden table with a bottle of alto wine, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and a copy of the *[Life of Uriel Septim VII](/wiki/Skyrim:Life_of_Uriel_Septim_VII "Skyrim:Life of Uriel Septim VII")*. Against the northeast wall is a cupboard holding clutter, with a round wooden table to the left with a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") on top. To the left is an apprentice-locked wooden door that leads into a small storeroom containing two sets of shelves and a barrel of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). On the shelves is a locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), a bulb of garlic, an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), and some bread and cheese. Leaning against one of the sets of shelves is a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute").

The adept-locked door in the first corridor leads to another storeroom containing three sets of shelves. One set of shelves holds many pieces of cheese and four cabbages, another holds only clutter, and the third holds a leveled [potion of pickpocketing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Pickpocketing "Skyrim:Potion of Pickpocketing") and a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). There are several sacks and two barrels containing foodstuffs, as well as three baskets, one containing [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), another containing [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and the third containing [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") and [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"). Finally, there are two unlocked chests in the room.

At the end of the corridor, the hall turns to the southeast and opens into a room. At the far end of the room you can see a mercenary sitting at a table against the far wall, facing away from you. Two long end tables are against the southwest wall, and a small end table is on your left, beside a wooden bench. To the right of the bench is a doorway into a dining room with a large [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") head mounted on the opposite wall. The dining room can be used to [sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") past the nearby mercenaries if your sneak skill is good enough. To the right of the doorway is a round wooden table and two chairs, and an end table beside it. On the table is a loaf of bread. At the far end of the room is an empty set of shelves facing away from you, with the table and chairs the mercenary is sitting at behind it. There are two other mercenaries at the end, one patrolling a corridor to the left, and the other sitting out of sight. The corridor to the left has a long end table against the southeast wall. To the right of the corridor is an apprentice-locked door leading to another storeroom, which contains a set of shelves holding a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") and three common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"), with an unlocked chest to the left.

Down the middle of the dining room are two long wooden tables laid end-to-end, with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a cabbage, a drum, two [goat cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), and four loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. In the southern, western, and northern corners are sets of shelves holding clutter, with a few [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), and a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") on top. Against the northwest and southeast walls are long end tables, with a square wooden table also against the southeast wall. In the eastern corner is another doorway. Through the doorway is yet another corridor with a flight of stairs up to the second floor to the left, while to the right is a novice-locked gate. In front of the gate is the corridor patrolled by the mercenary from the far end of the previous room. Behind the gate is a small end table and a flight of stairs descending into the basement and the shortcut back to the sewer seen from below. If you are sneaking, you will need to listen for the mercenary to start walking away from you to open the gate. It can be opened with the [cellar key](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Goldenglow Cellar Key") carried by Aringoth.

### Goldenglow Estate Second Floor

The second floor consists of seven rooms, with only one long corridor and one exit back to the first floor. Through the door is a room with three sets of shelves against the walls holding a bottle of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"), five bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two bottles of alto wine, and three bottles of wine. There are three round wooden tables and chairs arranged around the middle of the room, with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a total of ten loose septims on the tables. A [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") is in the room's western corner. To the northwest is a doorway with a small square table to the right of it. Through the doorway is a corridor with two turns, and an open door opposite with another storeroom behind. The storeroom contains a food barrel and a set of shelves holding a woodcutter's axe, a pair of iron boots, a flute, and a bulb of garlic.

Following the turns in the corridor past two wooden benches (one of which holds an apothecary's satchel), ahead is a set of shelves holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and a food sack. To the left the corridor continues, passing a door on the left; at the far end you can see a mercenary leaning against the wall facing away from you. If your sneak skill is high enough, you can avoid alerting him. The door on the left leads into a bedroom containing two unowned single beds coming out from the southeast wall, and a dresser between them with a flute and a common book on top. By the northeastern wall is a dresser. In the western corner is a small square table, with a set of shelves coming out from the southwest wall facing it. On the shelves is a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), three bulbs of garlic, and a cabbage. To the left of the shelves is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), and farther to the left is an open door back into the corridor. If you left the mercenary at the end of the previous corridor, as you leave through this door, you will need to hug this side of the corridor, as to the right is another wardrobe that will block you from view of the mercenary. If you instead opt to kill the mercenary, you will find a small square table holding bread and cheese in the corridor across from where he stood, and a wardrobe nearby. Turning left, at the end is a corridor heading northeast ending in a doorway, with a round table on the right holding a bulb of garlic and three loose septims. On your immediate right before the round table is a doorway into a room, with a mercenary sitting at a table against the southwest wall. There is an iron dagger, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), and a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") on the table, and two wardrobes against the south wall. On the left is a novice-locked door into Aringoth's bedroom.

The doorway at the end of the previous corridor leads into another bedroom containing an unowned single bed in the western corner, a dresser by the foot of the bed containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), and a small square table and chair against the northeast wall with a bowl of [beef stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Beef_Stew "Skyrim:Beef Stew"), a [pheasant roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Roast "Skyrim:Pheasant Roast"), and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on top. Against the southeast wall is a wardrobe, with an adept-locked door to the right. Behind this door is another small storeroom, which contains a set of shelves holding a large coin purse, two loose septims, a leveled [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), and a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") hidden under the sack beside it. On top of the shelves is an apothecary's satchel. Also in this room are several food sacks and a barrel with three loose septims on top.

Aringoth's room contains a long wooden table on your left upon entering with a knapsack, a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a purple mountain flower, and three loose septims on top. To the right of the door is a cupboard holding clutter, and a set of shelves against the southeast wall holding six bottles of alto wine and eight bottles of wine. To the north is a slightly raised section with a double bed coming out of the middle of the north wall. Aringoth will likely be crouching beside a cupboard on the left. You will need a Speech skill of 75 (53 with the Persuasion perk) to successfully persuade Aringoth to give you the [safe key](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Safe_Key "Skyrim:Goldenglow Safe Key"), or alternatively you may kill him and take it off his corpse along with the cellar key to the novice-locked gate blocking access to the basement. The cupboard beside him holds two drums. On either side of the bed are small tables, with the one on the right having a unique [Queen Bee Statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Queen_Bee_Statue "Skyrim:Queen Bee Statue") on top. This can be sold to [Delvin](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") in [The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon") for a tidy sum, and is one of several unique items found throughout [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") that are part of the quest [The Litany of Larceny](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Litany_of_Larceny "Skyrim:The Litany of Larceny") that only ever appear as miscellaneous quests to return the items to him. At the foot of the bed is an apprentice-locked chest containing minor loot. To the left of the bed is a dresser with a unique [Bee in a Jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Bee_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Bee in a Jar") on top and a wardrobe farther to the left. To the right of the bed is a set of shelves holding a bottle of alto wine, two bottles of wine, a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), and a red and a blue mountain flower. Against the east wall is a round wooden table and two chairs, with a bottle of alto wine and a medium coin purse on the table.

### Goldenglow Estate Basement

Through the novice-locked gate on the main floor and down the stairs is a room with two sets of shelves holding a few food sacks and a door to the basement. As soon as you enter the basement, you are in a large room full of broken and disused furniture and cobwebs showing the basement isn't in regular use, with two mercenaries in the corner diagonally opposite. Both mercenaries will be carrying copies of the cellar key. In the same corner as the mercenaries is an apprentice-locked chest. Opposite the basement entrance is another door leading to a corridor heading northwest that soon ends at a T-junction. To the left is a room containing a round wooden table with a small coin purse on top, while to the right in a small alcove are two [deer hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), a [wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt"), and a [bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt"). Turning right at the junction, the corridor turns first to the northwest and then to the southwest. Ahead you can see an oil slick on the ground, which you can use to deal with a mercenary who is just around the corner out of sight. Past the mercenary is a flight of stairs descending to the southeast. At the bottom, a room on the left contains a novice-locked chest holding minor loot, with the [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Safe "Skyrim:Safe") to the right, and a round wooden table beside the safe. On the table is a small and a large coin purse and three loose septims. The safe is expert-locked, but can be opened using the safe key carried by Aringoth, and contains the *[Goldenglow Bill of Sale](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenglow_Bill_of_Sale_(safe) "Skyrim:Goldenglow Bill of Sale (safe)")*. To the southeast is an unlocked gate with a trapdoor behind leading back into the sewer. Through the trapdoor is a short twisting tunnel leading to the hole in the floor seen from below.

## Notes

- If you try to enter the premises before Loud and Clear has begun, you will be blocked by invisible barriers all over the place.

## Bugs

- Goldenglow Estate isn't marked as owned by the faction Aringoth and the mercenaries belong to, making it possible to enter and take everything inside without penalty.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.
- Everything outside respawns despite the building itself being classed as a "no-reset zone". **?**

Goldenhills Farm Bunkhouse

**Goldenhills Farm Bunkhouse** is a small house at [Goldenhills Plantation](/wiki/Skyrim:Goldenhills_Plantation "Skyrim:Goldenhills Plantation"), east of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). Initially the [farmhands](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmhand "Skyrim:Farmhand") and [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") you hire will set up camp next to the stables, east of the main house. These bedrolls will be replaced by the bunkhouse as soon as you [construct](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction") it using the [Farmer's Workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer%27s_Workbench "Skyrim:Farmer's Workbench").

It consists of one area only, *[Goldenhills Farm Bunkhouse](#Goldenhills_Farm_Bunkhouse)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Farmhands](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmhand "Skyrim:Farmhand") †  [Personal Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") ‡ |

† Two farmhands can be hired during the quest [A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me"). They can later be dismissed. Your Personal Steward can hire 2 [Farmhands](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmhand "Skyrim:Farmhand"), or you can hire [Angrenor Once-Honored](/wiki/Skyrim:Angrenor_Once-Honored "Skyrim:Angrenor Once-Honored"), [Brenuin](/wiki/Skyrim:Brenuin "Skyrim:Brenuin"), [Embry](/wiki/Skyrim:Embry "Skyrim:Embry"), or [Narfi](/wiki/Skyrim:Narfi "Skyrim:Narfi").
‡ You can appoint one of your [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") (see [list](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward#Followers_Who_Can_Become_Stewards "Skyrim:Personal Steward") of those available) or your [Spouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") as steward to run the farm. They can later be dismissed after completing [A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me").

## Goldenhills Farm Bunkhouse

Bunkhouse interior

The bunkhouse contains little of any value. A single [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") can be found in front of the fire. [Dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), and [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") can all be found hanging inside. The two tables hold food and farm equipment respectively. On the opposite side of the house are the three beds used by any individuals you hire to work on the farm.

Goldenhills Plantation

**Goldenhills Plantation** is an abandoned [farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Farms "Skyrim:Farms") east of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). The farm is initially haunted, but you will be able to claim it as your own once you've put the spirits to rest as part of the quest [The Unquiet Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Unquiet_Dead "Skyrim:The Unquiet Dead")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming "Skyrim:Farming"). The farm has various exterior [construction](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction") options, and you can hire a [personal steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward") to manage the farm's production and buy upgrades for the farmhouse interior. You are also able to set any [pet](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers#Creatures "Skyrim:Followers") capable of combat (with the exceptions of [Meeko](/wiki/Skyrim:Meeko "Skyrim:Meeko") and [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh")) to guard the farm. Like the steward, these can be swapped out at any time.

The interior of the farmhouse consists of 5 rooms across three floors, including a two-room basement and a large master bedroom/loft. There's a skill book [Song of the Alchemists](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Alchemists "Skyrim:Song of the Alchemists") on the shelf in the basement.

[‡](#note_Library)The Child's Bedroom and the Library/Display Room are exclusive, as they occupy the same room. You can switch from the Library/Display Room to the Child's Bedroom for 500 gold. However, once selected, you cannot change the Child's Bedroom to the Library/Display Room.

## Income

One farmhand makes 12.5% more money than no farmhand, two farmhands make 25% more money than no farmhand. [Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction") makes 15% more money, bunkhouse's benefit is always available even if there's no farmhand. Bunkhouse can stack with farmhands, makes 1.25\*1.15=1.4375 times comparing to the base income.
There's definitely a fractional part that doesn't show directly in the game when calculate the income.
Though you cannot collect gold while you have no steward, profits will still accumulate over time despite not having a steward assigned. Simply hire a steward to collect all the money.
The plantation has a total of 38 plots of [Fertile Soil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fertile_Soil "Skyrim:Fertile Soil") (27 in front of the house, 11 on the side of the house). By building the [Exterior Decoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction") you gain an additional 6 plots of Fertile Soil, bringing the total of available plots of Fertile Soil to 44.

| Project | Base income per day |
| --- | --- |
| plant any ingredient | ingredient value \* planted number |
| livestock a cow | 50 |
| livestock 2 goats | 2\*20=40 |
| livestock 3 chicken | 3\*10=30 |
| [Apiary](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction") | 50 |
| [Windmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Farming_Construction "Skyrim:Farming Construction") | 100 |
| total | 270 |

If prefer the alchemy way, 12 [Creep Cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), 19 [Mora Tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), and 13 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") produces the most profitable potions for selling to make money, don't forget to also harvest the Pantry Cupboard inside the house. But if you have some obsessive compulsive disorder and want to neglect the Pantry Cupboard, 12 [Creep Cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), 20 [Mora Tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), and 12 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") is also good.
If prefer the lazy way, planting all 44 fertile soils with [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") can make the most profitable automatically, with all projects in the table above, (44\*12+270)\*1.4375=1147 gold/day can be collected from the steward.

## Notes

- There's a [Nord War Horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Unobtainable_Items#Nord_War_Horn "Skyrim:Unobtainable Items") in Rin's room, which is unobtainable otherwise, a unique Alembic in [Jonquil](/wiki/Skyrim:Jonquil "Skyrim:Jonquil")'s secret lab, a [Broken Iron War Axe Head](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Broken_Iron_War_Axe_Head "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots") and a [Broken Iron War Axe Handle](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots#Broken_Iron_War_Axe_Handle "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots") in the box on the second floor. They will disappear once the rooms are renovated.
- After completing [A Farmer's Life For Me](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Farmer%27s_Life_For_Me "Skyrim:A Farmer's Life For Me"), the steward can be fired and rehired as much as you like. An active steward cannot be asked to follow you (as opposed to [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") [stewards](/wiki/Skyrim:Personal_Steward "Skyrim:Personal Steward")), so they must be fired to do so. The same is true with the guard pet.
- Unlike at your [player-built homes](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), you can create butter by placing milk into the butter churn here, and you don't need to wait for it to replenish.
- Not all containers can be used as safe storage. The two barrels at left side when enter the cellar and the Fish Barrels behind the workbench are all respawning containers.
  -  This issue has been addressed by the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"); barrels in the house don't respawn anymore.
- [Armored Trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Armored_Troll "Skyrim:Armored Troll") that are told to guard the farm cannot be taken as followers again. Once dismissed as a guard, you cannot ask it to follow and you will have to buy a new one.
- You can use console commands to swap the children's room for the library. Select the addition you currently have using `prid <RefID>`, then type `disable` to remove it. Then type `prid <RefID>` to select the addition you want, and type `enable` to enable it instead. The RefID for the children’s room is `FExxx945` and the library is `FExxx94A`.
- Changing the shrine in your library via console commands is possible.[*verification needed — what's the default?*] First, remove your current shrine by typing `prid <RefID>` then `disable`, and place the new one by typing `prid <RefID>` then `enable`. The RefIDs for the shrines are Akatosh: `FExxxD96`, Arkay: `FExxxD7E`, Azura: `FExxx8FC`, Boethiah: `FExxxD94`, Dibella: `FExxx90C`, Julianos: `FExxxBFC`, Kynareth: `FExxxC86`, Mara: `FExxxC54`, Mephala: `FExxxBD6`, Stendarr: `FExxxC51`, Talos: `FExxxD8F`, and Zenithar: `FExxxD75`.

## Bugs

- Purchasing the alchemy and enchanting lab and entering the house may crash the game.
  - Purchasing this upgrade last seems to prevent this. If this happens, try to purchase the upgrade, then fast travel away and back before entering the house for the first time.
- Children and pets may not recognize the farm as a home. However, [Hilda](/wiki/Skyrim:Hilda "Skyrim:Hilda") (the pet goat) goes there if the player commands it.
- Children may freeze in place at the spot they are adopted.
- If children are adopted before Grelod the Kind is killed, your child might get stuck at the orphanage. Even if you tell them "it's time for bed". They still have all of the regular dialogue they would at your home, however they will not leave the orphanage. **?**
- Once the Dawnguard quest line is started random groups of three vampires will attack the farm. Farm animals including horses will protect the farm. **?**
- The cupboard at the bottom of the stairs will be replaced by a Pantry Cupboard later, leaving any stored items in the original cupboard permanently inaccessible. **?**
  - To recover the items, use the following console command: `"FExxxDB9".removeallitems player`.

Goldenrock Mine

**Goldenrock Mine** is a small [corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum "Skyrim:Corundum") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") in southeastern [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing"). It contains only one zone, *[Goldenrock Mine](#Goldenrock_Mine)*.

It was discovered and established by the adventurer [Annekke Crag-Jumper](/wiki/Skyrim:Annekke_Crag-Jumper "Skyrim:Annekke Crag-Jumper"). [Verner Rock-Chucker](/wiki/Skyrim:Verner_Rock-Chucker "Skyrim:Verner Rock-Chucker") will [buy corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore") from you.

## Residents

| Goldenrock Mine Camp |
| --- |
| [Derkeethus](/wiki/Skyrim:Derkeethus "Skyrim:Derkeethus") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") \*  [Hrefna](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrefna "Skyrim:Hrefna")  [Sondas Drenim](/wiki/Skyrim:Sondas_Drenim "Skyrim:Sondas Drenim")  [Tormir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tormir "Skyrim:Tormir") |

\* Only appears after completing the quest [Extracting an Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Extracting_an_Argonian "Skyrim:Extracting an Argonian").

## Related Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Mine Ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Mine_Ore "Skyrim:Mine Ore")**: Get paid to [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") ore. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Mine treasure

Around the entrance to the mine are stacks of crates and food sacks that are marked as owned. Among these are four pieces of owned [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore"). The [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") is a few paces away, with three owned [corundum ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ingot "Skyrim:Corundum Ingot") on the ground beside it.

The miners' camp is just outside and to the right of the mine entrance. It consists of a central campfire surrounded by four small tents, three of which contain bedrolls, while the fourth contains a hay pile. Once you are on friendly terms with the settlement, you can use these freely. Eight whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") hang on fishing racks behind the tents.

### Goldenrock Mine

Mine interior

The mine has many [pickaxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") and shovels lying around. The entrance tunnel descends to the southeast to a T-junction with a corundum ore vein on the ground at the junction and a dead end to the right with a second ore vein. The tunnel continues descending ahead. At the bottom there is a braced section with a bedroll under it along with a couple food barrels; on top of one of the barrels is a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Chimarvamidium](/wiki/Skyrim:Chimarvamidium "Skyrim:Chimarvamidium")*. The tunnel turns to the northeast and opens into a larger cavern with wooden scaffolding around a central rock pillar allowing access to two more ore veins. At the bottom on the left are several food sacks and a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") on a stack of crates. Ascending the ramp leads to the two ore veins on the walls, a small round wooden table with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top, and an open box holding three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead").

## Maps

- 

  Goldenrock Mine

# Skyrim:Good Intentions

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Find and consult the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"), [The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden") |
| Reward: | [Mage's Circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Mage%27s_Circlet "Skyrim:Mage's Circlet") |
| ID: | MG04 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books") | **Next →** [Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Hitting the Books](/wiki/Skyrim:Hitting_the_Books "Skyrim:Hitting the Books") | | → Next | [Revealing the Unseen](/wiki/Skyrim:Revealing_the_Unseen "Skyrim:Revealing the Unseen") | | |

Quaranir waiting to speak with you

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak with [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir").
2. Listen to Tolfdir.
3. Follow [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano").
4. Speak with [Quaranir](/wiki/Skyrim:Quaranir "Skyrim:Quaranir").
5. Find the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain").
6. Report to [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren").

### An Orb Worth Noting

Quaranir freezing time to speak with you

After your conversation with Urag gro-Shub about the newly recovered books, the librarian suggests you speak with Tolfdir about the findings. Tolfdir can be found in the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements"), in deep rumination about the orb from [Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Saarthal "Skyrim:Saarthal"), or [the Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus"). Let him know about your findings and he will begin to discuss the Eye with you. He will explain how the markings seem to be unique, as they do not appear to be [Elven](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeris "Lore:Aldmeris"), [Daedric](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Alphabet "Lore:Daedric Alphabet"), or [Ayleid](/wiki/Lore:Ayleid_Language "Lore:Ayleid Language"). Ancano will interrupt Tolfdir's musings and demand that you follow him to meet a mysterious visitor who has asked to speak with you.

### A Moment in Time

Follow Ancano to the Arch-Mage's quarters and you will meet Quaranir, another representative from the [Psijic Order.](/wiki/Skyrim:Psijic_Order "Skyrim:Psijic Order") Quaranir will freeze time in order to speak privately with you. He will explain that you must prevent anyone from using the Eye of Magnus, as he fears the consequences its misuse will bring. He will suggest that you seek out the Augur of Dunlain within the College, who may be able to give you better guidance. Quaranir will then unfreeze time and leave, confusing Savos and angering Ancano.
Speaking to the various mages about the Augur will lead you to either Tolfdir or [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") for more information. Tolfdir will tell you about the Augur immediately, but you must pass an easy-level [Speech check](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Persuasion_Options "Skyrim:Speech") to convince Mirabelle. Either way, you will learn that the Augur is a former student at the College, but something befell him as a result of his own ambitions. He can now be found in [The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden") in his altered state.

The Augur of Dunlain

### The Unearthing

You can access the Midden from a trap door in the northern corner of the courtyard or by the stairwell in the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"). Making your way to the Augur of Dunlain is relatively easy; you will likely encounter a few [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), along with a small number of [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton").
Proceed into [The Midden Dark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden#The_Midden_Dark "Skyrim:The Midden") and continue until you reach a locked door. When you approach it, the Augur will warn you from the other side that your efforts will only end in disappointment. The door will then open.

### The Augur

The Augur will inform you that others (including Ancano) have previously sought information about the Eye of Magnus without realizing the dangers it poses. While the Augur speaks only of disaster for the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"), he seems encouraged by your path and offers to help you further. He will then inform you that you will need the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus") to avert the disaster the Psijics warned you about, and urges you to share this information with [Savos Aren](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren").

### More than a Mere Apprentice

Speak to Savos and inform him of the Augur's message. It takes a bit of convincing to get Savos motivated and interested in this turn of events. Eventually, he will direct you to Mirabelle Ervine for more information on the Staff and then give you the [Mage's Circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Mage%27s_Circlet "Skyrim:Mage's Circlet"), impressed with your performance thus far.

## Notes

- After Quaranir freezes time but before you speak to him you can steal any item in the Arch-Mage's Quarters without acquiring a bounty.
- If you follow Quaranir out of the College after he freezes time in the Arch-Mage's Quarters, he will walk through Winterhold and enter [The Frozen Hearth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Frozen_Hearth "Skyrim:The Frozen Hearth").
- After you receive the objective to "Report to Savos Aren", [Atronach Forge Recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") will begin to appear in random loot.
- When the Eye of Magnus appears in the Hall of the Elements, there is an option to "Activate Eye of Magnus" when you point your crosshairs over it in close proximity, but doing so has no effect.

## Bugs

- When you enter the Arch-Mage's Quarters and go upstairs, time may stop yet Quaranir is not there, and you're stuck forever.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
  -  Open the console and manually advance the quest by entering `setstage MG04 40`.
  -  Using the console command `prid 0002BA3D` and then `moveto player`, will move him to the College, and the quest should proceed normally.
- When the quest begins, you may be able to use the door linking the Arcaneum to the Arch-Mage's Quarters, even though the Arch-Mage's Quarters is supposed to be off-limits at that point. Entering prior to being told to go there by Ancano will freeze out the quest, requiring you to exit the game via the console.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- You may not get the next quest "Revealing the Unseen" after completing the quest. This appears to be permanent and cannot be fixed by reloading. As the quest does not load, Mirabelle will have normal dialogue and the quest is impossible to begin.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
- When talking to Ancano after talking to Tolfdir, you may get locked in dialogue with him permanently, preventing you from doing anything. **?**
  -  Open the console and manually advance the quest by entering `setstage MG04 30`.
- Ancano may not open the door to the Arch-Mage's Quarters and lead you there. **?**
  -  Open the console command and manually advance the quest stage by entering `setstage MG04 30`. The quest marker above Ancano's head should disappear. The door to the Arch-Mage's Quarters should be unlocked. You are now free to talk to Quaranir and continue the storyline.
- The Augur of Dunlain may be unable to speak his expected lines if you go to the Midden before asking where he is. This is due to a set of bad conditions on the quest script.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.8, fixes this bug.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MG04 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MG04`.

# Skyrim:Grave Concoctions

## Overview

Grave Concoctions in Falkreath

**Grave Concoctions** is a store in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") specializing in [alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") and home for [Zaria](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaria "Skyrim:Zaria") who runs the store.

Grave Concoctions

It is found between [Lod's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod%27s_House "Skyrim:Lod's House") and [Falkreath Barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Barracks "Skyrim:Falkreath Barracks"), opposite the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Falkreath) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Falkreath)").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Zaria](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaria "Skyrim:Zaria") [Alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Alchemist") |

## Related Quests

- **[Alchemy Tutorial](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Tutorial "Skyrim:Alchemy Tutorial")**: Learn the basics of potion making. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

There is a wooden bench in front of the house and a patch of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") mushroom growing to the right. It is difficult entering with [stealth](/wiki/Skyrim:Stealth "Skyrim:Stealth") due to a [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Guard "Skyrim:Falkreath Guard") being posted opposite outside the Jarl's Longhouse.

### Grave Concoctions

The store is run by [Zaria](/wiki/Skyrim:Zaria "Skyrim:Zaria"), a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") immigrant that moved to Falkreath to explore her love of [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"). The store's name honors the large cemetery - a tradition shared by many of the businesses in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"), such as [Corpselight Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpselight_Farm "Skyrim:Corpselight Farm") and [Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink") - although she always comments on the name, showing concern that it might put you off.

Upon entering, the counter is immediately on your left, on which there is a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and several [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") that can be bought or stolen, while under the counter is a copy of *[On the Great Collapse](/wiki/Skyrim:On_the_Great_Collapse "Skyrim:On the Great Collapse")* and a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"). Behind the counter in the southwestern corner of the building is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel, which is where Zaria normally spends her time making [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison") and potions. Beside the lab is a basket containing a sample of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and, against the east wall, a cupboard holding several potions and [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") that she sells, along with a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). Hanging from the ceiling above the cupboard are two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). Opposite the door is a fireplace, with several barrels containing ingredients to the left. On the hearth is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and on the mantelpiece there are a few poisons and potions on display.

To the right of the fire is another cupboard, above this are three more bunches of elves ear and two more of frost mirriam. The cupboard only holds clutter. To the right of the cupboard obscured by baskets is a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[De Rerum Dirennis](/wiki/Skyrim:De_Rerum_Dirennis "Skyrim:De Rerum Dirennis")*. Coming out from the middle of the west wall is an owned single bed, with an end table to the left and a dresser to the right. On the end table is a bottle each of wine and alto wine, while on the dresser is a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"). To the right against the north wall is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot. To the right of this is a round wooden table and two chairs, holding a bottle of wine on one and a bottle of wine and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on the other.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, on counters and the like. They can be purchased from the merchant or stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

- Ingredients: 6 [Deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell"), 1 [Fire Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), 1 Fly Amanita, 3 [Frost Salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), 1 Giant's Toe, 6 [Hagraven Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), 1 [Hagraven Feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), 1 [Ice Wraith Teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), 1 [Jazbay Grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), 5 [Rock Warbler Egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), 2 [Salt Pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), 1 [Scaly Pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), 1 [Spriggan Sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), 1 [Taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), 1 [Troll Fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat")
- Poisons: 1 [Weak Fear Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Fear_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Fear Poison"), 1 [Weak Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison")
- Potions: 1 [Conjurer's Potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer%27s_Potion "Skyrim:Conjurer's Potion"), 1 [Draught of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health"), 1 [Potion of Brief Invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"), 1 [Potion of Cure Disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), 1 [Potion of Extra Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), 2 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 1 [Potion of Plentiful Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Stamina"), 1 [Potion of Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Stamina"), 1 [Potion of True Shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"), 1 [Solution of Lasting Potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Solution of Lasting Potency")

This is the merchandise found in Grave Concoction's [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

## Notes

- The name for the inside of the store appears as "Watchman's Hut" on the local map. This is due to the location data present being `FalkreathWatchmansHutLocation`. This implies the building might've had a completely different purpose altogether originally.
- Grave Concoctions [also appears](/wiki/Legends:Grave_Concoctions "Legends:Grave Concoctions") in [Legends](/wiki/Legends:Legends "Legends:Legends").

## Bugs

- Grave Concoctions is not flagged with keywords to mark it as a dwelling or a store despite it being both.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Gray Pine Goods

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Store: Gray Pine Goods ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gray+Pine+Goods)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Proprietor | [Solaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Solaf "Skyrim:Solaf") |
| Services | |
| [Gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Commerce#Merchants.27_Gold "Skyrim:Commerce") | 750 (+500 [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor"); +1000 [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader")) |
| Sells | See [Standard Merchandise](#Standard_Merchandise) |
| Buys | All |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| FalkreathGrayPineGoods | |
| Region | |
| [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | |
| Location | |
| [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") | |

Gray Pine Goods on a rare sunny day

**Gray Pine Goods** is a small general goods store in [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") home to the proprietor [Solaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Solaf "Skyrim:Solaf") and his brother [Bolund](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolund "Skyrim:Bolund").

Gray Pine Goods

It is near the center of Falkreath, opposite [Dead Man's Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Drink "Skyrim:Dead Man's Drink") and next to [Lod's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lod%27s_House "Skyrim:Lod's House").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bolund](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolund "Skyrim:Bolund")  [Solaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Solaf "Skyrim:Solaf") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods") |

### Exterior

The building has a balcony at the front, which is accessible from the rear via a flight of wooden stairs or from the door on the top floor of the house. Underneath the balcony to the left of the entrance is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel. To the right of the property is another flight of stairs ascending to the top of a wall that serves as a lookout point for the town guards.

### Gray Pine Goods

Upon entry, Bolund will be in the process of leaving (see [bugs](#Bugs)). The counter is to the right of the entrance and contains several items. Against the southwest wall is a set of shelves and a cupboard, both of which are filled with food, beverages, and [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). A food barrel is in the west corner, and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") is under the counter. Against the southeast wall is a dresser with a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and three [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on top. A ceiling rack containing three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, and two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") hangs above the dresser.

Opposite the door on the southeast wall is a fireplace with four [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from a rack to the left. Further to the left is a food barrel and a set of shelves containing an iron mace. There is a flight of stairs leading up to the living quarters against the northeast wall with several barrels, a pile of firewood, and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot underneath.

At the top of the stairs is a long wooden table against the southeast wall. On the table are several pieces of cheese, two pieces of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat"), three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and three [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). To the right is a set of shelves holding only clutter. Coming out from the southwest wall are two owned single beds with a round table between them and an unlocked chest to the left. On the table are two bottles of alto wine and five [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). In the northern corner above the stairs are several sacks of foodstuffs and a couple of barrels. A door leading out onto the balcony is located in the middle of the northwest wall.

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store. They can be purchased from the merchant or stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days.

- Arrows: 3 Iron Arrow
- Clutter: 2 [Wooden Bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Wooden_Bowl "Skyrim:Wooden Bowl")
- Food: 2 Alto Wine, 3 Bread, 1 [Cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), 3 [Eidar Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), 3 [Goat Cheese Wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), 6 [Potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), 3 [Wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine")
- Potions: 2 [Potion of Minor Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), 1 [Potion of Minor Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), 1 [Potion of Regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), 1 [Potion of Resist Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire")
- Weapons: 1 [Iron Dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), 1 Iron Mace, 1 [Iron Sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), 1 Steel Sword

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Gray Pine Goods' [Merchant Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") every two days.

## Bugs

- Bolund will only exit Gray Pine Goods if you enter the store, and therefore will not be found at the mill when entering Falkreath.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Graywinter Watch

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Graywinter Watch ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Graywinter+Watch)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Froki's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Froki's Bow") *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| GraywinterWatchExterior, GraywinterWatch01 | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | |
| Location | |
| East of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") South of [Shimmermist Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Shimmermist_Cave "Skyrim:Shimmermist Cave") | |

Graywinter Watch

**Graywinter Watch** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). It contains only one zone, *[Graywinter Watch](#Graywinter_Watch)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

### Exterior

The cave, which is beneath the [Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") overlooking the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), is easily reachable from the nearby road. Along the west side of the Ritual Stone's rock foundation is a dirt path which leads directly to the cave.

### Graywinter Watch

Froki's Bow, with a nearby dead bandit

There are two [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") in the cave; one is visible from the tunnel, and the other is hidden near the campfire. Six [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), three [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), and four [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungi grow throughout the cave. To the right of the entrance is a ramp to the higher part of the cave.

At the top of the ramp is a row of nine skulls. There is a small campsite here, with a central campfire and the corpses of a [female Nord bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#Nord_Female "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") and a [male Nord bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#Nord_Male "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)"). There are two bedrolls on one side of the fire, and a tent on the other. To the right of the tent is a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")*, three [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), a pile or quiver of random [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), and the respawning [Froki's bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Froki's Bow") atop a food barrel. Lastly, by the bedrolls is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack").

## Notes

- There are fifteen humanoid skulls in the cave, though only twelve can be lifted.
- Two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") are north of the cave, across the river next to a rocky outcropping and a tree.
- With version 1.3.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), Froki's Bow will only spawn here once.

# Skyrim:Great Lift at Alftand

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Dwemer.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Dwemer.png) | Dwarven Ruin: Great Lift at Alftand ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Alftand)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BlackreachElevatorAlftand, BlackreachQuickExitAlftand | |
| Regions | |
| [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") | |
| Location | |
| Northeast of [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") Southeast of [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass") | |

The Alftand Lift to Blackreach

The **Great Lift at Alftand** is a Dwarven lift to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") located northeast of [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") and southeast of [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass"). It is a mechanical lift which can only be entered and used after starting the quest [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane"). Inside the lift building is a lever which, when activated, will bring you up from or take you down into Blackreach. The lift will open a short distance south-southeast of the exit from [Alftand Cathedral](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand#Alftand_Cathedral "Skyrim:Alftand") inside Blackreach. The topside of the lift is housed in a building surrounded by metal barriers, one of which is a gate. The gate can only be opened from within, by pulling a lever to the right of the gate, after which the lift can be entered from [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") whenever you travel there (fast traveling places you right outside the lift). The map marker for this location does not appear until the lift is activated inside Blackreach.

The lift is Dwemer in origin, and is one of seven entrances to Blackreach, which must first be entered by traversing the ruins of [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"), [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"), or [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") and using the [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") from [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus") to open a door to Blackreach.

## Related Quests

- **[Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane")**: Uncover the secrets of the mysterious Dwemer lockbox.

### Exterior

The lift is in a fairly isolated location, east of the path between [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") and [Wayward Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Wayward_Pass "Skyrim:Wayward Pass"). The lift is on the edge of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)"), but overlooks [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") with its stunning landscape. The inn can be seen to the southwest. To the northwest you may encounter leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"), [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), or [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter"), often battling each other.

### Great Lift at Alftand

In [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), the lift is south-southeast of the exit from Alftand Cathedral and southeast of [Sinderion's Field Laboratory](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinderion%27s_Field_Laboratory "Skyrim:Sinderion's Field Laboratory"). Before using this lift to enter Blackreach, you must first lower spears blocking access to the lift in Blackreach by activating a button on a sculpted metal head in front. You may then ride the lift up and use a lever to open a gate in Skyrim. There are two [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") plants nearby: one is at the base of the stairs, and the other is around the side of the structure to the right when facing the lift. A [falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and a [chaurus cocoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") containing a [chaurus hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") are a short distance north of the lift, between the lift and the exit from Alftand Cathedral.

## Bugs

- A bug may occur when the great lifts are accessed to or from Blackreach. When the character reappears in Skyrim or in Blackreach, the game autosaves, then the screen goes blank/black, reappears a few seconds later, and then goes blank/black again. This continues to occur indefinitely; attempts to move/run/sprint or use Whirlwind Sprint only result in the character reappearing at the original place of arrival during intervals when the game screen reappears.
  - Opening the menu or favorites screen and leaving the screen open for 15 - 30 seconds stops the bug.
- Sometimes after activating the lift from Blackreach, you are positioned outside the lift building on the surface, preventing you from opening the door from within the building. This bug may also be triggered if you have too many followers from unfinished quests and/or summoned followers, such that you are pushed outside the lift building on the surface in order to make room for the followers.
  - If this happens, load the previous save, then have your dog and regular follower (if any) wait for you in Blackreach outside the lift area before activating the lift. You may then use the lift and open the gate from within the lift building once you reach the surface.

# Skyrim:Great Lift at Mzinchaleft

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Dwemer.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Dwemer.png) | Dwarven Ruin: Great Lift at Mzinchaleft ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Mzinchaleft)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BlackreachElevatorMzinchaleft, BlackreachQuickExitMzinchaleft | |
| Regions | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch"), [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") | |
| Location | |
| South of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") | |

The Great Lift at Mzinchaleft

The **Great Lift at Mzinchaleft** is a Dwarven lift to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") located south of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"). It is a mechanical lift which can only be entered and used after starting the quest [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane"). Inside the lift building is a lever which, when activated, will bring you up from or take you down into Blackreach. The lift will open a short distance southeast of the exit from [Mzinchaleft Gatehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft#Mzinchaleft_Gatehouse "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") inside Blackreach. The topside of the lift is housed in a building surrounded by metal barriers, one of which is a gate. The gate can only be opened from within, by pulling a lever to the right of the gate, after which the lift can be entered from [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") whenever you travel there (fast traveling places you right outside the lift). The map marker for this location does not appear until the lift is activated inside Blackreach.

The lift is Dwemer in origin, and is one of seven entrances to Blackreach, which must first be entered by traversing the ruins of [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"), [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"), or [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") and using the [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") from [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus") to open a door to Blackreach.

## Related Quests

- **[Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane")**: Uncover the secrets of the mysterious Dwemer lockbox.

### Exterior

The lift is in a tower just off the road between [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), a short distance down the road from the lift that provides a shortcut exit from the ruins of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") itself. There is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") a few paces northwest of the entrance, and a [frost troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") may be found wandering the forest nearby. Southwest of the lift, along the road to [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), the player will come across a battle between a group of [conjurers](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjurer "Skyrim:Conjurer") driving a horse-drawn wagon and a group of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). The wagon contains a crate holding a selection of [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a basket holding several [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), two satchels containing more ingredients, and a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v6 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v6")*.

### Great Lift at Mzinchaleft

In [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), the lift is southeast of the exit from Mzinchaleft Gatehouse and northwest of the [Hall of Rumination](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Rumination "Skyrim:Hall of Rumination"). Before using this lift to enter Blackreach, you must first lower spears blocking access to the lift in Blackreach by activating a button on a sculpted metal head in front. You may then ride the lift up and use a lever to open a gate in Skyrim. Similar to the lift entrance on the surface, there is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") a few paces northwest of the Blackreach entrance. On the road to the southeast, a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") patrols the road over an underpass, under which is a chest and a [Dwarven centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") in a docking station.

## Bugs

- A bug may occur when the great lifts are accessed to or from Blackreach. When the character reappears in Skyrim or in Blackreach, the game autosaves, then the screen goes blank/black, reappears a few seconds later, and then goes blank/black again. This continues to occur indefinitely; attempts to move/run/sprint or use Whirlwind Sprint only result in the character reappearing at the original place of arrival during intervals when the game screen reappears.
  - Opening the menu or favorites screen and leaving the screen open for 15 - 30 seconds stops the bug.
- Sometimes after activating the lift from Blackreach, you are positioned outside the lift building on the surface, preventing you from opening the door from within the building. This bug may also be triggered if you have too many followers from unfinished quests and/or summoned followers, such that you are pushed outside the lift building on the surface in order to make room for the followers.
  - If this happens, load the previous save, then have your dog and regular follower (if any) wait for you in Blackreach outside the lift area before activating the lift. You may then use the lift and open the gate from within the lift building once you reach the surface.
