# Skyrim:Great Lift at Raldbthar

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Dwemer.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Dwemer.png) | Dwarven Ruin: Great Lift at Raldbthar ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Great+Lift+at+Raldbthar)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BlackreachElevatorRaldbthar, RaldbtharExterior01 | |
| Regions | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"), [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") | |
| Location | |
| West-southwest of [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill") East of [Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand") | |

The Raldbthar Lift ready for use

The **Great Lift at Raldbthar** is a Dwarven lift to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") located west-southwest of [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill") and east of [Irkngthand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand "Skyrim:Irkngthand"). It is a mechanical lift which can only be entered and used after starting the quest [Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane"). Inside the lift building is a lever which, when activated, will bring you up from or take you down into Blackreach. The lift will open a short distance north-northeast of the [Derelict Pumphouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Derelict_Pumphouse "Skyrim:Derelict Pumphouse") inside Blackreach. The topside of the lift is housed in a building surrounded by metal barriers, one of which is a gate. The gate can only be opened from within, by pulling a lever to the right of the gate, after which the lift can be entered from [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") whenever you travel there (fast traveling places you right outside the lift). The map marker for this location does not appear until the lift is activated inside Blackreach.

The lift is Dwemer in origin, and is one of seven entrances to Blackreach, which must first be entered by traversing the ruins of [Alftand](/wiki/Skyrim:Alftand "Skyrim:Alftand"), [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"), or [Raldbthar](/wiki/Skyrim:Raldbthar "Skyrim:Raldbthar") and using the [Attunement Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere") from [Septimus Signus](/wiki/Skyrim:Septimus_Signus "Skyrim:Septimus Signus") to open a door to Blackreach.

## Related Quests

- **[Discerning the Transmundane](/wiki/Skyrim:Discerning_the_Transmundane "Skyrim:Discerning the Transmundane")**: Uncover the secrets of the mysterious Dwemer lockbox.

### Exterior

The lift is the first building passed when following the path that starts near the [Pale Stormcloak camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp") on [Lake Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Yorgrim "Skyrim:Lake Yorgrim") south up to the main entrance to Raldbthar. It is found above the snowline.

### Great Lift at Raldbthar

In [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach"), the lift is north-northeast of the [Derelict Pumphouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Derelict_Pumphouse "Skyrim:Derelict Pumphouse"), at the same level as the top of the lift in the Pumphouse, on the shore of a large pool. Before using this lift to enter Blackreach, you must first lower spears blocking access to the lift in Blackreach by activating a button on a sculpted metal head in front. You may then ride the lift up and use a lever to open a gate in Skyrim.

## Bugs

- Despite not being clearable, and having no associated dungeon, the map may still show this location as "Cleared".
- A bug may occur when the great lifts are accessed to or from Blackreach. When the character reappears in Skyrim or in Blackreach, the game autosaves, then the screen goes blank/black, reappears a few seconds later, and then goes blank/black again. This continues to occur indefinitely; attempts to move/run/sprint or use Whirlwind Sprint only result in the character reappearing at the original place of arrival during intervals when the game screen reappears.
  - Opening the menu or favorites screen and leaving the screen open for 15 - 30 seconds stops the bug.
- Sometimes after activating the lift from Blackreach, you are positioned outside the lift building on the surface, preventing you from opening the door from within the building. This bug may also be triggered if you have too many followers from unfinished quests and/or summoned followers, such that you are pushed outside the lift building on the surface in order to make room for the followers.
  - If this happens, load the previous save, then have your dog and regular follower (if any) wait for you in Blackreach outside the lift area before activating the lift. You may then use the lift and open the gate from within the lift building once you reach the surface.

# Skyrim:Greathall

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Greathall ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Greathall)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2SVGreathall | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Greathall

The **Greathall** is the home of chief [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice") and [Tharstan](/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan "Skyrim:Tharstan") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

It is on the east side of the village, north of the [Shaman's Hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Shaman%27s_Hut "Skyrim:Shaman's Hut").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Fanari Strong-Voice](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice")  [Tharstan](/wiki/Skyrim:Tharstan "Skyrim:Tharstan") |

### Exterior

The building has two entrances, with the front entrance to the west and the back entrance to the east. To the left of the front entrance is a lit brazier and a [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"). To the right of the front entrance is another lit brazier. The entrances are unlocked.

### Greathall

Greathall interior

The front entrance leads into a large hall with balconies around the western half of the room. Stairs are against the northern and southern walls. There is a large fire pit in the center of the room with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") on the south side. Around the fire pit are three pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), a pot of [honey](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey "Skyrim:Honey"), a stand containing three fillets of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat"), an open crate containing a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a cast iron pot, which contains two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), next to a chair.

Against the eastern wall is an open display case containing two [horker tusks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). In front of this, next to a pillar, is a basket containing three [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") samples. To the right of the display case, in the southeast corner, is a crate. Against the southern wall between the crate and stairs is a set of shelves containing an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), an [ash yam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"), a sack and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). Under the southern stairs are two crates, a mead barrel, three sacks and a chair. In front of this are two lit braziers with a wood pile and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). To the right of the lit braziers, hanging under the balcony, are two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"). Also against the southern wall is a barrel with a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide") beside it.

Back door

In the southwest corner, against the western wall is a set of shelves containing a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), three [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), two bottles of alto wine and a goat cheese wheel. There is a second entrance in the middle of this wall. Farther to the right is a small set of shelves containing two potatoes, a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"), a [snow fox pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Fox Pelt") and a metal bowl, which contains three [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore") samples. In the northwestern corner is an open display case containing two animal skulls.

Against the northern wall is a desk with copies of *[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(book) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (book)")*, *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")*, *[Children of the All-Maker](/wiki/Skyrim:Children_of_the_All-Maker "Skyrim:Children of the All-Maker")*, *[Fall of the Snow Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Fall_of_the_Snow_Prince "Skyrim:Fall of the Snow Prince")*, *[Ghosts in the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_in_the_Storm "Skyrim:Ghosts in the Storm")*, *[Last King of the Ayleids](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_King_of_the_Ayleids "Skyrim:Last King of the Ayleids")*, *[The Guardian and the Traitor](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Guardian_and_the_Traitor "Skyrim:The Guardian and the Traitor")*, *[The Song of Pelinal, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v3 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v3")*, *[The Real Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v3")*, *[Ahzidal's Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Descent "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Descent")*, a [roll of paper](/wiki/Skyrim:Roll_of_Paper "Skyrim:Roll of Paper"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and two bottles, one of alto wine and the other [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine").

To the right of the desk is an end table. Farther to the right, under the northern stairs, are two barrels, a crate and a sack. In front of these are two more lit braziers with a crate and three sacks in between. To the left of the lit braziers, hanging under the balcony, are two samples of elves ear, a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a pheasant. Still against the northern wall, between the stairs and the corner, is a small round table and two chairs. On the table is a wooden plate holding a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"). In the northeast corner is a set of shelves containing a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt"), an [empty bottle of wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"), a leather strip and an open crate containing three pieces of [leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather "Skyrim:Leather"). To the right of this is a barrel with a large piece of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal") on the ground beside it. Next to a pillar in front of the western entrance is a crate, with a basket containing five large pieces of charcoal in, and two more around, it. Towards the middle of the room between both sets of lit braziers is a long table with benches either side, on the table is a mead barrel and a cast iron pot containing a salmon steak and some [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks").

Boudoir

Climbing the northern stairs you come to the sleeping area for Fanari Strong-Voice. In front of you, in the northwest corner, is a barrel and a long end table with a horker tusk and sack. A crate and second sack is in front. To the left of the end table is a wardrobe, followed by a small end table with a sample of frost mirriam on top. To the left of this is a double bed and then another end table with a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") on top. Under the left-hand side of the bed is a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). Farther to the left is an empty chest. In the southwestern corner is a dresser with a [Sabre Cat snow pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Snow_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Snow Pelt"). There is a set of shelves against the southern wall that contain two sacks. At the front of the balcony from left to right is a dresser with an apprentice-locked display case on top. Inside the cabinet are three [pearls](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl "Skyrim:Pearl") and three [small pearls](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Pearl "Skyrim:Small Pearl"). Next is a bench and finally a crate with a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") on it.

# Skyrim:Greatsword for a Great Man

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Adrianne asks you to deliver a sword to [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), her father.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Adrianne Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adrianne_Avenicci "Skyrim:Adrianne Avenicci") |
| Location(s): | [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's") in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") |
| Reward: | 20 gold pieces |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 ([Adrianne Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adrianne_Avenicci "Skyrim:Adrianne Avenicci")) 0→1 ([Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci")) |
| ID: | FreeformWhiterunQuest03 |

Balgruuf's Greatsword

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Adrianne Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adrianne_Avenicci "Skyrim:Adrianne Avenicci").
2. Go to [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").
3. Talk to [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci").

## Detailed Walkthrough

| Balgruuf's Greatsword | | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| ID | Type | [Damage](/wiki/File:SkyrimTAG-icon-Heavy_Attack.png "Damage") | [Weight](/wiki/File:SR-icon-clothing-Leather_Backpack_(square).png "Weight") | [Value](/wiki/File:SR-item-Gold-heads.png "Value") |
| 000946fc | 2 Hand Greatsword | 17 | 17 | 200 |

### A Warmaiden's Gift

[Adrianne Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Adrianne_Avenicci "Skyrim:Adrianne Avenicci") is a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") who owns the smithy and weapons shop, [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's"), in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). When asked if she works her forge all day, Adrianne will admit that she does, and that she recently forged a greatsword for [Jarl Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") in an attempt to impress him. However, she can't seem to find an opportunity to deliver it. She would like for the sword to be delivered to her father, [Proventus Avenicci](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci"), the [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") of [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach") in Whiterun.

### Delivering the Sword

Proventus is generally found in the main chamber of Dragonsreach, beside the throne. Deliver the sword to him, telling him that it is from his daughter. He will remark, *"From Adrianne? Ah, this must be that weapon for the Jarl. Poor girl, so eager to prove herself. I'll present it to Balgruuf when his mood is... agreeable."* He will then reward you with twenty gold.

## Notes

- If you sided with the Stormcloaks in the Civil War and have completed [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)"), Proventus will be in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace")'s basement along with Balgruuf and Irileth. The quest is otherwise the same as if you had joined the Imperials.
- As a quest item, the sword has zero weight. It can be tempered, but not enchanted, making it a potentially useful item to hold onto early in the game.

## Bugs

- If you place Balgruuf's Greatsword on a weapon rack or plaque, the quest can still be completed by talking to Proventus, and the sword will disappear from the rack/plaque. However, the slot the sword occupied can never be used again.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- Proventus Avenicci equips the greatsword that was intended to be for Balgruuf.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. It will now simply be taken from you instead and placed in a display case in Balgruuf's quarters as was implied.

## Quest Stages

| Greatsword for a Great Man (FreeformWhiterunQuest03) | | |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 255, 300.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformWhiterunQuest03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformWhiterunQuest03`.

# Skyrim:Greenspring Hollow

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Grove.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Grove.png) | Grove: Greenspring Hollow ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Greenspring+Hollow)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| GreenSpringHollowExterior01 | |
| Region | |
| [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | |
| Location | |
| West-northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") Southwest of [Hamvir's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hamvir%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hamvir's Rest") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 1 |

Greenspring Hollow

**Greenspring Hollow** is a shallow outdoor cave west-northwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") containing a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals").

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights")**: Discover the writings of Shalidor and benefit from his wisdom. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

As you approach the outcropping, a single predator will likely attack you. Once it is dealt with, you can safely search the creature's den. It appears a foolish [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") decided to camp here and paid with his life. His body lies on the blood-splattered ground next to a fallen cooking spit. Some lootable skeletal remains are farther back next to two unusable bedrolls and a level-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). A copy of the *[Argonian Account, Book 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Account,_Book_2 "Skyrim:Argonian Account, Book 2")* rests on a boulder beside the chest, with a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") next to it.

The hunter's lean-to on the right side of the outcropping shelters a total of ten [pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Hides#Unprocessed "Skyrim:Animal Hides") of various animals. An [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") are near the lean-to. On the left side of the outcropping is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning"). A [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a piece of [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat"), and some [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") hang from the ceiling on a rope. Two clusters of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), and a [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") grow around the camp.

Follow the nearby stream south to find a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") and a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") near the river. You may encounter a few more predators in the area as well.

## Notes

- Only the level-locked chest, skeletal remains, and apothecary's satchel respawn. All other items, including the hunter's body, only appear on your first visit. Therefore, any radiant quest that requires recovering an item from this location can be completed even after it has been cleared.

## Bugs

- The animal does not respawn, which makes it impossible to complete the quest [Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)") if [Aela](/wiki/Skyrim:Aela "Skyrim:Aela") asks you to clear this location after it had been previously cleared.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Greywater Grotto

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Greywater Grotto ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Greywater+Grotto)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") | |

| Location | |
| East of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") South of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 1 |

| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 1 |

Greywater Grotto

**Greywater Grotto** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). It contains only one zone, *[Greywater Grotto](#Greywater_Grotto)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

There is a leveled animal guarding the entrance, which is covered in splattered blood and gore, with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") lying on the ground among it. There are also a number of [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes in the vicinity and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") above the entrance, accessed by heading west then ascending back to the east.

### Greywater Grotto

The cave is a long descending corridor following a stream down to a shallow pool. The animals in the cave are leveled, and seem to be entirely random. You are as likely to encounter [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf") as you are to encounter [snowy sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowy_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Snowy Sabre Cat"), [snow bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear "Skyrim:Snow Bear"), or [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), depending on your level. The cave itself is entirely natural in appearance, and descends in a series of plateaus with earthen ramps linking them.

Upon entering, there is a dead [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") in front on a ledge, with a ramp down to the left and an iron ore vein beneath it. Partway down, there is a wellspring that has formed a partially frozen pool that feeds a stream flowing to the south, with a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") to the north. To the right, the ground rises, with a couple more animals found at the point before the cave continues to descend, passing a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead) "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") near the west wall. A short way farther south, the stream forms a waterfall, with the path becoming a ledge along the west wall. Near the bottom, the path crosses below the waterfall as a bridge over another partially frozen pool. Three more animals are found at the bottom next to an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), with a second dead bandit and a medium coin purse on the ground among more human debris. There is a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") against the south wall of the cave. There are no plants or fungi anywhere inside the cave.

## Notes

- Whenever there are different animals present, it is possible you will only find the victors of any fights alive and the carcasses of the losers.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

# Skyrim:Grimsever's Return

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Recover [Mjoll](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness")'s beloved sword, [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever"), from [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Mjoll the Lioness](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness") |
| Location(s): | [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft") |
| Reward: | Mjoll the Lioness as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Mjoll the Lioness](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness")) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften09 |
| Required Level: | 14 |
| Suggested Level: | 16 |

Mjoll's sword and shield resting on a blood-stained stone table

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Mjoll the Lioness](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").
2. Find [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever") in the Dwemer ruins of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft").
3. Return to Mjoll.

### Mjoll the Lioness

[Mjoll the Lioness](/wiki/Skyrim:Mjoll_the_Lioness "Skyrim:Mjoll the Lioness") lives in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") where she spends her time speaking out against the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") and talking to her faithful follower [Aerin](/wiki/Skyrim:Aerin "Skyrim:Aerin") about the evils in the world. Acting on her convictions, she has taken on the responsibility of patrolling the town, which she does every day; from 9am she can be found in the Market, at noon she will be inside [The Bee and Barb](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bee_and_Barb "Skyrim:The Bee and Barb"), and from 6pm she patrols the streets of Riften until midnight. Once you reach level 14, however, Mjoll will have more on her mind than just the Thieves Guild. In her younger days, she traveled and adventured all over [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") but lost her favorite blade [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever") when she ventured into the ancient [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer") ruin of [Mzinchaleft](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft"). The dangers of the ruin nearly took her life as well, so she retired from adventuring and settled down in Riften. She admits that she feels defenseless without her blade and has a hard time finding a replacement. You can then offer to help her and, while she will refer to it as a 'fool's errand', she will also let you undertake the task, adding a map marker for Mzinchaleft.

### Mzinchaleft

Mzinchaleft

Mzinchaleft is a large Dwemer ruin located in the snowy tundra east of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"), northwest of the [Hall of the Vigilant](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Vigilant "Skyrim:Hall of the Vigilant"). [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") now inhabit the first zones of the ruin and you will encounter up to six of them guarding the entrance. Fight them, locate the door and prepare for a very long dungeon crawl. Once inside, head down the first two slopes and fight the two bandits residing near the campfire. Proceed through the tunnels until you reach a room with two bandits and a cauldron. Dispose of them and claim some minor loot from the chest. At the intersection, kill the bandit and claim [Maluril's Room Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril%27s_Room_Key "Skyrim:Maluril's Room Key") from his body, then use it to unlock the gate. During the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") quest [Kill Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Maluril "Skyrim:Kill Maluril"), the quarters behind the door will be occupied by [Maluril](/wiki/Skyrim:Maluril "Skyrim:Maluril") but, during this quest you will find them empty. Read through the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill book *[A Dance in Fire, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v7 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v7")* then backtrack to the intersection and proceed in a southern direction. In the next chamber you will witness two [Dwarven spheres](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere") dispose of some bandits before coming after you. Fight them all and keep heading south, following the path as it twists and turns, and disposing of the various automatons along the way.

Before long, you will reach an area with a handle and two gates, and several more handles behind the gates. Pull the only available handle and the gate to the east will open. Pull the new handle and the gate to the south will open. Pull the new handle and backtrack to the previous handle and pull it again. Go into a newly opened chamber to the south and pull the handle. Head south yet again and pull the handle, then backtrack to the previous handle and pull it again. Return to the very first handle and pull it. This opens the two gates to the southeast, giving you access to a valve. You'll find an unlocked chest and a master-locked chest in the room with the valve. Activate the valve and the path will now be clear and provide access to the next zone, [Mzinchaleft Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft_Depths "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft Depths").

### The Depths

When the elevator brings you down into the Mzinchaleft Depths, the first thing you will notice is a dead [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and the recognizable sound of a [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") on the other side of the locked door. The door hides a very large multi-leveled chamber filled with Falmer enemies and plenty of secret areas, so make sure to raid every corner before leaving through the door to the east. Two Falmer enemies wait in the next chamber, so dispose of them and proceed forward, into a tunnel-like system with more Falmer. Watch out for a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Tripwire "Skyrim:Traps") triggering a [claw trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Claw "Skyrim:Traps") as you enter the next room and fight even more Falmer and a chaurus. The tents contain minor loot and a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead)#Orc_Male "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)"). Find the tunnel to the north and open a gate to another huge chamber with a fountain in the middle. Fight the inevitable Falmer enemies and head up the bridge to the north. At the top, fight another Falmer and locate the button and activate it. This will open the path in the southwestern part of the chamber. More Falmer wait on the other side, including a boss, so finish them off and head up the stairs to the north and the entrance to the third and final zone, [Mzinchaleft Gatehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Mzinchaleft_Gatehouse "Skyrim:Mzinchaleft Gatehouse").

### Grimsever

In the Gatehouse, you will only have to go around the corner before you will encounter the [Dwarven Centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion") that nearly killed Mjoll the Lioness back in the day. It will attack right away and will be accompanied by a [Dwarven Sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Sphere "Skyrim:Dwarven Sphere"). After the battle, locate [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever"), which is lying on a table. Find the boss-leveled chest behind bars to the north and pull the nearby handle to gain access. Lastly, if you have the [attunement sphere](/wiki/Skyrim:Attunement_Sphere "Skyrim:Attunement Sphere"), you can gain access to [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") from here. When all is said and done, open the western door and activate the handle to be brought back outside, emerging from an alternate entrance west of the main entrance.

Back in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") you will find Mjoll patrolling [as usual](#Mjoll_the_Lioness). When you hand her the blade, she will be overly impressed: *"Astonishing. To think you actually were able to reach it and yet return to tell the tale. Rarely in my travels have I encountered those who possess skills equal to your own. I see I still have much to learn. If you'd permit me, I'd be honored to accompany you in your travels for a time."* Alternatively, if you told her of your hopes to join the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"), she will instead say: *"When you told me of your intent to join the Thieves Guild, I honestly didn't think we'd have much to speak about ever again. Yet here you are with my weapon that you could have easily sold or kept for yourself. Forgive me for my hasty opinion of you, I see that I was wrong and that there's much I can learn from you. If you'd permit me, I'd be honored to accompany you in your travels for a time."* Either way, she will then be available as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") and a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

## Notes

- [Grimsever](/wiki/Skyrim:Grimsever "Skyrim:Grimsever") can be found within Mzinchaleft before acquiring the related quest from Mjoll. This will open the quest dialogue with her. Level 14 is required for the sword to spawn however.
- Grimsever is a one-handed Glass Sword though Mjoll is more proficient in two-handed weapons.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.3, addresses this issue. Grimsever is now a Glass Greatsword to match her skills better.
- After completing the quest, Mjoll will be available as a follower, at which point you can "trade" inventory with her and take Grimsever back. Any smithing upgrades made to Grimsever before giving it back to Mjoll will be lost, though you can upgrade it again.
- If you are already level 14 or above when you first interact with Mjoll, you must also gain another level after your initial conversation and return to her before the dialogue option to begin this quest becomes available.
- The boss fight presents a considerable challenge for a level 14 character, but you don't actually have to defeat the Centurion to get Grimsever. You can make a run for it, pick up the sword on the fly and head straight for the exit.
- You will need to level up via skill increases to or beyond level 9 for the quest to be eligible to start. You cannot be console-commanded to an arbitrarily high level and start the quest.

## Bugs

- Mjoll might not give you the quest to retrieve Grimsever despite fulfilling the above criteria, and Grimsever may not appear in the Mzinchaleft Gatehouse as stated above.

:   -  You may use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to make her your friend with `player.setrelationshiprank 00019DF7 4`, allowing you to recruit her as a follower. After using her as a follower for a few days, she may give you the quest, and Grimsever should spawn.
    -  You can use the console code  `player.additem 00053379 1` to give yourself the sword, then talk with her and give it to her. This may result in two copies of Grimsever being present in the game.
    -  An internal conflict with the first scripted conversation between Mjoll and Aerin about "another run-in with the Thieves Guild" upon entering Riften means that you must level up -after- the scripted conversation has occurred (to level 14 or later) before Mjoll will offer the Grimsever quest.

## Quest Stages

| Grimsever's Return (FreeformRiften09) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Locate Grimsever |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return to Mjoll |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften09 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften09`.

# Skyrim:Grin and Bear It

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Give ten [bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt") to [Temba Wide-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Temba_Wide-Arm "Skyrim:Temba Wide-Arm").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Temba Wide-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Temba_Wide-Arm "Skyrim:Temba Wide-Arm") |
| Location(s): | [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") |
| Reward: | Random leveled enchanted war axe |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Temba Wide-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Temba_Wide-Arm "Skyrim:Temba Wide-Arm")) |
| ID: | FreeformIvarstead03 |

I need those pelts...

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Temba Wide-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Temba_Wide-Arm "Skyrim:Temba Wide-Arm").
2. Acquire ten [bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt").
3. Return to Temba Wide-Arm.

### Damn Bears

[Temba Wide-Arm](/wiki/Skyrim:Temba_Wide-Arm "Skyrim:Temba Wide-Arm") really does not like [bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear"). She is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") woman who has sunk all of her money into a mill in [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). Even in passing you will hear her complaining to anyone within earshot how the bears are running her business into the ground. If you stop to chat she will explain that bears are ruining the trees by scratching up the trunks, rendering them useless as lumber. She is sorely in need of help with the bear problem and offers payment if you bring her ten bear pelts, thus thinning out the bear population.

### Filling the Order

Temba will accept any combination of [bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt"), [cave bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt"), or [snow bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Bear Pelt"); it doesn't matter to her as long as they are ursidae.

There are two bear dens in the vicinity of Ivarstead: [Honeystrand Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeystrand_Cave "Skyrim:Honeystrand Cave") to the south past the river, and [Pinepeak Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinepeak_Cavern "Skyrim:Pinepeak Cavern") to the north near the steps leading up to [High Hrothgar](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Hrothgar "Skyrim:High Hrothgar"). There are also a number of bear pelts in [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto"), a cave north of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [Giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") frequently carry bear pelts, and you can also buy bear pelts from general goods [merchants](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Skyrim:Merchants"), [Khajiit caravans](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant#Khajiit_Traders "Skyrim:Merchant"), and [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") in the wild.

Once you bring the ten pelts to her she will be surprised that you came through for her and will reward you with a random leveled enchanted war axe.

## Bugs

- If you are carrying more than ten bear pelts, she will take them all, and it seems you cannot pickpocket them back.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
- You can get the quest reward and keep the pelts by putting the bear pelts in a container immediately after you tell her that you got the pelts. Be warned however, that doing this will cause the quest to be stuck in your journal indefinitely.

## Quest Stages

| Grin and Bear It (FreeformIvarstead03) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *(Only displayed if you don't already have 10 bear pelts)* *Objective 10:* Gather 10 bear pelts for Temba Wide-Arms *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* (<Global=FFI03BearCount>/10) |
|  |  | *(Displayed when you have the bear pelts)* *Objective 20:* Return to Temba Wide-Arms *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformIvarstead03 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformIvarstead03`.

# Skyrim:Gromm's Pass

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Gromm's Pass ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gromm%27s+Pass+%28CC%29)) | | |

| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |

Gromm's Pass

**Gromm's Pass** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") located in [the Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), south of [Forelhost](/wiki/Skyrim:Forelhost "Skyrim:Forelhost"). Until a recent collapse, it served as an underground pass through the [Jerall Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Jerall_Mountains "Skyrim:Jerall Mountains") to [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil").

It consists of one zone: [Gromm's Pass](#Gromm.27s_Pass).

## Related Quests

- **[Blue in the Face](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_in_the_Face "Skyrim:Blue in the Face")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins"): Investigate rumors of the Blue God's return.

### Exterior

The cave entrance is marked by a lit brazier among the bones and blood. A [bear](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear "Skyrim:Bear") spawns right where the fast travel marker is, so be prepared for an ambush if you aren't approaching on foot. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") can be found to the right of the entrance.

### Gromm's Pass

Gromm's Pass interior

Gogh next to the throne

Not far from the entrance are two goblins guarding, on ground are seven dead skeletons. Head north and see the dead [Avanessa Calladius](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanessa_Calladius "Skyrim:Avanessa Calladius"), nearby are six dead skeletons. Head west there's another dead skeleton on ground, and a goblin guarding the north west corridor. Head west and find a large room with a pit at center, in the pit [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh") is fighting against three goblins. West of the pit are two kneeled goblins worshipping a leader named [Blue God](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_God "Skyrim:Blue God"), the Blue God carries a unique staff [Goblin Totem Staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves#Goblin_Totem_Staff "Skyrim:Staves")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblins "Skyrim:Goblins"). There're several dead corpses in the large room and in the pit. Head west is a small room containing a boss chest. Head north and walk into a small room stocked plenty of [Steel-Blue Entolomas](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel-Blue_Entoloma "Skyrim:Steel-Blue Entoloma"). North of the large room mentioned before is a corridor, north of the corridor is a small mining room, a goblin is face away to the player and mining. South of the corridor leads to a way blocked by spears and a chain, pull the chain to lower the spears and reach to pit in the large room mentioned before, [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh") is in the pit and can be talked with to release him as a fighting type pet.

## Notes

- This cave is the only place where [Steel-Blue Entoloma](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel-Blue_Entoloma "Skyrim:Steel-Blue Entoloma") grow naturally.
- If [Gogh](/wiki/Skyrim:Gogh "Skyrim:Gogh") leaves your service as a [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers"), he will return to the throne room here.
- A Nord named [Gromm](/wiki/Oblivion:Gromm "Oblivion:Gromm") appears in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*.

# Skyrim:Guard Barracks (Gate)

## Overview

.jpg)

The barracks by the gate in Whiterun

**Guard Barracks** is a building near the main gate in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It is located across the street from [Warmaiden's](/wiki/Skyrim:Warmaiden%27s "Skyrim:Warmaiden's").

It is used by [Whiterun Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") as an alternative to the bigger, and similar named [barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks "Skyrim:Guard Barracks") behind the [Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Commander Caius](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Caius "Skyrim:Commander Caius")  [Whiterun Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") |

## Guard Barracks

.jpg)

Guard Barracks interior

The barracks consists of two cramped rooms, a dining room often used by a single [guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard"), and a sleeping area with four owned beds. The dining room contains two chairs by a table, a minor loot chest, a food barrel, and four food sacks. The small table seats two and has some food on display, two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). A set of shelves contains a chunk of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"), the loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), and [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese").

The sleeping area contains four beds squeezed head-to-toe between the north and south walls with an end table with clutter between them. The end table to the east has a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and two [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") on top and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") on the floor below. A copy of *[Beggar Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_Prince "Skyrim:Beggar Prince")* is carelessly thrown on the floor in the northeastern corner. The shelves along the northern wall hold two bottles of wine, two bottles of ale, and a head of [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). The cupboard under the shelves holds clutter. Under the cupboard sits a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") and, placed on a stool, a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat").

## Notes

- There is a  "Danger") Danger [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") around the right corner from the door and double marked low down on the wall and a wooden support.
- If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") takes over Whiterun during [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)"), nobody will live in the barracks and all items will be free to take.
- There are four food barrels on the roof of the barracks.

# Skyrim:Guard Barracks

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

This article is about the main barracks. For the barracks by the gate, see [Guard Barracks (Gate)](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks_(Gate) "Skyrim:Guard Barracks (Gate)").

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Barracks: Guard Barracks ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guard+Barracks)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |

| Location | |
| Plains District of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") | |

Guard's Barracks exterior

The **Guard Barracks** is a building in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") where guards live when not on duty. It is located behind [the Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare") in the Plains District.

It is the main barracks of Whiterun and it consists of only one area, *[Guard Barracks](#Guard_Barracks)*. There is another [barracks](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Barracks_(Gate) "Skyrim:Guard Barracks (Gate)") by the main gate to the city, for use by the guards who guard the gate.

The building itself is quite hard to spot for the casual user of Whiterun's services. The path to the building starts between the Bannered Mare and [Arcadia's Cauldron](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcadia%27s_Cauldron "Skyrim:Arcadia's Cauldron"), it runs south, then follows a loop to the east, and then back northwards and straight to the door.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Commander Caius](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Caius "Skyrim:Commander Caius")  [Whiterun Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") |

## Guard Barracks

The Entrance to the Guard Barracks

The Sleeping Quarters

The interior of the building is split into four rooms with a hallway in the middle of the building connecting the four rooms. Upon entering, the first room contains a dining area along the western wall while the eastern wall is used for storage. A large sack with food sits next to the front door and another large sack rests underneath a locked display case with a [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe") on display. The rest of the area contains two food barrels, a cupboard with clutter and an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") and a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") on the shelves above, and two sacks with food. Along the western wall is a small table with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bowl with four [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"). A set of shelves holds five bottles of Nord mead and some regular books and two wheels of goat cheese. The dinner table is set for five and contains a piece of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and a coin purse.

The hallway in the center contains a wooden table with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and underneath the table, a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"). It also contains three food barrels and four bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), along with a dresser with normal clothing. The western room contains three food barrels and the secret entrance to [Dragonsreach Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach_Dungeon "Skyrim:Dragonsreach Dungeon") while the eastern room has four large food sacks, two food barrels, a wardrobe with clothes and a bit of gold and two bottles of wine.

The last room is a sleeping area where the guards relax in shifts. It contains eight owned beds and opens up to the sight of a small dining table with a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), three [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") and a bowl with eight [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"). Behind the entrance door is a set of shelves with a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"). To the west are four of the beds, an end table with clutter and some more cheese on top, a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge") and some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). A pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") is on the floor next to a huge wardrobe with minor valuables. A large sack lean against another bed, a minor chest and another end table with clutter can be found between two beds, with a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale") and four wedges of goat cheese. The eastern part of the sleeping area contains the rest of the beds. Going clockwise, you will stumble upon a dresser with clothing, with a pair of shoes on the floor and some clothes on top, right next to a coin purse. An end table sits between the next two beds, with a coin purse on top. Between the last two beds are a pair of shoes on the floor and a small table with some food and drink, two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine").

## Notes

- The guards here will not be immediately hostile to you if you have escaped from jail, they will only say *"Wait! I know you..."*, when you get close to them, but will not try to arrest you, or attack you.

## Bugs

- This barracks plays dungeon music when it obviously isn't a dungeon.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Internal map

# Skyrim:Guard Tower

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Importance of Where](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Importance_of_Where "Skyrim:The Importance of Where")* *[Ice and Chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_and_Chitin "Skyrim:Ice and Chitin")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MarkarthGuardTower | |

| Center of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") | |

The Guard Tower of Markarth

The **Guard Tower** is a Dwemer tower in the center of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

The tower is the highest building in Markarth, found in the center of the city above the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Markarth City Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_City_Guard "Skyrim:Markarth City Guard") |

## Guard Tower

The Guard Tower is reached by climbing a flight of stairs to the north of [Ghorza gra-Bagol's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol") shop and [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") and then turn to the east and keep climbing, passing the alley that leads to the [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrine of Talos") all the way to the top. Entry is made at the top of the tower, with a flight of stone spiral stairs leading down inside to a Dwemer style corridor with two large rooms used as dormitories and a circular martial skills practice room. The Dormitories are on either side of the central corridor, with two doorways into each, at the far end of the corridor is the circular practice room.

The dormitory to the south contains five owned single stone beds, three along the south wall, with one coming out from the east and west walls. Against the north wall between the two doorways is a stone table with [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"), a [steel helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Helmet "Skyrim:Steel Helmet"), a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing") and two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top. In the southwestern corner is a square wooden table with a mead barrel, a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") and two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on top, while in the northwestern corner is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel with a set of [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor") on top.

The second dormitory is almost a mirror image of the first room with five owned single stone beds, three along the north wall, with one coming out from the east and west walls. Against the south wall between the two doorways is a stone table with a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Importance of Where](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Importance_of_Where "Skyrim:The Importance of Where")*, a set of steel armor, a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and a loaf of bread on top. There is a bucket containing five red and one [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on the floor beside the table. In the southwestern corner on a crate is a cast iron pot containing a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") and a couple of pieces of cheese. On the other side of the bed is a food barrel. In the northeastern corner of the room is a square wooden table with a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") skill book *[Ice and Chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_and_Chitin "Skyrim:Ice and Chitin")*, a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and two loaves of bread, while in the southeast corner is another food barrel with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") on top and a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword") leaning against it.

Along the corridor are four stone benches, four barrels containing foodstuffs and next to one of them is a basket containing a couple of [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and several [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). There is also a random [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") in the middle of the corridor, level with the second pair of doorways. The practice room contains three melee dummies, an archery dummy and an archery target. There are also four stone shelves built into the walls, they hold a [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe"), two [steel maces](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), a pair of [steel Nordic gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets"), a steel sword, a steel helmet and a steel shield.

## Notes

- You can freely enter the tower and rooms below without it being classed as trespassing, also as the guards are all asleep, unless it is during the change of the watch you can take whatever you want and practice your pickpocketing skills.

# Skyrim:Guardhouse

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Barracks: Guardhouse ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guardhouse)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| [2920, MidYear, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_MidYear,_v6 "Skyrim:2920, MidYear, v6") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MorthalGuardhouse, MorthalGuardhouseJail | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |
| Location | |
| [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 1 |
| # of [Stone Quarries](/wiki/Skyrim:Quarried_Stone "Skyrim:Quarried Stone")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | 1 |

The Guardhouse

The **Guardhouse** is the [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") barracks on the south side of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal").

This barracks appears similar to other local houses. The interior is divided into two zones: the *[Guardhouse](#Guardhouse)* and *[Morthal Jail](#Morthal_Jail)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Legate Taurinus Duilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Taurinus_Duilis "Skyrim:Legate Taurinus Duilis") (Imperial Legate)  [Arrald Frozen-Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrald_Frozen-Heart "Skyrim:Arrald Frozen-Heart") (Stormcloak Commander)  [Benor](/wiki/Skyrim:Benor "Skyrim:Benor") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Morthal Guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal_Guard "Skyrim:Morthal Guard") |

### Exterior

There is a covered porch in front with a wooden bench along the wall to the left of the door. The porch continues around to the left of the building. In this area there are two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, one with two unowned bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top, a target dummy, and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). [Benor](/wiki/Skyrim:Benor "Skyrim:Benor") often spends his time loafing here. The door is often novice-locked, and you will incur a 5 gold [bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime#Bounties "Skyrim:Crime") whether breaking in or out. There are two [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod") behind the building.

#### Guardhouse

This area is the barracks proper. [Morthal guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal_Guard "Skyrim:Morthal Guard") are constantly coming and going from this area. There are a total of four single owned beds, two against the west wall and two against the east wall. There is a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot between each pair of beds. Opposite the door is in the middle of the south wall is a fireplace, with eight bottles of Nord mead and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the mantlepieces. In front of the hearth is a kettle containing six [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast") and a small round wooden table and two chairs. On the table are five bottles of Nord mead, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

To the left of the fireplace is a barrel with three bottles of Nord mead on top and then, a flight of stairs leading down to *Morthal jail*. On the left of these is a food barrel with four more bottles of Nord mead on top. To the right of the fireplace is another food barrel, behind this is a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, MidYear, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_MidYear,_v6 "Skyrim:2920, MidYear, v6")*. Against the north wall is a long wooden table and bench. On the table are three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of wine, two bottles of Nord mead, several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and four [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on wooden plates. There is a basket of [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") to the right and a barrel with two [potions of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and one [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top. To the left of the table is a food barrel. Along the north wall and hanging above the table are four bunches of [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, three bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the right of these are two hanging racks holding four [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

### Morthal Jail

A Morthal guard keeps close watch over the jail

Downstairs is the jail, which consists of one large adept-locked cage at the rear of the room, containing three bed rolls and a pile of food sacks. The rest of the room is partitioned with wooden walls either side of an opening. On the northern side of the wall on the left are the evidence chest and the prisoners belonging's chest next to each other. The rest of the room is used by the guards. Against the east wall are three straw bales and a chair, which the guard normally sits on. Along the south wall are several crates and food sacks. The west wall has several food barrels against it. These aren't marked as owned and therefore can be freely emptied. There is a barrel with three [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and three bottles of Nord mead against the north wall. In the middle of the room is a long wooden table and chair. On the table is a bottle of wine, a bottle of alto wine and the [key to Morthal jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Morthal_Jail "Skyrim:Key to Morthal Jail").

## Notes

- Some items found in Morthal Jail are not owned and can be taken without stealing.

## Bugs

- Benor and Arrald Frozen-Heart don't have keys to the building, so they stand outside all day long.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Guards

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page or section is incomplete. You can help by adding to it.** For more information, see the [help files](/wiki/Help:Contents "Help:Contents"), the [style guide](/wiki/UESPWiki:Style_Guide "UESPWiki:Style Guide"), and this article's [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Guards). |

:   *For the mechanic that aggresses Guards, see [Crime](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime").*
:   *For their dialogue, see [Guard Dialogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Dialogue "Skyrim:Guard Dialogue").*

**Guards** are NPCs who are usually found in towns and cities in Skyrim. If you commit a [crime](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime "Skyrim:Crime"), they can arrest you and will attack if the arrest is resisted. Under some conditions, guards can be bribed; see the crime page for details.

## Guards by Region

All of the guards below will pay attention to your bounty in the hold that they are patrolling for, and only attack you if you resist arrest when they try to arrest you. Note that it is possible for a guard in the wilderness to wander into a different hold, usually because of combat, but you will still only be arrested if you have a bounty in the hold that the guard is from.

In some quests, there are NPCs called guards who do not obey these rules, and may attack you despite not having tried to arrest you; most of those NPCs are in the Reach.

| [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") | [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") | [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") | [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") | [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_(region) "Skyrim:Winterhold (region)") | [Solstheim](/wiki/Dragonborn:Solstheim "Dragonborn:Solstheim")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") |

## Notes

- Guards will attack you if they see you wearing the [Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"). [Followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") who wear the cowl are not affected by this.
- For unknown reasons, female guards only appear in [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks")-controlled cities and holds, and are completely absent from [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion")-controlled cities as well as [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock")[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn").

## Bugs

- Guards may have access to double-damage perks which can cause them to deliver one-shot deathblows, even to high-level players.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.
- A number of city, town, and hold guards fail to respawn due to missing respawn flags in the game data. This can potentially lead to depopulation of the entire guard force in the affected areas over time.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- CWSoldierExtraDamageToPlayer and CWGuardExtraDamageToPlayer don't take into account the NPCs with those perks using two-handed weapons, as other extra damage perks do.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.
- Guards will sometimes have their usual routines glitch so that instead of patrolling their areas, they will engage in common civilian behavior such as sitting on benches or chopping wood. **?**

# Skyrim:Guests for Dinner

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). |  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | *[Dinner Invitation](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinner_Invitation "Skyrim:Dinner Invitation")* |
| Location(s): | [Bloodchill Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Cavern "Skyrim:Bloodchill Cavern") |
| Reward: | Leveled Gold, [Bloodchill Manor Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor_Key "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor Key")(only play as a vampire) |
