| Added by: | [Bloodchill Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor") |

Guests for Dinner

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Bloodchill Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Cavern "Skyrim:Bloodchill Cavern").
2. Speak to the [waiter](/wiki/Skyrim:Waiter "Skyrim:Waiter").
3. Sit at the table and read the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Please_Read_Aloud "Skyrim:Please Read Aloud").
4. Defeat either the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") or the guests and [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").
5. Speak to the survivor to receive leveled gold and the key to your new home.

### Player as a Non-Vampire

The guests await

When you arrive at the manor, a number of guests are milling around the front door listening to a bard. Just inside, another reveler is drinking and dancing. Proceed down the hallway to the [waiter](/wiki/Skyrim:Waiter "Skyrim:Waiter"). No matter what you say, the outcome will be the same; with him handing you a [dinner menu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinner_Menu "Skyrim:Dinner Menu") (Version 1) and directing you and the other guests to your seats.

Sit down at the table, in a place of honor across from the door. Once you sit down, read the note on your plate named [Please Read Aloud](/wiki/Skyrim:Please_Read_Aloud "Skyrim:Please Read Aloud") to gain some insight into this mysterious dinner party and proceed with the quest. After you read the last page of the letter, the waiter will approach [Galtius](/wiki/Skyrim:Galtius "Skyrim:Galtius") across from you and bite him from behind, killing him. As the other guests rise from their seats in a panic, the bard in the room, the waiter, and two gargoyles will attack.

Deal with them, and be careful of the waiter: his lightning attacks are strong enough to one-shot lower-level players. [Resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic") gear and [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") might help. Once all the vampires and their stone minions are dead, speak with the "survivor." Some of the other guests may have survived your battle but the one to speak with is the Orc [Durian](/wiki/Skyrim:Durian "Skyrim:Durian"), who is revealed to be a member of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"):

:   **The vampires are all dead. And the will says the house belongs to me.**
:   *"Very good. But you've created a debt between us. Here. Take this. We are even now."*

He will then hand you a leveled amount of gold but no [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor_Key "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor Key"), and you will become the official owner of the manor. This completes the quest. The doors along the entry hallway will open and you can begin using your new base.

If there are any surviving guests besides Durian, they will return to sit at the dinner table amidst the carnage. Once you leave and reenter the cave, all of the bodies and debris will be cleaned up (including the vampiric bard near the entrance, which was presumably dispatched by Durian on your way into dinner), any surviving guests will have left, and the dinner table will be cleared out of the trophy room to allow your unimpeded access.

### Player as a Vampire

If the player is a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism"), things play out a little differently. When you arrive at the manor, pass through the guests and speak to the [waiter](/wiki/Skyrim:Waiter "Skyrim:Waiter") at the end of the hall. After choosing one of four options, the waiter will give a generic response and hand you the [dinner menu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinner_Menu "Skyrim:Dinner Menu") (Version 2). He will then turn and lead you to the banquet table.

Once there, sit and read through the feast note [Please Read Aloud](/wiki/Skyrim:Please_Read_Aloud "Skyrim:Please Read Aloud"). After doing so you are instructed to begin the feast, by drinking the blood of the already enthralled [Parven](/wiki/Skyrim:Parven "Skyrim:Parven"). At that point, the waiter will approach [Galtius](/wiki/Skyrim:Galtius "Skyrim:Galtius") and bite him from behind, killing him. After Galtius's death Parven will also terminate and the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") will enter the building, initiating battle.

After disposing of the Dawnguard and the remaining guests, speak to the waiter once more.

:   **The Dawnguard and the nobles are dead.**
:   *It would seem so.*
:   **The note seemed to imply the last survivor would get the house.**
:   *I'm so glad you succeeded. Here. Please take this for your trouble.*

At this point the waiter will give you the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodchill_Manor_Key "Skyrim:Bloodchill Manor Key") to the manor and some leveled gold, completing the quest. Three more dialogue options are given; all will end the conversation. The doors along the entry hallway are now open for use, and when you leave and reenter the cavern all of the destruction from your fight will be cleared away.

## Notes

- After the attack in the non-vampire version, Durian is renamed Dawnguard even if the player has not started the Dawnguard quest line.
- It is significantly easier to complete the quest as a Vampire, especially at lower levels, as the vampires are very threatening spellcasters and the gargoyles in the dining hall will also come to life and attack the player if they are not a vampire.

## Bugs

- You may receive a radiant quest from the Companions to intimidate the waiter, if you brawl the waiter and don't kill him, the quest will softlock, as your player will be unable to move when re-entering Bloodchill Cavern. **?**
- If you attack and kill the bard, waiter, and gargoyles before reading the note, the quest will still complete properly, but you will be left unable to move if you then read the note at any point after.
- If you start the fight and leave Bloodchill Cavern before finishing the fight, the doors will be closed and the gargoyles will not respond to any action, making the quest impossible to complete.
  - To fix this bug, use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") command `setstage ccEEJSSE005_Quest 100`.
  - This bug can also be fixed by attacking the person outside, which skips to the vampire attack and causes the door to open. However, the gargoyles will remain unresponsive.
  - If playing on consoles, a work around exists. Abilities with a large area of effect such as Kyne's Peace can be used to aggro the Waiter behind the locked doors. When leaving the cave, any aggressive vampires should appear outside with you after a small delay, making it possible to kill them. The disguised Dawnguard member will now reward you, completing the quest, and unlocking all the previously locked doors of the manor.
- After the quest is complete, the *Dinner Invitation* when read in your inventory may now be a blank sheet of paper. **?**

## Quest Stages

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccEEJSSE005_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccEEJSSE005_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Guild Halls

## Overview

The College of Winterhold

This page lists all the main faction **guild halls** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

### Bards College

:   **[Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College")** — A musical school in Solitude. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bards+College)

### Blades

:    **[Sky Haven Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Sky_Haven_Temple "Skyrim:Sky Haven Temple")** — A large mountaintop fort that served as the major Blades temple and outpost in Skyrim, now long abandoned and in Forsworn territory. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sky+Haven+Temple)

### College of Winterhold

:    **[College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)")** — A school of the arcane arts. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=College+of+Winterhold)

### Companions

:   **[Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr")** — The mead hall headquarters of the Companions. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Jorrvaskr)
:   **[The Underforge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Underforge "Skyrim:The Underforge")** — An ancient chamber hidden underneath the Skyforge used as a ritual chamber by the Circle of the Companions. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Underforge)

### Dark Brotherhood

:    **[Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Sanctuary")** — An active Dark Brotherhood sanctuary west of Falkreath. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dark+Brotherhood+Sanctuary)
:    **[Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary")** — A disused Dark Brotherhood sanctuary on the shore of the Sea of Ghosts near Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dawnstar+Sanctuary)

### Dawnguard DG

:    **[Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large fort southeast of Riften which serves as the Dawnguard's base of operations. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Dawnguard+%28DG%29)

### Thieves Guild

:    **[Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(place) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (place)")** — The headquarters of the Thieves Guild located with the sewers beneath Riften, known as The Ratway. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Thieves+Guild)
:   **[The Ragged Flagon](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon")** — A tavern that is part of the Thieves Guild's headquarters. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Ratway)
:    **[Nightingale Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingale_Hall "Skyrim:Nightingale Hall")** — The home of the Nightingales between Riften and the Shadow Stone. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Nightingale+Hall)

### Volkihar Vampire Clan DG

:    **[Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large fortress on an island far northwest of Solitude connected to Castle Volkihar which serves as the Volkihar vampire clan's home. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)

# Skyrim:Guldun Rock

## Overview

Guldun Rock

**Guldun Rock** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") east of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). It contains only one zone, *[Guldun Rock Cave](#Guldun_Rock_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Two mammoth cheese bowls

The camp is off the road that follows the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River") east from Whiterun to [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol"), directly south of [Valtheim Towers](/wiki/Skyrim:Valtheim_Towers "Skyrim:Valtheim Towers"). A path leading from the road is marked by a stone cairn surrounded by two [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") shrubs and several [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"). Near the first bend in the path is a leveled [animal](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") that will normally be alerted to your passing. The path leads to a wide flight of stairs up to the plateau with the camp.

Two [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") occupy the camp. Several painted stones are on your right as you approach the camp; between two of these is a fire-hardened stake with bunches of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") and [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") hanging from it. Nine [mammoth cheese bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl") and many bones and skulls are scattered around the camp. The campfire is north of *Guldun Rock Cave* up a flight of stone stairs on top of a ruined stone building. It provides a good vantage point to view quite a distance to the north. North of the campfire, near two [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein"), is a leveled animal.

### Guldun Rock Cave

Guldun Rock Cave

The cave is typically unoccupied. Two patches of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") mushrooms grow within the cave. As you enter, there is a central rock pillar with painted stones and a mammoth cheese bowl around it. On a flat rock to the west is a dead [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") with three [charred skeever hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") under it and another mammoth cheese bowl beside it. A large campfire is on the other side of the central pillar with a dead [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow") to the west, while to the south is another flat rock with two [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") (one large, one medium), a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), six loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Knights of the Nine](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Knights_of_the_Nine "Skyrim:The Knights of the Nine")* on top and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") behind. Northeast of the central pillar is a second fire built from carefully stacked wood of the type usually used by giants to cook larger animals like [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses") and cows.

# Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Gyldenhul Barrow ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Gyldenhul+Barrow)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Gyldenhul_Barrow "Lore:Gyldenhul Barrow")) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |

| Special Features | |

Gyldenhul Barrow

**Gyldenhul Barrow** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") containing the spirit and treasure of [Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand"). It contains only one zone, *[Gyldenhul Barrow](#Gyldenhul_Barrow)*.

The ruin only becomes accessible near the end of the quest [Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)").

## Related Quests

- **[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)")**: Find the treasure of [Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand").

### Exterior

The entrance is on the northwestern shore of [Horker Island](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Island "Skyrim:Horker Island"). Two small rowboats are drawn up on the nearby beach, and two leveled [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") guarding the entrance will attack on sight. There are four [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Grass Pod") plants on the shore, a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush and a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") to the left of the entrance, and several standing stones around the entrance. The entrance is through an iron door requiring the [Gyldenhul Barrow key](/wiki/Skyrim:Gyldenhul_Barrow_Key "Skyrim:Gyldenhul Barrow Key"), which is found upon collecting the fourth piece of the [Deathbrand armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Armor "Skyrim:Deathbrand Armor") treasure.

### Gyldenhul Barrow

A stalhrim deposit

Upon entering, you will be in a small catacomb area. A dead adventurer is sitting against a wall in front of you. A pickaxe is beside him, and he is carrying a [torn note](/wiki/Skyrim:Torn_Note_(Dragonborn) "Skyrim:Torn Note (Dragonborn)"). Two upright sarcophagi to the east and west contain [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") deposits, as does an upright sarcophagus in front of you with a [dead draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") spilling out (although this small northern deposit cannot be mined). After you mine the stalhrim to the west, pass through the now unblocked sarcophagus to enter a wide corridor with stairs descending on your left to a key-locked iron door. The same key that opened the outside door opens this one.

_05.jpg)

The treasure of Haknir Death-Brand

Through the door is a wide corridor leading to another locked iron door that uses the same key. The corridor is full of treasure, some of which is trapped, causing a gate to drop behind you and sealing you in when you take it, and forcing you to explore further into the barrow to escape. At the far end on the left is a master-locked chest, and at the near end on the right is an expert-locked chest with two [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") beside it. In the middle of the corridor is a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"). Found in the corridor are a quiver of [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows"), a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), a [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe"), a [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"), a [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword"), a [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), a pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets")/bracers, a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), a set of [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), a [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") potion, four additional potions, an empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a filled soul gem, all of which are random and set the first time you enter the barrow even if you didn't mine the stalhrim deposit. In addition, there is a [potion of ultimate healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Healing"), a [potion of ultimate magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Magicka"), three [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), four [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"), a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond"), two [emeralds](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"), a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), seven [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), two [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst") (this is almost under the front of the master-locked chest and can be easily missed), and 6400-9600 [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Both chests are opened with the same key used for the doors. The only way you can go is forward through the second iron door.

The King of Ghosts' skeleton

Upon opening the second door, you find yourself at the top of several flights of stairs leading down to the southeast. At the bottom of the stairs is a doorway into a huge room, featuring arches on either side and tall pillars rising to a suspended ceiling. Ahead is a wide flight of stairs leading up to the south-southeast. At the top is an altar upon which the skeleton of Haknir Death-Brand is laid out. Beside him is [Bloodscythe](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodscythe "Skyrim:Bloodscythe"), a unique [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar"). Upon taking the weapon, the whole barrow will shake, and [Haknir's ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand") will rise behind you, down on the main floor of the room. In addition to fighting his ghost, you also must face the ghosts of his quartermaster [Garuk Windrime](/wiki/Skyrim:Garuk_Windrime "Skyrim:Garuk Windrime"), his helmsman [Thalin Ebonhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalin_Ebonhand "Skyrim:Thalin Ebonhand"), and [the ghosts of his former crew](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir%27s_Crew "Skyrim:Haknir's Crew"), making this quite a long and potentially difficult fight.

Once they are all vanquished, you will complete the quest Deathbrand, and can loot his skeleton for some gold and Bloodscythe's bladed companion, the unique scimitar [Soulrender](/wiki/Skyrim:Soulrender "Skyrim:Soulrender"). There are short flights of ascending stairs on either side of the altar, one to the northwest with a large urn at the top, and the other to the southeast leading to the boss chest.

## Notes

- Gyldenhul Barrow also [appears](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Gyldenhul_Barrow "Bloodmoon:Gyldenhul Barrow") in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")*.

## Bugs

- Gyldenhul Barrow's entrance door is locked by a master-level lock and technically requires the Gyldenhul Barrow key to open. However, this can be circumvented by attempting to pick the lock while having the [Wax Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Wax_Key "Skyrim:Wax Key") perk, which gives you a copy of the required key. Entering through this method and proceeding to fight Haknir will break the quest and may cause it to remain permanently in your quest log, as the correct quest stages are skipped.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=11965)) The entrance door is now marked as requiring the key, such that you can't attempt to lockpick it and thus can't receive a duplicate key.

# Skyrim:Haafingar Stormcloak Camp

## Overview

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Haafingar Stormcloak Camp

**Haafingar Stormcloak Camp** is a [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"), located northeast of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") and south of the [Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia").

The camp is normally commanded by [Istar Cairn-Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Istar_Cairn-Breaker "Skyrim:Istar Cairn-Breaker"), except during the related quests, at which point [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") will assume command.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Istar Cairn-Breaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Istar_Cairn-Breaker "Skyrim:Istar Cairn-Breaker") (commander)  [Stormcloak Quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster")  [Stormcloak Soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier")  [Galmar Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Galmar_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Galmar Stone-Fist") (commander) [†](#intnote_Q) |

[†](#note_Q)This person only resides here during the related quests.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Hraggstad")**: Prepare for the final assault on [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") by taking [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").
- **[Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude")**: Conquer the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [capital](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and free Skyrim from the Empire! ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Haafingar Stormcloak Camp

It is a typical Stormcloak camp, consisting of a central campfire with a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") hanging over it, around which the rest of the camp is arranged. To the south of the campfire are three small tents containing unowned hay piles. To the southwest is the command tent, containing a dresser and a large table covered with a map of Skyrim showing the progress of the civil war and the various forts and cities held by each side. This is where the commander spends most of their time. To the right of the command tent are some barrels. To the south is the commander's tent, containing an owned bedroll, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and an end table. To the north of the campfire is another small tent containing an unowned hay pile, with a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") plant behind the tent. Farther to the north is the hospital tent, which contains three hay piles occupied by wounded soldiers and a low table holding a random [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). To the left of the hospital tent is a table with a built-in [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), next to an unlocked chest containing various items to treat the sick, including potions of [cure poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Poison "Skyrim:Cure Poison"), potions of [cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Cure Disease"), and [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). To the right of the hospital tent is another small tent containing an unowned hay pile. Beyond the small tent are two picketed [horses](/wiki/Skyrim:Horses "Skyrim:Horses"). They are owned, and taking them is considered stealing. In front of the hospital tent is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). To the south is the workstation for the [Stormcloak quartermaster](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Quartermaster "Skyrim:Stormcloak Quartermaster"), consisting of an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). A long wooden table and a crate hold various [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") and [steel weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Weapons "Skyrim:Steel Weapons") and [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). There are many [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") near the camp at night, and during the day several [butterflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Passive_Creatures#Insects "Skyrim:Passive Creatures") can be found near the picketed horses.

Any time [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") is controlled by the Stormcloaks, this camp will not be present. As long as you haven't completed [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion"), you are free to sleep in the small tents and trade with the quartermaster.

## Bugs

- The camp may not be properly disbanded while Haafinger is under Stormcloak control, leaving the soldiers and commanding officer present.

Haafingar, a hold in northwest Skyrim

**Haafingar** is a relatively small [hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Holds "Skyrim:Holds") in northwest [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"), containing the provincial capital [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). As the home of the provincial capital, Haafingar is the center of [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") rule in Skyrim. It only becomes Stormcloak-run if you join the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") and complete the entire questline, including both [The Battle for Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Hraggstad") and the [Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude").

Haafingar is dominated by a large ridge that runs the length of the hold. Pine forests and meadows cover the southern slopes down to the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River"), while the north side is colder, and dominated by mountains and frozen coastline. Solitude itself sits on a massive natural archway that extends over the mouth of the Karth from the eastern spur of the ridge.

Map of Skyrim with Haafingar marked in red

Solitude, capital of Haafingar and Skyrim

## Flora and Fauna

Haafingar's coastline is ideal for the growth of [nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") and [clams](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam") in the water and [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") and [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") on land. Near [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), [fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fish "Skyrim:Fish") can be enjoyed around [Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill") where [dragonflies](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonfly "Skyrim:Dragonfly") play over the water. A fair amount of [nightshade plants](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") grow inside the capital. [Mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), [mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Mountain Flower"), and [thistles](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle") can be found in the lower parts of the hold while only [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") and sporadic mountain flowers can be found in the snow-covered tail of the [Druadach Mountains](/wiki/Skyrim:Druadach_Mountains "Skyrim:Druadach Mountains").

## Places

All locations in Haafingar with individual map markers are listed. There are a few places without map markers listed for their significance.

### Hold Capital

-  **[Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")** — A major city on the northwest coast of Skyrim, and the capital of both Haafingar and the entire province. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude)
- **[Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College")** — A musical school in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bards+College)
-  **[Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace")** — The current seat of power for [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), Haafingar, and [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"); and home to the [High King of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blue+Palace)
- **[Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour")** — A large [fortress](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") which acts as the headquarters of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and residence of the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Dour)
-  **[East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse")** — A warehouse on the [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") docks immediately southeast of the city. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=East+Empire+Company+Warehouse)
- **[Solitude Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Stables "Skyrim:Solitude Stables")** — The [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") serving the city of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Stables)

### Farms, Towns, and Settlements including Orc Strongholds and Inns

-  **[Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge")** — A milling [town](/wiki/Skyrim:Towns "Skyrim:Towns") in southern Haafingar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragon+Bridge)
- **[Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Lumber_Camp "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Lumber Camp")** — A sawmill and lumber camp in the southwestern part of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragon+Bridge+Lumber+Camp)
-  **[Ironback Hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironback_Hideout "Skyrim:Ironback Hideout")** — A dilapidated house to the northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), a short distance east of [The Steed Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Steed_Stone "Skyrim:The Steed Stone"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ironback+Hideout)
-  **[Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm")** — A small [farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Farms "Skyrim:Farms") and [stable](/wiki/Skyrim:Stables "Skyrim:Stables") along the [Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River"), outside of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Katla%27s+Farm)
- **[Lylvieve Family's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Lylvieve_Family%27s_House "Skyrim:Lylvieve Family's House")** — A small farmhouse on the northwestern side of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), located next to [Horgeir's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Horgeir%27s_House "Skyrim:Horgeir's House"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lylvieve+Family%27s+House)
-  **[Solitude Sawmill](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Sawmill "Skyrim:Solitude Sawmill")** — A wood mill southwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Sawmill)
-  **[Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy")** — The [Aldmeri Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion")'s diplomatic mission to [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Thalmor+Embassy)

### Camps , including Giant Camps and Military Camps

-  **[Dragon Bridge Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge_Overlook "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge Overlook")** — A small [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") south of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dragon+Bridge+Overlook)
-  **[Haafingar Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Haafingar Stormcloak Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") in Haafingar, located northeast of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") and south of the [Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haafingar+Stormcloak+Camp)
-  **[Solitude Military Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Military_Camp "Skyrim:Solitude Military Camp")** — A [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Camps "Skyrim:Stormcloak Camps") set up west of [Katla's Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Katla%27s_Farm "Skyrim:Katla's Farm") for the [attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude") on [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Military+Camp)

### Caves

-  **[Brinewater Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Brinewater_Grotto "Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker") or [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brinewater+Grotto)
-  **[Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder") and their leader [Captain Hargar](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Hargar "Skyrim:Captain Hargar"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Oar+Grotto)
- \* **[Lost Echo Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Echo_Cave "Skyrim:Lost Echo Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Lost+Echo+Cave)
-  **[Lower Steepfall Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Lower_Steepfall_Burrow "Skyrim:Lower Steepfall Burrow")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") and [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steepfall+Burrow)
-  **[Pinemoon Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") and [wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinemoon+Cave)
-  **[Ravenscar Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravenscar_Hollow "Skyrim:Ravenscar Hollow")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") inhabited by [hagravens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven") west of the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy") and due east of the [Steed Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Steed_Stone "Skyrim:The Steed Stone"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Ravenscar+Hollow)
-  **[Rimerock Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Rimerock_Burrow "Skyrim:Rimerock Burrow")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing an [atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach "Skyrim:Atronach") and the powerful conjurer [Sebastian Lort](/wiki/Skyrim:Sebastian_Lort "Skyrim:Sebastian Lort"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Rimerock+Burrow)
-  **[Shadowgreen Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Shadowgreen_Cavern "Skyrim:Shadowgreen Cavern")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing leveled [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") and [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Shadowgreen+Cavern)
-  **[Steepfall Burrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Steepfall_Burrow "Skyrim:Steepfall Burrow")** — A small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") and [ice wolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf "Skyrim:Ice Wolf"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steepfall+Burrow)
-  **[Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave")** — A medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") or [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Wolfskull+Cave)

\* Though located well within Haafingar's borders, the location is marked as belonging to [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold").

### Ruins including Dwarven and Nordic

-  **[Volskygge](/wiki/Skyrim:Volskygge "Skyrim:Volskygge")** — A medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), and the [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") [Volsung](/wiki/Skyrim:Volsung_(creature) "Skyrim:Volsung (creature)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Volskygge)

### Towers and Forts

-  **[Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A large [castle](/wiki/Skyrim:Castles "Skyrim:Castles") on an island far northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") connected to [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Castle+Volkihar+%28DG%29)
-  **[Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad")** — A medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Hraggstad)
-  **[Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep")** — A small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Northwatch+Keep)
-  **[Pinefrost Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinefrost_Tower "Skyrim:Pinefrost Tower")** — A small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") northwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Pinefrost+Tower)
-  **[Widow's Watch Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Widow%27s_Watch_Ruins "Skyrim:Widow's Watch Ruins")** — A small ruined [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Towers "Skyrim:Imperial Towers") west-northwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing a [hag](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Widow%27s+Watch+Ruins)

### Standing Stones and Daedric Shrines

-  **[Statue to Meridia](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_to_Meridia "Skyrim:Statue to Meridia")** — The [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Meridia](/wiki/Lore:Meridia "Lore:Meridia"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Statue+to+Meridia)
-  **[The Steed Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Steed_Stone "Skyrim:The Steed Stone")** — One of the thirteen [Standing Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:Standing_Stone "Skyrim:Standing Stone") scattered across Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Steed+Stone)

### Landmarks , including Bodies of Water , Clearings , Ships and Shipwrecks

-  **[Clearpine Pond](/wiki/Skyrim:Clearpine_Pond "Skyrim:Clearpine Pond")** — A pond with a small island, located west-southwest of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), just to the northeast of [Pinemoon Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Pinemoon_Cave "Skyrim:Pinemoon Cave"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Clearpine+Pond)
-  **[Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload")** — A [ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") docked north of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Dainty+Sload)
-  **[Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — An isolated region in northwestern Skyrim once inhabited by the [Snow Elves](/wiki/Lore:Snow_Elf "Lore:Snow Elf") worshipping the god [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Forgotten+Vale+%28DG%29)
-  **[Icewater Jetty](/wiki/Skyrim:Icewater_Jetty "Skyrim:Icewater Jetty")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") — A small isolated [dock](/wiki/Skyrim:Other_Places#Docks "Skyrim:Other Places") far west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and northwest of [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Icewater+Jetty+%28DG%29)
- **[Karth River](/wiki/Skyrim:Karth_River "Skyrim:Karth River")** — A river flowing from [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Karth+River)
-  **[The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah")** — The personal transport vessel of the Emperor, [Titus Mede II](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=The+Katariah)
-  **[Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear")** — A [shipwreck](/wiki/Skyrim:Shipwrecks "Skyrim:Shipwrecks") west of [Ravenscar Hollow](/wiki/Skyrim:Ravenscar_Hollow "Skyrim:Ravenscar Hollow") on the northern coast. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Orphan%27s+Tear)
- **[Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts")** — A vast ocean to the north of Skyrim. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sea+of+Ghosts)
-  **[Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse")** — A stone building on the northern coast of Skyrim that helps to guide ships into Solitude harbor. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Solitude+Lighthouse)

## Haafingar Quests

All the quests that are started in or are related to Haafingar (except for radiant quests begun in other holds) are listed here:

### Main Quest

- **[Diplomatic Immunity](/wiki/Skyrim:Diplomatic_Immunity "Skyrim:Diplomatic Immunity")**: Infiltrate a party at the [Thalmor Embassy](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor_Embassy "Skyrim:Thalmor Embassy").
- **[Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")**: Enforce a ceasefire to secure [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach").

### Imperial Legion Civil War Quests

- **[Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion")**: Prove yourself worthy to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)")**: Find the [Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[Message to Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Message_to_Whiterun_(Imperial) "Skyrim:Message to Whiterun (Imperial)")**: Deliver the message that will decide [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")'s allegiance.
- **[Reunification of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Reunification_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Reunification of Skyrim")**: Reunite Skyrim under the leadership of the Empire. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)")**: Find and deliver some forged [documents](/wiki/Skyrim:StormCloak_Documents "Skyrim:StormCloak Documents") to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").
- **[Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav")**: Take [Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Fort Kastav") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and rescue the prisoners within. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)")**: Take [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)")**: Take [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall") for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Stormcloaks Civil War Quests

- **[Liberation of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Liberation_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Liberation of Skyrim")**: Drive the Imperials from Skyrim. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Hraggstad")**: Prepare for the final assault on [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") by taking [this fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad") for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").
- **[Battle for Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Solitude "Skyrim:Battle for Solitude")**: Conquer the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [capital](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and free Skyrim from the Empire! ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Daedric Quests

- **[The Mind of Madness](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mind_of_Madness "Skyrim:The Mind of Madness")**: Gain access to and solve the mystery of the [Pelagius Wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Pelagius_Wing "Skyrim:Pelagius Wing").
- **[A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend")**: Help [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") reunite with his [master](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile").
- **[The Break of Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Break_of_Dawn "Skyrim:The Break of Dawn")**: Find [Meridia's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Meridia's Beacon") and use its light to cleanse her [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Kilkreath_Ruins "Skyrim:Kilkreath Ruins") of undead.

### Dark Brotherhood

- **[Bound Until Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Bound_Until_Death "Skyrim:Bound Until Death")**: Assassinate [Vittoria Vici](/wiki/Skyrim:Vittoria_Vici "Skyrim:Vittoria Vici") at her own wedding.
- **[Breaching Security](/wiki/Skyrim:Breaching_Security "Skyrim:Breaching Security")**: Kill and frame the [son](/wiki/Skyrim:Gaius_Maro "Skyrim:Gaius Maro") of a high-ranking [Imperial guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
- **[To Kill an Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:To_Kill_an_Empire "Skyrim:To Kill an Empire")**: Attempt to assassinate the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") while disguised as the [Gourmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourmet "Skyrim:Gourmet").
- **[Hail Sithis!](/wiki/Skyrim:Hail_Sithis! "Skyrim:Hail Sithis!")**: One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.
- **[Kill Safia](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Safia "Skyrim:Kill Safia")**: Kill a [pirate captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Safia "Skyrim:Safia") on her own [ship](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Wave "Skyrim:Red Wave").

### Thieves Guild

- **[Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly")**: Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.
- **[No Stone Unturned](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Stone_Unturned "Skyrim:No Stone Unturned")**: Find the [24 gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Unusual_Gem "Skyrim:Unusual Gem") to restore the Crown of Barenziah.
- **[The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload")**: Frame a [ship's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") captain to get revenge for a [jilted merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur").

### Bards College

- **[Tending the Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Tending_the_Flames "Skyrim:Tending the Flames")**: Unveil the truth about a deceitful [King](/wiki/Skyrim:Olaf_One-Eye "Skyrim:Olaf One-Eye") and become a member of the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College").
- **[Finn's Lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute "Skyrim:Finn's Lute")**: Return an invaluable [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Finn%27s_Lute_(item) "Skyrim:Finn's Lute (item)") to [Inge Six Fingers](/wiki/Skyrim:Inge_Six_Fingers "Skyrim:Inge Six Fingers").
- **[Pantea's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute")**: Find a missing [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea%27s_Flute_(item) "Skyrim:Pantea's Flute (item)") for [Pantea](/wiki/Skyrim:Pantea_Ateia "Skyrim:Pantea Ateia").
- **[Rjorn's Drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Rjorn%27s_Drum "Skyrim:Rjorn's Drum")**: Retrieve a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Rjorn.27s_Drum "Skyrim:Quest Items") for [Giraud Gemane](/wiki/Skyrim:Giraud_Gemane "Skyrim:Giraud Gemane").

### Side Quests

- **[The Man Who Cried Wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf")**: Investigate reports of strange happenings in [Wolfskull Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolfskull_Cave "Skyrim:Wolfskull Cave").
- **[The Wolf Queen Awakened](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen_Awakened "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen Awakened")**: Potema must be stopped.
- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.
- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

### Dawnguard Quests

- **[Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Choose your side!
- **[Prophet (Dawnguard)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
- **[Prophet (Vampire)](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Vampire) "Skyrim:Prophet (Vampire)")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): The time of prophecy has arrived! Locate [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") for the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").
- **[Kindred Judgment](/wiki/Skyrim:Kindred_Judgment "Skyrim:Kindred Judgment")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Confront [Lord Harkon](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Harkon "Skyrim:Lord Harkon").

### Creation Club Quests

- **[Brothers in Irons](/wiki/Skyrim:Brothers_in_Irons "Skyrim:Brothers in Irons")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Iron "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Iron"): Investigate a wanted criminal.
- **[Gift of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Gift_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail"): Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").
- **[The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_of_Nocturnal "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl of Nocturnal")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gray_Cowl_Returns! "Skyrim:The Gray Cowl Returns!"): Investigate the legend of the Gray Fox.
- **[More Than You Can Chew](/wiki/Skyrim:More_Than_You_Can_Chew "Skyrim:More Than You Can Chew")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Netch Leather Armor"): Obtain the secrets of crafting with [netch leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Netch Leather") from a tribe of [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling").
- **[Night Hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Hunter "Skyrim:Night Hunter")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Elite_Crossbows "Skyrim:Elite Crossbows"): Claim the belongings of a Haafingar vampire hunter.
- **[Over the Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Over_the_Edge "Skyrim:Over the Edge")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier"): A criminal has sensed his past catching up with him.
- **[The Restless](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Restless "Skyrim:The Restless")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Man%27s_Dread "Skyrim:Dead Man's Dread"): Search for an ancient pirate ship.
- **[Restoring Order](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoring_Order "Skyrim:Restoring Order")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Saints_%26_Seducers "Skyrim:Saints & Seducers"): Put an end to the melding of planes under [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

### Other

In addition, many miscellaneous quests, such as favors, are located in Haafingar. They are listed [here](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests#Haafingar "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests").

## Bugs

- Although Castle Volkihar is located here, crimes committed there may earn you a bounty in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") instead. **?**

Haelga's Bunkhouse

**Haelga's Bunkhouse** is a boarding house in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") run by [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga") that houses several of Riften's citizens.

It is the first building on the right when entering via the main gate to the north.

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga") (Owner)  [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") (Worker and Niece)  [Brand-Shei](/wiki/Skyrim:Brand-Shei "Skyrim:Brand-Shei")  [From-Deepest-Fathoms](/wiki/Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms "Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms")  [Grelka](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelka "Skyrim:Grelka")  [Niluva Hlaalu](/wiki/Skyrim:Niluva_Hlaalu "Skyrim:Niluva Hlaalu")  [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing")  [Tythis Ulen](/wiki/Skyrim:Tythis_Ulen "Skyrim:Tythis Ulen")  [Ungrien](/wiki/Skyrim:Ungrien "Skyrim:Ungrien")  [Viriya](/wiki/Skyrim:Viriya "Skyrim:Viriya")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing")  [Wujeeta](/wiki/Skyrim:Wujeeta "Skyrim:Wujeeta") |

## Related Quests

- **[Caught Red Handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_Red_Handed "Skyrim:Caught Red Handed")**: Gather three marks of Dibella to help [Svana Far-Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") against [Haelga](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga").
- **[Taking Care of Business](/wiki/Skyrim:Taking_Care_of_Business "Skyrim:Taking Care of Business")**: Collect some debts for the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Haelga's Bunkhouse

Upon entering you are faced with the L-shaped counter with a door behind. On the counter is a copy of *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")*, a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Until_Next_Time "Skyrim:Until Next Time") from one of [Haelga's](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga "Skyrim:Haelga") suitors, four loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") underneath. To the right above the counter on the west wall is a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a couple of sacks. On your right when you enter, against the east wall is a dresser. To the west is the dining area with two long wooden tables with benches and one small square table with two chairs. On the tables are four [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, a [raw rabbit leg](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottle of wine and several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese. In the southwest corner is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand next to a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel.

To the east of the counter is a large open area with chairs and barrels in the northwestern corner, under the stairs that lead up to the bedrooms above. Against the east wall is a square wooden table and two chairs with a bottle of wine on the table, a wooden bench and a cupboard holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"). At the southern end of the room is a door that leads to the staircase down to the cellar with a dresser to the right of it against the wall, on this is a [statue of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Statue_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Statue of Dibella"), a bunch of lavender and two wooden bowl containing two of each [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower").

Behind the counter, the door leads to Haelga's bedroom, which contains a double bed (complete with shackles) coming out from the middle of the west wall, with an end table to the left which holds *[The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v1 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1")* and *[v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v2 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v2")*, a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a bottle of Nord mead and if you have completed the initial [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Chance_Arrangement "Skyrim:A Chance Arrangement") also a bottle of [Falmer Blood Elixir](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Blood_Elixir "Skyrim:Falmer Blood Elixir"). At the foot of the bed is a dresser with a [Shrine of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Shrine of Dibella"), a [honey](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey "Skyrim:Honey") pot--(see [notes](#Notes)), a bunch of lavender, a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a bowl containing a red, blue and purple mountain flower. To the right and under the bed are additional leather strips as well as a horker tusk. On the wall to the right of the bed is a chair and on the north wall is a wall shelf holding an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") and two potions of minor stamina, a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina") and a [potion of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor"), which are obviously for use by her suitors as she spreads the love of [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella") in her unique way, which you will quickly learn by listening to Haelga and her niece Svana. Further to the right, still against the north wall is a wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and in the northeast corner is a small square wooden table, with a bottle of Nord mead and the [business ledger](/wiki/Skyrim:Business_Ledger "Skyrim:Business Ledger") on top.

There are several food barrels by the top of the staircase down to the cellar and on one of these are three loose [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Descending the stairs brings you to the first of two rooms linked by a doorway both used for storage. The first contains more barrels some containing foodstuffs, others containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), a pile of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") including four loose pieces and several bales of straw. The second room in the cellar contains various pieces of disused furniture, more barrels and sacks, three sets of shelves and a cupboard. The cupboard only holds clutter, but the shelves hold three bottles of Nord mead, two bottles of wine, two cabbages, ten [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two loaves of bread and many pieces of cheese.

At the top of the stairs leading up to the second floor, there is an alcove in front containing a few barrels of food. There are two doorways from here; one to the west and the other to the east. Both rooms are very similar as both room have five single beds, four end tables, a fireplace with a piece of firewood beside it and a door to the south. The room to the west has a wardrobe in an alcove to the north and on the end tables are three bottles of wine and a bottle of Nord mead. The door to the south opens into a storeroom with several barrels and crates. The room to the east has a dresser with a bottle of alto wine and a copy of the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Beggar](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_(book) "Skyrim:Beggar (book)")* on top, in the alcove to the north and on the end tables are a bottle of Nord mead, a bottle of wine and a salmon steak, with a second bottle of Nord mead on the mantelpiece and a wall shelf on the east wall with a couple of sacks and another bottle of Nord mead. The door to the south open into [Svana Far-Shield's](/wiki/Skyrim:Svana_Far-Shield "Skyrim:Svana Far-Shield") bedroom which consists of an owned single bed in the northeast corner, with an end table beside it, a wall shelf above, holding a bottle of wine and a wardrobe containing clothes against the south wall.

## Notes

- Although Svana has her own room, she seems to sometimes sleep in one of the dormitories with the others.
- The honey pot is one of only two to be found in the base game.

## Bugs

- When doing [The Numbers Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Numbers_Job "Skyrim:The Numbers Job") for the Thieves Guild, there is a 50% chance that the quest marker for the Haelga's Bunkhouse Ledger is pointing to a crate instead of the ledger. See the [quest page](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Numbers_Job#Bugs "Skyrim:The Numbers Job") for details.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- The beds in the bunkhouse are free to sleep in even though Haelga claims that you can't sleep here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, addresses this issue. All beds in the bunkhouse are now marked as owned by the bunkhouse faction.
- Be careful if [Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(A) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (A)") sends you here. The bunkhouse cell will often have numerous other NPCs inside who don't live here that can be easily killed by the animal. This can end up breaking quests due to NPCs who are not flagged essential.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.8, addresses this issue. The bunkhouse has been added to the exempt list to prevent that from happening.

# Skyrim:Haemar's Shame

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Haemar's Shame ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Haemar%27s+Shame)) | | |
