Haemar's Shame

**Haemar's Shame** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") east of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") containing [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). It contains two zones: *[Haemar's Cavern](#Haemar.27s_Cavern)* and *[Haemar's Shame](#Haemar.27s_Shame)*.

Shrine of Clavicus Vile

The cave also features the [shrine](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric_Shrines "Skyrim:Daedric Shrines") to the [Daedric Prince](/wiki/Lore:Daedric_Princes "Lore:Daedric Princes") [Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile").

## Related Quests

- **[A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend")**: Help [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas") reunite with his [master](/wiki/Lore:Clavicus_Vile "Lore:Clavicus Vile").
- **[Culling the Beast](/wiki/Skyrim:Culling_the_Beast "Skyrim:Culling the Beast")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Kill the thin-blooded [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The entrance is in a pass through the snow-covered mountains that leads between Helgen and [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead"). To the left of the main entrance are three unusable barrels and an empty cart, while on the ground in front of the entrance are splattered blood stains. There is also a second entrance, in the mountains to the northwest of the main entrance. However, this cannot be used as a practical entrance, due to spears blocking progress a short distance into the cave when entered from that direction.

### Haemar's Cavern

The entrance leads into a natural tunnel, which after a few paces turns south. The passage opens into a chamber featuring a large wooden scaffold opposite, with two [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels beneath it. There is a [vampire thrall](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Thrall "Skyrim:Vampire Thrall") at the top of the structure. A wooden ramp leads up to a small table and chair, with three loose [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on the table. Next to the table is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). The way forward is to the east. The passage takes several turns before opening into another chamber. There is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") at the top of a wooden ramp which triggers a [spike wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap, and a leveled vampire patrolling the bottom of the ramp.

The ramp leads down to a campfire with a small table and chair facing away from you; a vampire thrall sits at this table, which has gory human bones in bowls on top. There is a charred skeever on a spit cooking over the fire, which can be harvested for a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"). Behind the campfire are two food barrels and a raised wooden platform in the southern corner of the room, where a leveled vampire is standing. On the platform, on the left is a small table and chair covered in blood holding an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"). Next to this table is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), with a cupboard next to the pot holding a filled [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and copies of *[The "Madmen" of the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_%22Madmen%22_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:The \"Madmen\" of the Reach")*, *[Ruins of Kemel-Ze](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruins_of_Kemel-Ze "Skyrim:Ruins of Kemel-Ze")*, *[Biography of Barenziah, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v1 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v1")*, *[Biography of Barenziah, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Biography_of_Barenziah,_v2 "Skyrim:Biography of Barenziah, v2")*, and *[The Song of Pelinal, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v1 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v1")* on the shelves. To the right of the cupboard is an unlocked chest. Farther to the right is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), and another small table and two chairs with an iron dagger on top. Above the lab is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from a rack, with a pheasant on the floor underneath, both of which can be harvested. Under the ramp are two sets of shelves holding a random helmet, a bowl of frost salts, a bowl of void salts, a random healing potion, a random magicka potion, and two further random potions. There are also two coffins under and on the platform. The exit from the cave is to the west, passing on your right yet another table, this one with a dead [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_(dead) "Skyrim:Imperial (dead)") and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on top and an iron dagger beneath it.

The passage turns and continues to descend before opening into another chamber with two levels. Around the outside where you enter is a raised level, while in the middle is a lower level. There is a wattle fence around the edge of the drop, with a leveled vampire on your right and a vampire thrall on your left patrolling the top level. There is also a leveled vampire on the lower level who may be alerted to any fighting. On the upper level is a tunnel to the south leading to a small room, which contains a set of shelves holding a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), a [potion of ultimate magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Magicka"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a food sack, and copies of *[The Real Barenziah, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v3 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v3")*, and *[v4](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Real_Barenziah,_v4 "Skyrim:The Real Barenziah, v4")*. To the southwest is a small table holding an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and against the west wall is an adept-locked chest. There are also two empty hanging cages and three coffins in the room.

Back in the two-level cave, there is a wooden ramp down to the lower level in the northwest corner. Following the ramp down, you will see that it splits to the left and right. To the left, the ramp continues down to a tunnel heading north into the next zone, *Haemar's Shame*. To the right is a table and chair, with a leveled vampire sitting in the chair unless they've already been dealt with. There are three dead [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(dead) "Skyrim:Bandit (dead)") between the bottom of the ramp and the table. If you alert the vampire sitting at the table at any point, they may raise these bandits to aid them in the fight. On the table are two ruined books, two random potions of healing, a [deadly aversion to magic poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Deadly_Aversion_to_Magic "Skyrim:Deadly Aversion to Magic"), and copies of *[Antecedants of Dwemer Law](/wiki/Skyrim:Antecedants_of_Dwemer_Law "Skyrim:Antecedants of Dwemer Law")* and the [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Response to Bero's Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Response_to_Bero%27s_Speech "Skyrim:Response to Bero's Speech")*. There are two sets of shelves behind the table holding copies of *[Aedra and Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Aedra_and_Daedra "Skyrim:Aedra and Daedra")*, *[Dwemer Inquiries Vol III](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Inquiries_Vol_III "Skyrim:Dwemer Inquiries Vol III")*, *[Song of the Askelde Men](/wiki/Skyrim:Song_of_the_Askelde_Men "Skyrim:Song of the Askelde Men")*, and *[Mixed Unit Tactics](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixed_Unit_Tactics "Skyrim:Mixed Unit Tactics")*, as well as a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and a ruined book. There is another set of shelves to the right of the table holding copies of *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")*, *[Ancestors and the Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestors_and_the_Dunmer "Skyrim:Ancestors and the Dunmer")*, two copies of *[Chance's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Chance%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Chance's Folly")*, *[The Song of Pelinal, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v5 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v5")*, *[Mystery of Talara, v 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v_1 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v 1")*, *[The Wolf Queen, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v7 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v7")*, *[Brief History of the Empire, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v3 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v3")*, and *[Brief History of the Empire, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v4 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v4")*, as well as three ruined books. There is also a bench and two coffins nearby. Return to the north and take the exit to *Haemar's Shame*.

### Haemar's Shame

Following the tunnel east, then south, it opens into a chamber containing a [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"); once it is dealt with, there are two spider [egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sac "Skyrim:Egg Sac") that can be harvested. Another tunnel continues to the south, turning twice before opening into a room with several hanging cages, a table holding an iron dagger and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), and a second table with a built-in [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") and a random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). There is also an unlocked chest and a set of shelves opposite; on the shelves are copies of *Antecedants of Dwemer Law*, *[Brief History of the Empire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v1 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v1")*, *Brief History of the Empire, v4*, *[The City of Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_City_of_Stone "Skyrim:The City of Stone")*, and *[Spirit of Nirn](/wiki/Skyrim:Spirit_of_Nirn "Skyrim:Spirit of Nirn")*, as well as another iron dagger. The tunnel continues west then back to the east, following a stream, with a vampire thrall patrolling the area.

The passage turns south, west, and south again, finally opening into another two-level cave. On a ledge ahead is the shrine of [Clavicus Vile](/wiki/Skyrim:Clavicus_Vile "Skyrim:Clavicus Vile"), while a leveled vampire is to your left. The boss and one other vampire will be at the bottom near the front of the shrine, with the final vampire up the stairs behind the shrine. A dead bandit is near the bottom of the earthen ramp that leads down to the bottom level, while a dead Imperial in front of the shrine may be raised by the vampires. Once the enemies have been dealt with, you will find in front of the shrine a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a haunch of [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat"), and two stone bowls containing two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and seven [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"). Stairs on either side of the shrine lead up to a raised area behind the shrine, where an unlocked boss-level chest and a shortcut exit are found. The exit is blocked by spears, which are lowered by a chain on the right.

## Notes

-  If you enter the dungeon via the shortcut exit, you will find spears blocking your way. However, if you reload the freshly created autosave with the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), the spears will be lowered for a moment before being raised again. You can use a word of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") to get past the spears during this brief window of time, thus skipping the entire dungeon.
- Prior to the start of the quest [A Daedra's Best Friend](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Daedra%27s_Best_Friend "Skyrim:A Daedra's Best Friend"), the statue of Clavicus Vile has a dog, [Barbas](/wiki/Skyrim:Barbas "Skyrim:Barbas"), at his side. During the quest, the dog disappears from the statue, but returns once the quest is complete.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

- The game may crash in this location if you have completed A Daedra's Best Friend.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.

| HagRockRedoubtExterior, HagRockRedoubtExterior02, HagRockRedoubtExterior03, HagRockRedoubt01 | |

| [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") | |
| Location | |
| South of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") East of [Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock") | |
| Special Features | |

| # of [Tanning Racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning "Skyrim:Tanning") | 2 |
| # of [Forges/Anvils](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") | 1 |
| # of [Workbenches](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") | 1 |
| # of [Wood Chopping Blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") | 1 |

Hag Rock Redoubt

**Hag Rock Redoubt** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). It contains only one zone, *[Hag Rock Redoubt](#Hag_Rock_Redoubt)*.

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah").
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader.
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The redoubt is a multi-tiered structure with multiple entrances and exits on different levels of the mountain. You must go through at least the exterior section in order to reach [Dead Crone Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Crone_Rock "Skyrim:Dead Crone Rock").

As you approach the site, there is a typical Nordic tower in front of you and a path leading past it to the south with tall arches high above. There is a Forsworn standing just outside an open doorway to the tower. Inside, stairs lead up and out the back to a wooden ramp winding up to the next level. Here there are another leveled Forsworn, an empty set of shelves, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), an unowned bedroll, and some [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels. In front of the shelves is an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") (The Dagger may also be on the table next to the helmet and sword on the level above the shelves). There are wooden stairs leading up to a level with parts of the floor missing and a wooden table on the far side of a gap. On the table are a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") and [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). There are stairs up to the highest level, where there is a stone walkway to the start of a Forsworn encampment. There are many [juniper trees](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") around the encampment.

Opposite towards the right is a Forsworn tent with a leveled magic-using Forsworn lying on a hay pile and hanging above a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"). In front of the tent are a campfire and a wooden table with three random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on top. Beside the tent to the left is a rack with a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), with a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") to the right. To the left of the walkway is a stone hut containing a leveled Forsworn, a set of shelves, an adept-locked chest, and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"). On the shelves are a random potion each of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), and [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and two [apothecary's satchels](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). Behind the stone hut are stairs leading up to more terraces with [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") strung across the stairs, with each terrace guarded by several Forsworn. To the left of the hut is the main path seen previously with the high arches overhead with more Forsworn patrolling, and also the lowest entrance to the interior.

The next terrace has a Forsworn tent at the top of the stairs containing a hay pile, a food barrel, and a random potion of magicka, with a campfire in front and an empty pot hanging over it. To the right is a wooden block with a woodcutter's axe on top, and to the left is a rack with two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from it. There are also two tables, a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), an [anvil](/wiki/Skyrim:Anvil "Skyrim:Anvil"), and two [tanning racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") in this area. One table has a [Forsworn bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Bow "Skyrim:Forsworn Bow"), a quiver of [Forsworn arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Arrow "Skyrim:Forsworn Arrow"), and a random [potion of true shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot") on top, while the other has a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"), a [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"), and a random potion of stamina on top. To the right of the next set of stairs is a lean-to with an unowned bedroll under it and a campfire in front. Farther to the right is the lower of the alternative exits from the interior.

There is another flight of stairs up to the next terrace with a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers a [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") trap at the bottom and a walkway over them. To the left of the stairs are two Forsworn tents, each containing a hay pile and the second also containing a table and chair, while to the right is another stone hut over a wooden spiral staircase leading up from the highest exit from the interior. One final flight of stairs leads up to the top terrace where a [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") and a [monster](/wiki/Skyrim:Monsters "Skyrim:Monsters") are inside another Forsworn tent. The tent contains an unlocked chest. If the monster is a giant [frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), it can get stuck in the tent, allowing for easy dispatch. From this terrace there is a path heading south to stairs leading up to the entrance to Dead Crone Rock.

### Hag Rock Redoubt

The easiest entry point will be the door on the lowest level of Hag Rock Redoubt labeled "Hag Rock Redoubt Ruin" (one of three such doors in the exterior area). This will normally be the first door you come to when approaching Hag Rock Redoubt. Once inside, your way up to the first level of the redoubt is lit by a brazier. Three Forsworn are found at the top of the incline, one patrolling and two dining at the table in the room to the right. Once you have the place to yourself, head to the dining table to retrieve the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Last Seed, v8](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Last_Seed,_v8 "Skyrim:2920, Last Seed, v8")* and two potions. Also find a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). To the left of the table, behind the pillar, a sample of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") is on a crate, with a bucket beside it containing two samples of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers") and an iron dagger. Due east from the table in a darkened alcove is an adept-locked chest.

To the north is a flight of wooden spiral stairs leading up to a jail area containing one leveled Forsworn guarding two adept-locked cells. The guard is sitting at the top of the stairs beside a cupboard holding an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"), an iron dagger, a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flower, a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), and a [Hag Rock Ruin Jail key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Ruin_Jail_Key "Skyrim:Hag Rock Ruin Jail Key"). The key will only open the cell directly across from the entrance on the west wall, which unfortunately yields nothing of interest. Beside the cupboard is a bucket containing two samples of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"). The second cell is to the left of the entrance, to the south. Inside are the body of a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and a random potion of magicka. There is an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus growing among a cave-in to the left of this cell. Past the jail area is another passage heading north which takes a couple turns and ends at a wooden door.

Through the door is a Forsworn Briarheart's quarters. Most likely he will have his back to you working at an alchemy lab as you approach, allowing for an advanced sneak attack. On the stone table along with the lab are a random potion of healing, as well as a cast iron pot and a wooden bowl containing two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales") and three [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") between them. To the right of the stone table is a boss level chest, and beside that is a small round wooden table with a sample of [Jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a sample of [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"), and another slaughterfish egg. To the left of the alchemy lab are a food barrel with three sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") on top and a long wooden table with an iron dagger on top and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") underneath. Also in the room are an unowned bedroll by the south wall, a wooden block against the north wall with a rabbit on top, and a cupboard against the east wall. On the shelves of the cupboard are a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle"), a bulb of garlic, a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), and two random potions.

To the left of the cupboard is a wooden door leading to an iron door that leads back outside via the lower of the two exits. Almost directly across from the cupboard, facing west, is a hallway that splits into two passages. Straight ahead is a sideboard, on top of which is an apprentice-[trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") chest that triggers a [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from the floor unless disarmed before opening. If you notice the arrangement of the spear receptacles on the floor, you will be able to avoid the trap by standing to the far right or left of the chest and flush against the sideboard. The cupboard shelf below the chest holds a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"), a bowl of bone meal, another sample of creep cluster, a [blue dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing"), and an open crate containing two pieces of [quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore"). The left-hand passage leads up stairs to an iron door that leads back outside via the higher of the two exits. Waiting outside the second exit are the Forsworn Briarheart and a monster, unless you previously dealt with all of the external Forsworn and the monster.

## Bugs

- The Hag Rock Ruin Jail Key unlocks only one of the two jail cell doors.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

Hag's End

**Hag's End** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") west of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing a [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"), [hags](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag "Skyrim:Hag"), and [witches](/wiki/Skyrim:Witch "Skyrim:Witch"). It contains only one zone, *[Hag's End](#Hag.27s_End)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Once inside, a hagraven will engage you in combat and teleport to different rooms as you deal damage to her and kill her minions.

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Hagravens) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Hagravens)")**: Do a favor for [Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund"), the Jarl of Markarth, by retrieving a [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrolfdir%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Hrolfdir's Shield"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Locate the Assassin of Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Locate_the_Assassin_of_Old "Skyrim:Locate the Assassin of Old")**: Find the Dark Brotherhood [Assassin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin").
- **[The Words of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Words_of_Power "Skyrim:The Words of Power")**: Follow the [Greybeards](/wiki/Skyrim:Greybeards "Skyrim:Greybeards")' advice to learn a [Word of Power](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_of_Power "Skyrim:Word of Power") from a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Hag's End is found within [Deepwood Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Vale "Skyrim:Deepwood Vale"), which is only accessible via [Deepwood Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deepwood_Redoubt "Skyrim:Deepwood Redoubt"). The entrance to the redoubt is in the mountains west of Dragon Bridge, south of the barrow [Volskygge](/wiki/Skyrim:Volskygge "Skyrim:Volskygge").

### Hag's End

First floor

Upon entering, to your right is a lit brazier atop a stand and to your left is a sideboard with a shelf. On the sideboard are a sample of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and a [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk"). Opposite you is a stone table with a [cup](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") on it. The corridor ends at an unlocked iron door on the left. Through the door is a dining hall, where you will encounter the hagraven leader and two witches. Once you initiate the fight, a third witch will run into the room from the room on the left. After you have dealt some damage to the hagraven, she will teleport to a room on the third floor. In the dining room is a very long table with a total of eleven chairs along the sides. On the table are a [sabre cat snow pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Snow_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Snow Pelt"), a [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt"), two [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), a stone bowl that contains a [hagraven claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), and two wooden plates, one with a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), and one with a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"). On your left is a wooden door to what looks like a bedroom. To the right of the door are a sideboard and, on the floor, a stone bowl which contains a horker tusk. On the sideboard are a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk"), a horker tusk, and a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). To the right of the sideboard is a cupboard with nothing of interest. At the far end of the room is another wooden door with a path heading northeast. In the middle of the southeast wall is a fireplace with a [cooking](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") pot in front of it. On your right as you first enter the room is a stone bench, and to the left is a stack of three barrels and three sacks.

As you enter the bedroom, on your left there is a stone table with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") inset. To the left is a [potion of plentiful magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), and to the right is a bowl of bone meal. There are five single beds in the room; between the second and third from the left is a [horse hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Hide "Skyrim:Horse Hide") on a piece of rubble, and between the third and fourth is a random pair of boots. There is an end table to the left of the fifth bed. Between the fifth bed and the door is a sideboard, on which are some [mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Mage Robes") and a random potion of healing. In the middle of the room is a double sideboard with a lit brazier on top. Around the brazier are a [scroll of Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Firebolt "Skyrim:Scroll of Firebolt"), a pair of random gauntlets, and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

Through the door to the northeast is a short corridor with a flight of stairs up on your right-hand side. Ahead is a room with snow; be careful as there are also three [frost runes](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Rune "Skyrim:Frost Rune") on the floor, one ahead and one to either side. At the rear of the room is a random piece of chest armor on a broken table with a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") just in front of it against the wall, and in the snow at the back of the room is a bowl. Against the north wall is a broken sideboard with a mead barrel, a bowl, and a burial urn on top, with a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from a rack above. To the left as you enter the room is a bookcase containing a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). There is a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") to the right of the bookcase. There are a set of shelves, two barrels, and a small set of shelves on the right as you enter, but they hold nothing of interest, except a bowl on the larger set of shelves. Be careful when activating the runes, as they will blow everything around the room.

At the top of the flight of stairs is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") activating a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") from your left. To the left is a stand holding an empty random soul gem. In front of you is a sideboard with a statue above it; on the sideboard are two burial urns and an apprentice-[trapped](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") chest which activates a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") fired from the statue in front of you. The path continues to the southwest up a few steps to an unlocked wooden door.

Hagraven and witches

Opening the door will reveal the hagraven sitting on her throne with two witches sitting facing her on either side. Again once you have dealt enough damage, the hagraven will teleport to a higher level. Initiating the fight will alert others to your presence; however, they can not get into the room until you drop a wooden bridge, which is on your right as you enter the room, with the lever to the right of the bridge. On your left as you enter is a stone table with a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, Part 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_Part_4 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, Part 4")*. There are four benches at an angle in front of the throne. Against the southeast wall are two sideboards on top of each other with a random potion of healing on top.

The Dark Brotherhood Assassin

Behind the throne is a hidden room in which you can find an unlocked boss chest and the [Assassin of Old](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood_Assassin "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood Assassin"). The switch used to enter this hidden room is right behind the throne, but it will not appear until you have started the associated quest (see [Notes](#Notes) for 3 workarounds).

As you cross the wooden bridge, be careful not to alert a hag that is just out of sight to the left of the corridor ahead. On the other side of the bridge the corridor climbs a few steps, and then there is an iron door on your left with a lit brazier opposite. In this room will be a hag, unless you have already dealt with it. A large frostbite spider will also descend from above in the center of the room and attack as soon as you enter the room. There are stone benches on either side of the entrance, with two bookcases along the southeast wall. The first has nothing of interest, but the second has a horse hide, a random helmet, and on top an [ice wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Ice Wolf Pelt"). To the right is a throne, with a fireplace nearby. On a small wall shelf to the right of the fire, you will find the [Hag's End key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag%27s_End_Key "Skyrim:Hag's End Key"). There are a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* and a random poison on a sideboard against the west wall, and at least seven hagraven feathers in the straw in the center of the room.

Back in the corridor and continuing to the northwest, past a stone table and after climbing a few more stairs, you come to a junction. To your left is a master-locked gate that will unlock with the Hag's End key, and on your right is a dropped gate with a handle to its left. Through the locked gate, past a statue on either side is an unlocked expert-trapped chest with a [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") to the right hiding the tension cable trapping the chest, with a random shield to the left. There are also dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") that can be looted in alcoves to either side of the chest. The trap on the chest activates [flamethrowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Flamethrower_Statues "Skyrim:Flamethrower Statues") from the two statues and from a third in the ceiling.

Oil slick

Return to the corridor and pull the handle to open the gate. Wait a few seconds before moving forward, as pulling the handle will also activate [spear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap") from either side; there is a series of three gates that open one after the other a few seconds apart, with more spear traps between each gate. At the top of the stairs you enter a room with the hagraven, a witch, and a hag. Like before, dealing enough damage to the hagraven will cause it to teleport farther up the ruin. After dealing with the other two enemies, you can explore the room. Things may get blown around this room during the fight, but there is a filled random soul gem and an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") on your right as you enter, among some rubble. There is an expert-locked iron door on the left against the northwest wall. There are two burial urns, one on either side of a raised area, with a plinth that has a *[Spell Tome: Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Flames "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Flames")*, and also an urn on the near side beside the burial urn. There are many candles lit on the floor arranged in circles around the room. Opposite the iron door is a path blocked by a lowered gate. In the southern corner of the room is a small empty alcove blocked by an expert-locked gate. To the right is a second empty petty soul gem, and beside this is a stone bowl with a second filled random soul gem inside. Behind the iron door is a small area with a burial urn, a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), a plate, a random helmet, and a potion of minor healing. There is also an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") at the top of the pillar that can be shot down to set fire to the [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slick "Skyrim:Oil Slick") in the large circle in the middle of the room. Finally, there is a central pillar with a chain that activates the closed gate on the southeast wall. There is also a [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem") on some pots to the left of this pillar.

Word wall

Activating the chain will open the closed gate to the southeast and also a second gate at the far end of the pathway. This path has alcoves for the dead on either side, but no draugr; there is only a burial urn in an alcove on the right. At the top you enter a room with the [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") off to the right and stairs in front of you with an iron door opposite leading back outside, and a stone table on the left covered in blood and decapitated [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). In the eastern corner is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). In the western corner is a burial urn that has nearly been completely buried in snow. The word wall teaches you part of the [Slow Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Slow_Time "Skyrim:Slow Time") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). There is nothing else of interest in this large room.

Final confrontation atop Hag's End

Exiting through the iron door opposite brings you out onto a balcony above Deepwood Vale and the final showdown with the hagraven. As soon as you exit, the hagraven will summon two frostbite spiders or ice wraiths, depending on your level, but they will not disappear when the hagraven dies and must be dealt with separately. Once they are all dealt with, there is a stone table in the middle of the balcony with a dead witch laid out on top. Beside her is a unique weapon called [Bloodthorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthorn "Skyrim:Bloodthorn"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") with a three-second [soul trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)") enchantment. There are also three hagraven feathers and a sample of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") on the table. On the northern end of the precipice is the boss leveled chest for this location.

Once you've dispensed with everything, work your way over to the waterfall (on the right, facing out to the vale) using [mountain climbing](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") or one word of [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). There is an expert-locked chest with decent loot with a pair of unique boots, [Predator's Grace](/wiki/Skyrim:Predator%27s_Grace "Skyrim:Predator's Grace"), next to the chest. Note the [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") nearby.

## Notes

- If you don't want to enter Hag's End but want Bloodthorn and both boss chests, you can climb the steep hillside to the left of the door to the building and reach the top of the waterfall, where the Predator's Grace, quicksilver ore vein, and first boss chest are. Afterward, you can head far left on the hill and get as close to the platform of Hag's End as possible, then leap over near the other boss chest. From there, you can loot the other boss chest and Bloodthorn.
- The hagraven's teleportation is scripted, and will always occur if you attempt to attack it using any means. However, it is possible to kill the hagraven before she teleports if wielding Mehrunes' Razor. If you manage to kill her before she teleports, she will appear dead at the top of Deepwood Vale.
- It is possible to obtain the Ancient Shrouded Armor without starting the quest or if you finish [Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroy_the_Dark_Brotherhood! "Skyrim:Destroy the Dark Brotherhood!") instead. Take [Serana](/wiki/Skyrim:Serana "Skyrim:Serana") with you into Hag's End and during the fight with the first set of witches, she will resurrect the body of the Dark Brotherhood Assassin, who will join you. When he turns to ash, loot the ash pile for the entire set of Ancient Shrouded Armor.
  - Another option without Serana is to have [the Ritual Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ritual_Stone "Skyrim:The Ritual Stone") activated. In the room where the second encounter with the hagraven occurs, stand as close as possible to the stone wall behind the throne and active the power of The Ritual Stone. Exit the area and the corpse of the Dark Brotherhood Assassin will be reanimated and following you. Kill him and to loot the armor from the remains.
  - Another version that doesn't require Serana or a Standing Stone power is simply to glitch through the sealed door via a plate pressed up against it and running against it or using [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint"). Once inside, grab his armor and the loot in the chest and then glitch back out via the same plate method.

## Bugs

- After getting the first word of the Slow Time shout from elsewhere, the word wall may not work properly. The wall's sound effects can be heard, but no word is learned when the wall is approached.
  -  You can use the console command `player.teachword 48ACB` to learn the second word (or `48ACC` for the third word).
- The oil slick doesn't appear. **?**
- If you soul trap the hagraven before the final encounter with the [Black Star](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Star "Skyrim:The Black Star") empty, the hagraven will teleport away and you will permanently lose the Black Star. **?**
- If you manage to kill the hagraven in the first room, there is a chance she will not appear at the end of the dungeon, though you can hear her teleporting ahead. **?**
- After the hagraven disappears in the first room, moving through the hallways may cause a crash to desktop when her spawn in the next room is triggered. **?**
- Even if you manage to kill and possibly soul-trap the hagraven in one of the interior rooms, she will still appear on the final balcony and you will have to deal with (and optionally soul-trap) her again. She may also reappear in one of the Forsworn tents at ground level, where she will be paralyzed and can be "killed" (and soul-trapped) again.
- Clearing out this dungeon and then starting Locate the Assassin of Old may cause the Dark Brotherhood Assassin's corpse to disappear.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Hail Sithis!

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Dark Brotherhood.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Dark_Brotherhood.png) | **One of the biggest [contracts](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") in [Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") history is yours to fulfill.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") |
| Location(s): | [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") docks, [The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah") |
| Reward: | 20,000 gold, [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") |
| ID: | DB11 |
| Suggested Level: | 6 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate") | **Next →** [Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head..."), [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Death Incarnate](/wiki/Skyrim:Death_Incarnate "Skyrim:Death Incarnate") | | → Next | [Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head...](/wiki/Skyrim:Where_You_Hang_Your_Enemy%27s_Head... "Skyrim:Where You Hang Your Enemy's Head..."), [The Dark Brotherhood Forever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dark_Brotherhood_Forever "Skyrim:The Dark Brotherhood Forever") | | |

Alone with the Emperor at last...

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to Whiterun and talk to [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre").
2. Knowing the true Emperor's location, travel to [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")'s docks.
3. *(Optional)* Kill [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro").
4. Board [The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah").
5. Kill [Emperor Titus Mede II](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)").
6. Return to Amaund to learn the location of the dead drop.
7. *(Optional)* Kill Amaund Motierre to fulfill the Emperor's dying wish.
8. Travel to [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud") to collect your reward.
9. Return to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") at the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary").

### Time to Settle the Score

Despite the devastation wrought on the Dark Brotherhood, the [Night Mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Mother "Skyrim:Night Mother") wants you to finish your contract and kill the Emperor, [Titus Mede II](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)"). The real Emperor's whereabouts are unknown, so travel to [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and find [Amaund Motierre](/wiki/Skyrim:Amaund_Motierre "Skyrim:Amaund Motierre") in his room at [The Bannered Mare](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bannered_Mare "Skyrim:The Bannered Mare"). Amaund will reveal that the true Emperor is on board his ship, [The Katariah](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Katariah "Skyrim:The Katariah"), near [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude")'s docks. Amaund will also inform you that [Commander Maro](/wiki/Skyrim:Commander_Maro "Skyrim:Commander Maro") is outside the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse") at the docks, should you wish to exact revenge.
Go to the East Empire Company Warehouse, near Solitude. Commander Maro will be standing on the dock. If you approach him, he will be startled by your appearance and proceed to attack. This will allow you to kill him without incurring a bounty, and the nearby guards may even assist you if you allow Maro to make the first strike. Alternatively, kill Maro from a distance or sneak up to him and kill him stealthily. It's worth noting that Maro has his own faction, so any bounty you incur when attacking him will be lost on his death. You can, if you wish, ignore Maro completely and move on to the next objective.

### Bringing Down an Empire

The Katariah

The next target is the true Emperor, aboard his ship The Katariah, moored out to the north of the city in a channel called the Solitude Inlet. Security has been relaxed somewhat, as the [Penitus Oculatus](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus") believes that the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") has been completely eradicated. Nonetheless, many bodyguards are still present on the ship. Access the ship underwater by using the anchor to climb aboard. On board the ship are sailors and [Penitus Oculatus Agents](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Agent "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Agent"), both of which are relatively weak and easy to defeat. You can fight your way through the ship or simply sneak through, as few guards will be patrolling the hallways and can all be picked off quite easily, though some will attack with both sword and shock spells. You will not earn a bounty for killing or being seen by anyone on board.

You can also traverse the upper deck, which contains many guards. A unique sword, [Windshear](/wiki/Skyrim:Windshear "Skyrim:Windshear"), can be found at the very end of the bowsprit - the slanted mast at the ship's bow. *[King](/wiki/Skyrim:King "Skyrim:King")*, a [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books"), can be found next to the throne, on the highest part of the ship's deck. [Captain Avidius](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Avidius "Skyrim:Captain Avidius") and [Lieutenant Salvarus](/wiki/Skyrim:Lieutenant_Salvarus "Skyrim:Lieutenant Salvarus") are also present on the ship, both in their individual private quarters, and are somewhat tougher than the other guards. They both carry a [Katariah Master Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Katariah_Master_Key "Skyrim:Katariah Master Key"), which will open all doors on the ship, including the Emperor's Quarters. There is another master key on a hook in the captain's quarters, just to the side of the door.

### An Honorable Man

Enter the Emperor's Quarters. Whether you came in sneaking or not, the Emperor will greet you straight away, as he has been expecting you. He will acknowledge that it is his destiny to die by your hand, and will not fight you. He asks, however, for you to listen for a moment before killing him. You can, if you want, kill the Emperor instantly, or hear what he has to say. The Emperor simply asks that you consider killing the person who masterminded his assassination, as he feels that his intentions could be malevolent. After slaying the Emperor and finally completing this arduous contract, take a look around his quarters. There are some rare books lying about and some very expensive gems and jewelry behind a locked door, which can be opened with the key the Emperor holds. The unique [Gilded Wristguards](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilded_Wristguards "Skyrim:Gilded Wristguards") and an extra set of the [Emperor's Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Emperor's Robes") are also to be found. There is even a [book on the third era](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v2 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v2"), which tells about [Empress Katariah](/wiki/Lore:Katariah "Lore:Katariah"), after whom the ship was named.

### A Hard-Earned Reward

Use the Emperor's key to exit the ship and return to Whiterun to speak to Amaund. He will reveal that the money for the contract is in a dead drop inside the cavern where you first met, in [Volunruud](/wiki/Skyrim:Volunruud "Skyrim:Volunruud"). After informing Amaund of the Emperor's death, you may speak to him again to say that you have unfinished business with him, but he does not comprehend what you mean by your cryptic words and will not attack you. You may kill him if you wish to fulfill the Emperor's last wish. If you do, a surprised Amaund's last words will be, *"But... we had a deal..."* Amaund's corpse can be looted for a significant amount of gems. However, if you do not wish to kill Amaund, the gems may be easily pickpocketed from him.

Go to Volunruud and the chamber where you first met Amaund. Inside, you will find a normal chest and an urn containing 20,000 gold. Return to the [Dawnstar Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Dawnstar Sanctuary") and speak to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") about the gold, and he will ask how much money you received. You can choose to lie to him, but you keep the entire reward regardless of the option you choose. [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir") will point out that [Delvin Mallory](/wiki/Skyrim:Delvin_Mallory "Skyrim:Delvin Mallory") of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") could assist in using the gold to restore the sanctuary.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked at the end of this quest:

-  **Hail Sithis!** (30 points/Silver)

## Notes

- The weapons found on the ship are level-dependent, with a chance of rare items being found.

## Bugs

- In the room with the alchemy lab, both a Penitus Oculatus guard and a sailor appear dead in their bed. This appears to be deliberate, as both their references have the **"Starts Dead"** box checked. However, due to their placement, they may end up clipping through their beds and end up either half-buried in them or clip completely through them, ending underneath.
- If you approach Maro for the first time after killing the Emperor, but before turning the quest in, he'll ignore you and neither attack nor talk.
- Sometimes, jumping on a table against the wall in the Emperor's chambers will cause you to fall through the ship into the water.
- Depending on how you kill him (such as with certain spells) the Emperor might end up getting stuck outside the wall of the cabin and you will be unable to loot him.
- Sometimes, on approaching Amaund Motierre in the Bannered Mare the first time, he will act as if he has already given you the information, and the only dialogue options will be the ones for after the Emperor has been killed. The quest marker will be stuck on him with no way to proceed. **?**
  - Advance the quest by entering in the console `setstage DB11 15`.
- If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capture Solitude, the [Penitus Oculatus Outpost](/wiki/Skyrim:Penitus_Oculatus_Outpost "Skyrim:Penitus Oculatus Outpost") will remain active in [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge"), which can result in Penitus Oculatus agents and [Stormcloak soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") engaging each other in combat.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, addresses this issue. If this quest and the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") questline for the Stormcloaks are finished, the Penitus Oculatus Outpost will be cleared out.
- The combat taunts from the guards on the ship may be the ones used against dragons or other targets, rather than you.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 4.3.4, addresses this issue. They weren't checking to see if the target was in the Dark Brotherhood.

## Quest Stages

| Hail Sithis! (DB11) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | The Night Mother has spoken to me once again. The true Emperor must be assassinated - the contract with Amaund Motierre must be completed. *Objective 5:* Talk to Nazir |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Talk to Amaund Motierre |
| 15 |  | *Objective 15:* Board the Katariah |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Kill the Emperor! |
| 40 |  | *Objective 40:* (Optional) Kill Commander Maro |
| 50 |  | *Objective 50:* Report to Amaund Motierre |
| 60 |  | *Objective 60:* Retrieve the payment |
| 70 |  | *Objective 70:* (Optional) Kill Amaund Motierre |
| 80 |  | *Objective 80:* Report to Nazir |
| 200 | ☑ | The Emperor has been assassinated. The Dark Brotherhood will, once more, be feared and respected the world over. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 1, 2, 3, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DB11 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DB11`.

# Skyrim:Haknir's Shoal

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Camp.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Camp.png) | Camp: Haknir's Shoal ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Haknir%27s+Shoal)) | | |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 10 |
| Occupants | |
| [Pirate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate "Skyrim:Pirate"), [Pirate Captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_Captain "Skyrim:Pirate Captain"), [Pirate Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_Mage "Skyrim:Pirate Mage") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Deathbrand Helm](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Helm "Skyrim:Deathbrand Helm") [Deathbrand Treasure Map](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Treasure_Map "Skyrim:Deathbrand Treasure Map") [East Empire Pendant](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2HaknirsShoalExterior01, DLC2HaknirsTreasurePOI02 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| North-northwest of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") East of [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Orichalcum](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore") | 2 |

Haknir's Shoal

**Haknir's Shoal** is a small [pirate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate "Skyrim:Pirate") [camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps") north-northwest of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").

## Related Quests

- **[Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)")**: Find the treasure of [Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand").
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

## Walkthrough

There be pirates!

The three pirates, comprising a [pirate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate "Skyrim:Pirate"), a [pirate mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_Mage "Skyrim:Pirate Mage"), and their [pirate captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_Captain "Skyrim:Pirate Captain"), will attack as soon as they detect you. Once you have taken care of them, you may loot the pirate captain for the [Deathbrand Treasure Map](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Treasure_Map "Skyrim:Deathbrand Treasure Map"). Obtaining the map will complete the miscellaneous quest to search for the treasure of [Haknir Death-Brand](/wiki/Skyrim:Haknir_Death-Brand "Skyrim:Haknir Death-Brand") and initiate the quest [Deathbrand](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_(quest) "Skyrim:Deathbrand (quest)").

A campfire is in the middle of the camp, with a wooden plate holding a [venison chop](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison_Chop "Skyrim:Venison Chop") beside the fire. There are three tents pitched around the fire. The tent nearest the small boat contains a bedroll only, and to the left of the tent is a firewood pile, a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). The middle tent contains a bedroll and a wooden plate holding a [grilled chicken breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Grilled Chicken Breast") and a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), while at the back of the tent is an expert-locked [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox"). To the west of this tent is a mead barrel on a rock with a random potion, three sacks, and a random healing potion beside it. The tent nearest land contains a bedroll, a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a pair of random light [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and two food sacks. Outside this tent on the left is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack").

The treasure

To the northwest of the campfire is an expert-locked ancient chest containing the [Deathbrand Helm](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbrand_Helm "Skyrim:Deathbrand Helm"). There are two [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") in the area: the first is west-northwest of the ancient chest, and the other is farther north at the tip of the isle. Scattered around the isle are nine [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Ashen Grass Pod") plants, a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant, three [pearl oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster"), and to the northeast a [clam](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam") that can be harvested for [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat"). There is a small boat at the edge of the water just northeast of the fire, with a random [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), two crates, four sacks, and a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") inside.

On the shoreline opposite the shoal are more spiky grass plants, two more Nirnroot plants, and a [horker](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker").

# Skyrim:Halbarn Favor Quest

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

[Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur") near his smelly forge

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur") in [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall").
2. Find ten [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") samples and fifteen [ebony ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony_Ingot "Skyrim:Ebony Ingot").
3. Give the items to Halbarn and collect your reward.

### After the Attack

Once the quest [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk") has been completed, the [Nord](/wiki/Lore:Nord "Lore:Nord") warriors of [Thirsk](/wiki/Lore:Thirsk "Lore:Thirsk") move back into [Thirsk Mead Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Thirsk_Mead_Hall "Skyrim:Thirsk Mead Hall"). However, during their lengthy exile in [Bujold's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Bujold%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Bujold's Retreat"), the invading [Rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling") turned the hall upside down, with much cleanup to be done. The blacksmith of the hall, [Halbarn Iron-Fur](/wiki/Skyrim:Halbarn_Iron-Fur "Skyrim:Halbarn Iron-Fur"), found his forge filled with slop and had to request assistance from [Elmus](/wiki/Skyrim:Elmus "Skyrim:Elmus") to clean it up. Despite the terrible smell coming from the flames, he is still able to do some work, although he has more problems: *"Cleaning out the forge was the easy part. But those blasted rieklings made off with most of my materials. And I can't forge air. You tend to wander around, don't you? If you come across any stalhrim or ebony in your travels, bring them back to old Halbarn. Help each other out."* This starts the quest and adds an objective to your journal. You will have to gather ten samples of [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") and fifteen [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") ingots for Halbarn. Note that you will have to keep count yourself, as the quest will not update.

### Stalhrim

The [Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source")

[Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim") can only be found on [Solstheim](/wiki/Lore:Solstheim "Lore:Solstheim"), in stalhrim deposits. They can only be mined using an [ancient Nordic pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nordic_Pickaxe "Skyrim:Ancient Nordic Pickaxe"), the reward for completing the quest [An Axe To Find](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Axe_to_Find "Skyrim:An Axe to Find"). Alternatively, you can buy one from [Baldor Iron-Shaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Baldor_Iron-Shaper "Skyrim:Baldor Iron-Shaper") in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). Baldor is also the only merchant that will sell you stalhrim, although he never sells more than four (75% chance each), so you will need to find some stalhrim deposits as well.

The very best source for collecting stalhrim is the [Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source"), a landmark in northwestern Solstheim. If you have completed the quest [A New Source of Stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Source_of_Stalhrim "Skyrim:A New Source of Stalhrim"), the deposit will be marked on your map. It is located south of [Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing") and east of [Bristleback Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback_Cave "Skyrim:Bristleback Cave") and [Broken Tusk Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tusk_Mine "Skyrim:Broken Tusk Mine"). With the ancient Nordic pickaxe in hand, take the trip to the Stalhrim Source, and start mining. You can gather thirty pieces of stalhrim there. For other sources, see [this article](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim "Skyrim:Stalhrim").

### Ebony Ingots

[Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine")

With only seven fixed [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") ingots in the entire game, you will be forced to do some mining and smelting to retrieve the requested amount. Two ebony ores are used to smelt one ebony ingot, meaning you will need at least thirty ebony ores. If you are level 27 or above, there is a chance that blacksmiths and general goods merchants will sell you ores and/or ingots, and an additional chance of looting ores from [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn"), but mining is probably the easiest method to achieve your goal. There are two options available. You can travel back to Skyrim and find the biggest source of ebony ore in the game, namely [Gloombound Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Gloombound_Mine "Skyrim:Gloombound Mine") in the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Narzulbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Narzulbur "Skyrim:Narzulbur"). With sixteen ore veins, the mine will net you 48 ebony ores, for a total of 24 ingots, which is more than enough to satisfy Halbarn.

However, it is also possible to avoid the trip to Skyrim and stay on Solstheim. If you have completed the quest [The Final Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Final_Descent "Skyrim:The Final Descent"), thus helping the townsfolk of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), the local [Raven Rock Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock_Mine "Skyrim:Raven Rock Mine") will be reopened and new ore veins discovered. This makes the mine the second best source for ebony ore in the game, with a total of nine ore veins, and after some smelting, thirteen ebony ingots. You can also travel to [Northshore Landing](/wiki/Skyrim:Northshore_Landing "Skyrim:Northshore Landing") and find the ebony ore vein a few feet south of the abandoned shack where [Old Salty](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Salty "Skyrim:Old Salty") resides, and travel to the landmark [Horker Island](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Island "Skyrim:Horker Island") where the named [horker](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"), [Lord Tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord_Tusk "Skyrim:Lord Tusk"), lives. Head to the northeastern shore of the island, where a boat has sunken completely, head west up the beach until you reach the ebony vein next to the cliff wall. Mine your ore and smelt it until you have the fifteen ebony ingots for Halbarn.

### The Reward

When you have gathered all the items, return to Thirsk Mead Hall and Halbarn. Hand him the materials and he will hand you a [medium amount of leveled gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Gold_Rewards "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") and be quite happy: *"Just in time, too. Kuvar was starting to give me some grief about his new armor. This will do the trick nicely. You come back if you ever want some fancier armor yourself, now."*

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2ThirskFFHalbarn stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2ThirskFFHalbarn`.

## Bugs

- The dialogue to start the quest may not appear after finishing [Retaking Thirsk](/wiki/Skyrim:Retaking_Thirsk "Skyrim:Retaking Thirsk"). **?**
  -  To fix this, enter the command: `setstage DLC2ThirskFFHalbarn 0`
- The objective text says "Stalhrim Ore" even though Stalhrim is enchanted ice, not metal.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, addresses this issue. The objective text is changed from "Bring 10 Stalhrim Ore and 15 Ebony Ingots to Halbarn" to "Bring 10 Stalhrim and 15 Ebony Ingots to Halbarn".
