Half-Moon Mill

**Half-Moon Mill** is a lumber mill that supplies [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen") and [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath"). It is operated by [Hert](/wiki/Skyrim:Hert "Skyrim:Hert") and [Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Hern "Skyrim:Hern"), who live in a small cabin across from the mill itself. It is located on the shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"), west of [The Lady Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lady_Stone "Skyrim:The Lady Stone"), east of [Hunter's Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter%27s_Rest "Skyrim:Hunter's Rest"), beside the road that leads north from Falkreath towards [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Hern "Skyrim:Hern") [†](#intnote_1)  [Hert](/wiki/Skyrim:Hert "Skyrim:Hert") |

[†](#note_1)Only during the quest [Kill Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern").

## Related Quests

- **[Chop Wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood")**: Get paid to chop firewood. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Hern "Skyrim:Kill Hern")**: Kill [Hern](/wiki/Skyrim:Hern "Skyrim:Hern"), a reclusive vampire.

### Exterior

The cabin and chicken coop

The property is adjacent to the road, beside a stone bridge that crosses a stream that is filled with tree trunks and branches as it flows from [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"). The stream splits the property and is rich in [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)"). The [wood mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log") and a butcher shack are on the east side of the stream, with a wooden bridge leading to the main cabin to the west. The butcher shack contains a table holding three haunches of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") and two joints of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef"). Hanging from the ceiling is a rack holding two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). Under the table are gory human remains, a possible clue as to the [true nature](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") of the mill's inhabitants. A [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull") is found on the ground as well.

The cabin is a single-story building with a small henhouse containing two chicken nests between the road and the cabin. In front of the cabin, near the stream, is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and opposite the henhouse are a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block") and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). There are several tree stumps around the property, harvested by the mill. At the rear of the property is a large [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") stuck in the ground beside it, and not far to the north is another iron ore vein. Near this is a tree stump containing a dead rabbit, a fork, and a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). Numerous plants and flowers may be found around the property. If the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found near the shore, along with a salmon rack and two [baskets](/wiki/Skyrim:Basket "Skyrim:Basket"). Fish from [Temperate Lakes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") can be caught here.

When speaking with [Hert](/wiki/Skyrim:Hert "Skyrim:Hert"), she will instruct you to grab an [axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), as she will pay you for [chopping wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood").

| Plants | Animals | Other |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 5 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  6 [Purple Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower")  7 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower")  2 [Thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") | 3 [Chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") | 2 [Chickens' Nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") |

### Half-Moon Mill

The interior of the cabin

The cabin itself is a single-room dwelling. Upon entry there is a chair and barrels on the left, against the southeast wall. Against the southwest wall is a cupboard holding only clutter, with more [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels next to it, mostly containing raw meats. A long wooden table and bench along the northwest wall holds a haunch of raw venison, a joint of raw beef, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), with two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") under the table. Hanging above the table are three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the right is a hanging rack holding three rabbits and three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). To the right of the table is a kettle containing three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and another food barrel. In the middle of the northwest wall is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a kettle on the hearth containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"). In front of the fireplace is a round wooden table and two chairs. On this table is a bottle of wine, a bottle of alto wine, and two [pheasant breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"). To the right of the fireplace, against the northwest wall, is a large owned double bed with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of it. Under the bed on the right-hand side is a copy of *[Physicalities of Werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Physicalities_of_Werewolves "Skyrim:Physicalities of Werewolves")*. In the northern corner is an end table holding a bottle of Nord mead. Against the southeast wall is a wardrobe and dresser, both containing common [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a food barrel between them.

## Notes

- You can buy [sawn logs](/wiki/Skyrim:Sawn_Log "Skyrim:Sawn Log")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") here after installing [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") by speaking to Hert. You can also cut your own for free if she has given permission to do so.
- When [building](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") a home with the Hearthfire add-on, your map marker may send you here to buy sawn logs. If Hert is dead, you may simply go to [another wood mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Mills "Skyrim:Wood Mills") to purchase lumber to clear the objective.
- To the northwest is a memorial pillar with a flag and the corpse of a [Dark Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf_(dead) "Skyrim:Dark Elf (dead)") lying beside it.
- In the northwest corner of Lake Ilinalta, north from Half-Moon Mill, is an unmarked fisherman's camp with a copy of the [one-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Fire and Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_and_Darkness "Skyrim:Fire and Darkness")*.
- Although the owners here are vampires themselves, they will still become hostile towards you if you are a [blood-starved vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampirism#Stages_of_Vampirism "Skyrim:Vampirism").

## Bugs

- The ownership on the double bed here is incorrectly assigned to RiverwoodSvensHouseFaction instead of HalfMoonMillFaction, preventing Hert and Hern from using it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Hall of Attainment

## Overview

|  |

| [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") | |

The interior of the Hall of Attainment

The **Hall of Attainment** is a hall in the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") where the student sleeping quarters are located.

This is one of two halls at the college, the other being the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance").

## Residents

| Ground Floor |
| --- |
| [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") †  [Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") [Spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Spells") [Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[Alteration (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Alteration (Master)") |
| Upper Floor |
| [Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") #  [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods") [Fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Fence") \*  [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") ‡  [Nirya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirya "Skyrim:Nirya") |

\* Becomes a [fence](/wiki/Skyrim:Fence_(merchant) "Skyrim:Fence (merchant)") only after completing [Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers") quest
† No longer a resident after completing [The Eye of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Eye_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Eye of Magnus") quest
‡ No longer a resident after completing [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus") quest
# No longer a resident after completing [Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor") quest

## Related Quests

- **[Aftershock](/wiki/Skyrim:Aftershock "Skyrim:Aftershock")**: Put an end to the rupture caused by the Eye of Magnus. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Alteration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Alteration Ritual Spell")**: Acquire [Kahvozein's Fang](/wiki/Skyrim:Kahvozein%27s_Fang "Skyrim:Kahvozein's Fang") and use it to get [heartscales](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Heartscales "Skyrim:Dragon Heartscales") from a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") for [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Brelyna's Practice](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna%27s_Practice "Skyrim:Brelyna's Practice")**: Help [Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon") by allowing her to practice her spells on you.
- **[J'zargo's Experiment](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo%27s_Experiment "Skyrim:J'zargo's Experiment")**: Help [a student](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo") test out a fiery new spell.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rejoining the College](/wiki/Skyrim:Rejoining_the_College "Skyrim:Rejoining the College")**: Make amends for breaking the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") rules.
- **[Tolfdir the Absent-Minded](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir_the_Absent-Minded "Skyrim:Tolfdir the Absent-Minded")**: Help [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") find his missing [alembic](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir%27s_Alembic "Skyrim:Tolfdir's Alembic").

### Ground Floor

Each floor is split into eight sections or cubicles. There are three cubicles on each side with the entrance and stairwell opposite each other and separating them downstairs. Upstairs the dining room and stairwell do the same. The stairwell continues up to an exit onto the roof, from which you can access a similar entrance at the top of the [Hall of Countenance](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Countenance "Skyrim:Hall of Countenance"), and there are two entrances to the [Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum"). These are on either side of the tower that reaches above the two halls. Most of the sleeping quarters contain barrels and sacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). There are also many bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). All wardrobes found within the hall contain various items of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). There are many pieces of fine crockery including [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), etc. throughout the hall. Items in cubicles that are assigned to specific people are generally owned and taking them will be considered stealing.

Upon entering the hall there are moth-eaten college banners on either side wall and a focal point that is releasing magical energy upwards in the center of the lower level of the tower. Proceeding clockwise around the floor the first cubicle is [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir")'s sleeping quarters. His cubicle contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with small bedside tables on either side of the bed. To the left is a tall wardrobe and a couple of chairs, while to the right on the floor are two [drums](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and a narrow wooden table against the wall with some [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on top. Above the table are two wall shelves holding three empty [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems")—one [common](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"), one [lesser](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem") and one [petty](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem")—as well as two [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers, a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), two [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), and a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat").

The second cubicle is [Brelyna Maryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Brelyna_Maryon "Skyrim:Brelyna Maryon")'s sleeping quarters and it contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with a small bedside table and chair on either side of it. To the left of the bed is an unlocked long [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and to the right are two tall wardrobes separated by a small wardrobe. On the cupboard are two filled soul gems, one common and one lesser. The third cubicle is [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund")'s sleeping quarters. It contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with a small cupboard to the left and an unlocked wooden chest to the right. On the left side of the bed are two small wardrobes separated by a tall wardrobe. On the smaller ones is a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), one red and two green apples. On the right of the bed are two chairs and a small round table with a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top.

Next is the stairwell with a few crates, barrels and straw bales at the bottom. The next cubicle is [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano")'s sleeping quarters, though he is never seen in the hall. It contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with empty small bedside tables on either side. To the left of the bed are two more bales of straw, while to the right are some crates, a tall wardrobe and an unlocked chest. The next cubicle is [J'zargo](/wiki/Skyrim:J%27zargo "Skyrim:J'zargo")'s sleeping quarters which contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with a small wardrobe on either side of the bed. To the left is an unlocked long chest. To the right are a pair of chairs separated by another tall wardrobe.

The final cubicle (the first one on the right when entering) is the sleeping quarters that are given to you when you first enter the College and begin the questline by gaining official access. It contains an unowned single bed coming out from the wall with small wardrobes on either side. The one on the left has a copy of *[Azura and the Box](/wiki/Skyrim:Azura_and_the_Box "Skyrim:Azura and the Box")* atop. To the left of the bed is a chair and small round table between several barrels and a small table by the doorway with a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), a bowl of [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust") and two [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth") on top. To the right are two tall wardrobes with a small wardrobe between. On the smaller wardrobe there is an empty common soul gem and three [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull") on top. By the doorway is another small table with three [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm") on top, and on the floor at the rear of the room is a basket containing five bottles of Nord mead.

### Upper Floor

There is a hole in the center of the room with the magical energies from below rising into the ceiling. Around this is a low wall to prevent accidental falls. The first cubicle is [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir")'s sleeping quarters, where he spends most of his time. There is an owned single bed coming out from the wall, with small bedside tables on either side and an unlocked chest at the foot of the bed. On the left of the bed is a set of shelves holding three common books, a copy of *[Souls, Black and White](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls,_Black_and_White "Skyrim:Souls, Black and White")*, ten bottles of Nord mead, six bottles of alto wine, and a bottle of wine (see [bugs](#Bugs)). To the left of the shelves is an unlocked chest, with a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") leaning against it. To the right of the bed are two chairs, with a tall wardrobe between them.

The next cubicle is a dining room with a long wooden table and bench filled with [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), and a narrow table to the right. Next is [Nirya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirya "Skyrim:Nirya")'s cubicle, with an owned single bed coming out of the wall, and small wardrobes on either side. To the left of the bed is a set of shelves, a chair, and a drum on a barrel. To the right of the bed are two tall wardrobes with a small wardrobe between them. On top of the small wardrobe is a large coin purse and a small coin purse. The next cubicle is unused, and contains a large vat, several barrels, and some crates. It is full of cobwebs. The next cubicle is [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine")'s sleeping quarters, with a single bed coming out from the wall, several straw bales to the left, and two crates and two unusable barrels to the right.

The next cubicle has a wooden bench along the rear wall, with a large round wooden table and chairs to the left, and a narrow table and more chairs to the right. On top of the first table are two common books. The final cubicle is [Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane")'s sleeping quarters, with an owned single bed coming out from the wall, with small wardrobes on either side. There is a large coin purse on the wardrobe to the left. Also to the left of the bed are two sets of shelves holding samples of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), and [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungus, a basket containing four [spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), three [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flowers, three ice wraith teeth, a sample of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), a bowl of frost salts, two deathbell flowers, and a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") (see [bugs](#Bugs)). To the right of the bed are two tall wardrobes with a small wardrobe between them. On top of the small wardrobe is a filled common soul gem, an empty petty soul gem, and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull").

## Notes

- The room that you are given contains four respawning food barrels. The other containers in that room are non-respawning and safe for storage.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. The food barrels no longer respawn.
- The inhabitants of the downstairs rooms may wander into each others' rooms as well as yours and use the furniture, sometimes at unusual times. For example, you may find Tolfdir sitting in Brelyna Maryon's room, seemingly watching her sleep.

## Bugs

- Two of the bottles of Nord mead and a bottle of alto wine are unowned.
- Several [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") are shown as unowned.
- At some point in the game, you may be unable to sleep or wait in the Hall of Attainment because you are "being asked to leave".
- There is an unowned bed in the Hall of Attainment that's supposed to be owned by Arniel Gane.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Hall of Countenance

## Overview

The interior of the Hall of Countenance

The **Hall of Countenance** is the main living and sleeping quarters for most of the higher ranked mages of the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)").

Several mages have their cubicles and beds in this area, including [Drevis Neloren](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren"), the master [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") [trainer](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Skyrim:Trainers"), and [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"), the master [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") trainer. It is one of two sleeping areas at the college, the other being the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment").

There is a trapdoor to [the Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden") at the bottom of the stairs and an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") upstairs. There is also an alchemy lab in Drevis Neloren's bedroom on the bottom floor.

The hall can be accessed via a doorway in the southern part of the courtyard.

## Related Quests

- **[Conjuration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Conjuration Ritual Spell")**: Find a [Sigil Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigil_Stone "Skyrim:Sigil Stone") by summoning a daedra and learn more about [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration").
- **[Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell")**: Learn the most powerful [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells Skyrim has to offer.
- **[Enchanting Pick-Up](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Pick-Up "Skyrim:Enchanting Pick-Up")**: [Sergius](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") wants you to pick up an item from a client for enchanting. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Illusion Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Illusion Ritual Spell")**: Find some books about [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") magic to further your Illusion skills.
- **[Out of Balance](/wiki/Skyrim:Out_of_Balance "Skyrim:Out of Balance")**: Purify the focus points for magical energy around the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
- **[Restocking Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Restocking_Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Restocking Soul Gems")**: Help [Sergius Turrianus](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") to fill his stock with [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems").
- **[Restoration Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Restoration Ritual Spell")**: Find the [Augur of Dunlain](/wiki/Skyrim:Augur_of_Dunlain "Skyrim:Augur of Dunlain") and learn more about [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") magic.

### Ground Floor

Each floor is split into eight sections or cubicles. There are three cubicles on each side with the entrance and stairwell opposite each other and separating them downstairs. Upstairs the dining room and stairwell do the same. The stairwell continues up to an exit onto the roof, from which you can access a similar entrance at the top of the *[Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment")*, there are two entrances to *[The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum")*. These are on either side of the tower that reaches above the two halls. Most of the sleeping quarters contain barrels and sacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). There are also many bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). All wardrobe found within the hall contain various items of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"). There are many pieces of fine crockery including [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), etc throughout the hall. Items in cubicles that are assigned to specific people are generally owned and taking them will be considered stealing.

Upon entering the hall there are college banners on either side wall and a focal point that is releasing magical energy upwards in the center of the lower level of the tower. Proceeding clock-wise around the floor the first cubicle is an unused bedroom with an unowned single bed coming out from the wall with small bedside tables on either side. On the table on the left is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). To the left of the bed is a tall wardrobe and two chairs. On the right is a set of shelves holding two samples of [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), and three [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers. To the right is a small cupboard with a three [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a filled [petty](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and [common](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") and an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem").

The second cubicle has a large vat, some crates and barrels. It is also one of only three possible location you will find [Tolfdir's Alembic](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir%27s_Alembic "Skyrim:Tolfdir's Alembic") you need to find in order to help [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir") in a repeatable [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir_the_Absent-Minded "Skyrim:Tolfdir the Absent-Minded"). The third is [Phinis Gestor's](/wiki/Skyrim:Phinis_Gestor "Skyrim:Phinis Gestor") sleeping quarters it contains an owned bed coming out from the wall with small cupboards on either side. The cupboard on the left has a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") and [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") on top and an unowned bottle of Nord mead on the floor in front. The cupboard on the right has a filled lesser soul gem, a medium coin purse and ten loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. To the left of the bed are two tall wardrobe separated by a set of shelves holding a small and medium coin purse, a [potion of enduring invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enduring_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Enduring Invisibility") hidden inside a basket, a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), a [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), a [potion of plentiful magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), a [potion of extra magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extra_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Extra Magicka"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), a [potion of resist magic](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Magic"), a [potion of brief invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility"), three [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), a [long taffy treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Taffy_Treat "Skyrim:Long Taffy Treat"), an [apple pie](/wiki/Skyrim:Apple_Pie "Skyrim:Apple Pie"), a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") and a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"). To the right of the bed is a narrow table with a couple of loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"). To the right is a chair with a plate of two [boiled creme treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat") on a barrel to the right.

Next is the stairwell with a trapdoor into *[The Midden](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Midden "Skyrim:The Midden")* at the bottom. Continuing around the next cubicle is [Drevis Neloren's](/wiki/Skyrim:Drevis_Neloren "Skyrim:Drevis Neloren") sleeping quarters and contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with end tables on either side, the one on the left has a small coin purse on top. To the left of the bed is an unlocked long [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") with two wall shelves above. These hold a [staff of magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magelight "Skyrim:Staff of Magelight"), three loose septims, five soul gems, two empty petty, two empty lesser and a filled common soul gem. To the right are two tall wardrobe separated by a small cupboard with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") on top and a wall shelf above. To the left is a barrel containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"), with two [torchbug thoraxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") and a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") on top and an unowned [chaurus egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") on the floor beside it, while to the right is a chair. Beside the lab, on top of the cupboard is a deathbell flower, a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower and a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"). On the wall shelf is a [giant's toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe"), a [Falmer ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Ear "Skyrim:Falmer Ear"), a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), a bowl of ectoplasm, [potion of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"), a [draught of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Health "Skyrim:Draught of Health"), and a [potion of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina").

The next cubicle is a dining room containing a long wooden table with various foodstuffs on top. There are three loose septims on the floor to the right, by a barrel. The final cubicle is [Faralda's](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda") quarters and contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with sets of shelves on either side holding a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), a medium coin purse, seven loose septims, a basket containing three [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"), three samples of [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss"), two [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), three [hagraven claws](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Claw "Skyrim:Hagraven Claw"), a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), two [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), three pieces of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), a two chaurus eggs, a Falmer ear, and a piece of [creeper cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster"). To the left is a tall wardrobe and a chair, while to the right is a table and chair with a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") on top of the table. There are two wall shelves above the chair and a sweet roll on a barrel by the doorway.

### Upper Floor

There is a hole in the center of the room with the magical energies from below rising into the ceiling. Around this is a low wall to prevent accidental falls. The first cubicle on the left is an unused bedroom containing an unowned single bed coming out from the wall, with several crates, barrels and an unlocked wooden chest around the cubicle. The second cubicle is [Sergius Turrianus'](/wiki/Skyrim:Sergius_Turrianus "Skyrim:Sergius Turrianus") sleeping quarters. It contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with small cupboards on either side. The one on the left has a medium coin purse on top. To the left are two tall wardrobes separated by a chair. To the right is a narrow table with a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), a Falmer ear, a bowl of ectoplasm, a bowl of frost salts, a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a deathbell flower, and a piece of canis root, with a barrel to the right containing ingredients.

The third cubicle contains an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") with an unlocked display cabinet on either side containing soul gems; there are two empty and two filled common, a filled lesser and three filled petty soul gems. Above the cabinets are wall shelves, the one of the left has a row of [skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull") on top, while under the cabinet on this side is another of the three locations you can find Tolfdir's Alembic. You are free to take these soul gems. The next cubicle is a dining room with a long wooden table and bench filled with foodstuffs, on either side are chairs and barrels, on top of one of the barrels to the right of the dining table is the last of the three possible location to find Tolfdir's Alembic.

The next cubicle contains an alchemy lab with sets of shelves on either side and a couple of barrels containing ingredients and a chair to the left and a wooden bench to the right. The shelves hold two bowls of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), two bowls of [spriggan sap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan_Sap "Skyrim:Spriggan Sap"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), two [Nordic barnacles](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") and a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus, a [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota") fungus, three [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), two [purple](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and one [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), a potion of minor magicka, a potion of magicka, a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing"), a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a [paralysis poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Paralysis Poison"), two [swamp fungal pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Swamp_Fungal_Pod "Skyrim:Swamp Fungal Pod"), a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a sample of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), a sample of hagraven feathers, a bowl of bone meal, two dragon's tongue flowers, a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), two bowls of ectoplasm, an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), two rock warbler eggs, and a piece of canis root. Everything in this room is unowned and free to take.

The next cubicle is [Colette Marence's](/wiki/Skyrim:Colette_Marence "Skyrim:Colette Marence") sleeping quarters, it contains an owned single bed coming out from the wall with end tables on either side. The one on the right has six loose septims on top. To the left of the bed are two sets of shelves separated by a tall wardrobe. On the shelves are two [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two apples pies, four [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and two green apples and in front is a lute. To the right of the bed is an unlocked long chest with two wall shelves above it. These hold a [staff of lightning bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Lightning_Bolts "Skyrim:Staff of Lightning Bolts"), a [dragon priest dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Dagger "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Dagger"), and an [Orcish dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"). There is also a drum on the floor. The final cubicle only contains a couple of crates and barrels. It is also the location for finishing the [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor") to assist [Arniel Gane](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel_Gane "Skyrim:Arniel Gane") discover an ancient Dwemer secret.

The stairwell continues to the top and a door out onto the roof of the main walls and access to other areas in the college.

## Bugs

- A number of objects in the NPC's bedrooms in the Hall of Countenance aren't properly marked as owned.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Hall of Rumination

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Dwarven Ruin: Hall of Rumination | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [Falmer Servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BlackreachZcell06 | |
| Region | |
| [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") | |
| Location | |
| Northwestern part of Blackreach's city | |

Hall of Rumination

**Hall of Rumination** is a small [Dwarven ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Ruins "Skyrim:Dwarven Ruins") in [Blackreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackreach "Skyrim:Blackreach") occupied by [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [their servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant"). It is part of the Dwemer city in the western part of Blackreach.

### Exterior

The entire Dwemer city is patrolled by both [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and [their servants](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Servant "Skyrim:Falmer Servant"), who man the walls and wander the grounds. Many of them are near this building and the paths to it; care must be taken to avoid alerting too many at once. A good place from which to snipe them is the raised bridge between the [Pumping Station](/wiki/Skyrim:Pumping_Station "Skyrim:Pumping Station") and the [Debate Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Debate_Hall "Skyrim:Debate Hall"). Once these enemies are dealt with, the Hall of Rumination may be entered in the northwestern part of the city. There is only one ground-level entrance.

### Hall of Rumination

Upon entering, you emerge in a badly damaged room, with rubble everywhere. In the center is a basin with stone chairs arranged around it, two of which are occupied by Falmer servants. There is also a third servant off to the right on a raised section, and a Falmer to the left down a flight of stairs; both will be alerted to any fighting. Opposite the entrance, at the rear of the room in the northwest corner, is a metal gate blocking access to a flight of stairs. This gate is opened by a lever on the raised section to the north. To the south are stairs leading down to a large area including a room under the basin, but this area contains nothing of interest.

To the north are the stairs leading up to the raised section, which features two closed doors in the east wall. The door on the left opens into a room containing two Falmer servants sitting in chairs. In the northwest corner of this room is an unlocked wall [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). The room on the right is a bedroom, and contains two more servants as well as several stone beds, a table, and chairs. Whichever room you enter first, any fighting may alert the servants in the other room. In front of the second bedroom is a stone chair and the lever that opens the gate blocking the stairs in the northwest corner of the room.

Climbing the stairs in the northwest corner of the main room past the gate leads up to a corridor with a closed unlocked metal gate about halfway along it. Past the gate is a Falmer wandering around a T-junction, with a corridor leading to a lift ahead, and another corridor around the corner to the southeast. Taking the second corridor, you will find an unlocked chest on your left next to some piping, and a wall chest up ahead to the southwest where the corridor turns again to the southeast. There are two [garnets](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet") and a [Dwemer cog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog") on the small stone platform under the wall chest. Stairs to the southeast lead up to a door that exits outside, where you will find a tall circular rock pillar in front of you, and balconies extending to the left and right. From here, you can look out over most of the city.

Returning inside the hall to the lift and activating it will take you to a short exterior corridor that heads south before it turns to the east and ends at a door. The enemies beyond the door may detect you if you are not careful. The door opens to a far higher narrow balcony, with two Falmer servants and a leveled Falmer. Ahead is a curved ramp leading down to a large circular platform, with what appears to be a throne on a raised section in the center. Staying on the upper balcony and following it clockwise around the lift tower brings you to a [crimson nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Crimson_Nirnroot "Skyrim:Crimson Nirnroot") growing in a large urn. From the circular platform, you can see much of Blackreach far below you. The large orange globe hanging above the Silent City is slightly below you. Using [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") on the globe allows you to summon [Vulthuryol](/wiki/Skyrim:Vulthuryol "Skyrim:Vulthuryol"). You can also use [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") to safely jump down to the courtyard below.

## Maps

- 

  Hall of Rumination

# Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Falkreath)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |

The Hall of the Dead

The **Hall of the Dead** is both [Falkreath's](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") only temple and home for both [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil"), the priest of Arkay, and [Kust](/wiki/Skyrim:Kust "Skyrim:Kust"), who is responsible for looking after Falkreath's cemetery.

The living quarters are at the northern end of the house, while the southern end is given over for a shrine and for devotions. It is found at the far western end of Falkreath with cemeteries all around.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Kust](/wiki/Skyrim:Kust "Skyrim:Kust")  [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil") [Trainer (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Common)")[Conjuration (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Conjuration (Common)") |

## Related Quests

- **[Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery "Skyrim:Delivery")**: Deliver an item to an associate. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Ill Met By Moonlight](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight")**: Participate in the Daedric Prince [Hircine](/wiki/Skyrim:Hircine "Skyrim:Hircine")'s Great Hunt.

### Exterior

There is a [shrine of Arkay](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Arkay "Skyrim:Shrine of Arkay") on either side of the front porch entrance, as well as two tall posts with banners of Arkay hanging from them. Falkreath has been the site of many battles, helping to feed its massive cemetery. Many of the [Nords](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") see it as a grand honor to be buried there among the ancestors and heroes. The first time you visit Falkreath, as you approach the Hall, you will witness a funeral taking place for the daughter of [Mathies](/wiki/Skyrim:Mathies "Skyrim:Mathies") and his wife [Indara Caerellia](/wiki/Skyrim:Indara_Caerellia "Skyrim:Indara Caerellia"). Asking about will reveal their daughter was brutally murdered. [Runil](/wiki/Skyrim:Runil "Skyrim:Runil"), as the priest to [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay"), will be performing the service, while [Sinding](/wiki/Skyrim:Sinding "Skyrim:Sinding"), the culprit, is in [Falkreath jail](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Jail "Skyrim:Falkreath Jail"). Visiting and speaking to Sinding gives you the option to initiate the related [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Ill_Met_By_Moonlight "Skyrim:Ill Met By Moonlight"). There are several [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") plants and fungi growing among the gravestones around the hall.

| Plants | Mushrooms |
| --- | --- |
| 10 [Nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade")  1 [Red Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") | 4 [Bleeding Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown")  1 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") |

### Hall of the Dead (Falkreath)

.jpg)

The living area

_02.jpg)

The shrine of Arkay

It is a single-room house. In the middle of the south wall there is a shrine of Arkay, with a wooden bench and a couple of chairs in front and a couple of barrels in the corners. Opposite the door is a long wooden table and bench, the table holds a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bucket containing three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). Above the table is a rack with three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from it and three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from the ceiling beside it. To the right of the table is a fireplace with a kettle containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") on the hearth and a round wooden table and two chairs in front of the fire.

This table holds a bottle of alto wine, one of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). Coming out from the north wall are two owned single beds with an end table between them and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing minor loot at the foot of the left-hand one. On the end table is a bottle of Nord mead and a copy of *[Aedra and Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Aedra_and_Daedra "Skyrim:Aedra and Daedra")*. Against the east wall is a wardrobe containing common clothes and having a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace") on top, a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel and a dresser with more clothes in. On the dresser are two more pine thrush eggs, four bulbs of garlic, two bunches of frost mirriam, two bunches of elves ear and a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"), with three garlic braids and a bunch of each frost mirriam and elves ear hanging from the ceiling above the dresser.

## Notes

- A copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Doors of Oblivion](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Doors_of_Oblivion "Skyrim:The Doors of Oblivion")* can be found under the left-hand bed.
- The Hall of the Dead also appears in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Falkreath "Online:Falkreath") and [Legends](/wiki/Legends:Hall_of_the_Dead "Legends:Hall of the Dead").
- Every single instance of data such as the key, location data, and internal references except for the cell name itself, refers to this location under the name "**House of Arkay**" instead.

# Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)

## Overview

.jpg)

City entrance

The **Hall of the Dead** is a large building in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") where the corpses of the deceased are laid to rest.

There are two entrances to Markarth's Hall of the Dead. The first is found near the entrance to the [Hag's Cure](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hag%27s_Cure "Skyrim:The Hag's Cure") and the [Markarth Ruins](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Ruins "Skyrim:Markarth Ruins"). The second is found inside [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), near [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo"). The Hall is home to [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus"), and is the starting point for the quest [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death"). It consists of one zone, *[Hall of the Dead](#Hall_of_the_Dead)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus")  [Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower") \* |

\* Moves to [Reachcliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Cave "Skyrim:Reachcliff Cave") after the related quest.

## Related Quests

- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a [feast](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").

## Hall of the Dead

.jpg)

Hall of the Dead interior

There is very little within the hall. To the west of the shrine is a food barrel, two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two [eidar cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), and a sample of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"). To the east of the shrine is the skill book *[2920, Rain's Hand, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Rain%27s_Hand,_v4 "Skyrim:2920, Rain's Hand, v4")* above an owned bed.

## Notes

- You are required to [pick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") either adept-locked door to enter without the key. The key is given to you by Brother Verulus during the related quest.
- If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") capture Markarth (whether Markarth is taken by force or given to the Stormcloaks during [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending")), [Ondolemar](/wiki/Skyrim:Ondolemar "Skyrim:Ondolemar") will perish, and his remains will be found here.
- There is a secret room in the Hall. It can be seen on the map to the left of the altar of [Arkay](/wiki/Lore:Arkay "Lore:Arkay"), if you stick to the wall.

## Bugs

- Several coffins and other graves in this Hall of the Dead were not initially disabled like they should be, resulting in them all being marked as owned by Brother Verulus.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2b, addresses this issue. Unassigned coffins and urns have been changed to objects that don't display the owner's name.
